|| OM hR^idyapekShayA tu manuShyAdhikAratvAt.h OM || 

atra "vishvedevA upAsate' (kA.2-2-3) ityasya upAsyatvoktyA tajj~nAnAdeva mokShAvashyaMbhAvAt.h "tamAtmasthaM ye.anupashyanti' (kA.2-2-12) ityuktasya viShNuj~nAnAdeva mokSha ityasya AkShepAtsaN^gatiH | kAThake "aN^guShThamAtraH puruSho madhya atmani tiShThati IshAno bhUtabhavyasya' (kA.2-1-12) ityukteshAnaH kiM mukhyavAyuH uta viShNuriti sandehaH | vAyuriti pUrvaH pakShaH | "UrdhvaM prANamunnayati apAnaM pratyagasyati madhye vAmanamAsInaM vishvedevA upAsate' (kA.2-2-3) iti prANAdivyavasthApakatvamadhyamatvasarvadevopAsyatvAnAM shravaNAt.h teShAM cha "evameva eSha prANaH itarAn.h prANAn.h pR^ithakpR^ithageva sannidhatte' iti (ShaT.hpra.3-4) "athemameva nA nodyo.ayaM madhyamaH prANaH' (bR^i.3-6-21) iti vAjasaneye tR^itIye vAjasaneye chaturthe "ayaM vAva shishuH yo.ayaM madhyamaH prANaH' (bR^i.4-2-1) iti shishubrAhmaNe | "kuvidaN^ga namasA' (R^i.7-91-1) ityAdi shrutibhiH vAyudharmatvAvagamAt.h | viShNAvakSharanaye aNutvoktAvapi iha shrutAN^guShThamAtratvAyogAchcha | tasya tato.adhikaparimANarAhityArthatvAt.h | nacha hR^idayApekShayopapattiH | vikalpAsahatvAt.h | yatkiJNchidaN^guShThamitatve nirdhAraNAyogena upAsanAnupapattyA taduktivaiyarthyAt.h | tattadaN^guShyamitatve pashvAdestadabhAvena tadantasthasya tattvAyogAditi | siddhAntastu | vAmanamiti shrutavAmanashruteH "eSha u eva vAmaniH eSha hi sarvANi vAmAni nayati' (ChAM.4-15-3) "upendro vAmanaH prAMshuH' (viShNu.sa.nA.) ityAdishrutismR^itibhiH ekadeshavikR^itaM ananyavadbhavatIti nyAyena vidvatprasiddhayA cha yogarUDhibhyA viShNvekaniShThatvena anyatrAnavakAshAt.h | prANaniyAmakatvasya antaryAminayanyAyena (bra.sU.1-2-18) sarvaniyAmake harau yuktatvAt.h | "yaddevAn.h prANayo nava' (tai.A.3-14) iti vishiShya cha shrutyantare vaiShNavatvokteH madhya iti madhyashabdodhvarshabdasAhacharyeNa madhyadeshavAchitayA madhyamoktyabhAvena madhyadeshe.avasthAnasya viShNAvapi yogAt.h | sarvadevopAsyatvasyApi sarvajimAsyatvaparyAyatayA tasya daharanaye siddhatvAt.h | evaM sAvakAshatayA svatashcha durbalAnAM svato niravakAshatayA balavatyA shrutyA bAdhAt.h aN^guShThamAtratvasya cha tattadaN^guShThamitarUpavisheShasya vyaktyAtmanA aN^guShThamAtratvAdvA 
tAdR^ishasthAnahR^idayagatasya tatrasthAnini Ishe upachArAdvA yuktatvAt.h prANyantarasyAN^guShThabhAve.api shAstrasya manuShyAdhikAritvenAdoShAta ayamIshAno viShNureveti | phalaM tu upAsyatvamukhena jij~nAsAsUtrAkShepaH tatsamAdhishcha || 7 || 

|| OM taduparyapi bAdarAyaNaH sambhavAt.h OM || 8 || 

|| OM virodhaH karmaNIti chennAnekapratipatterdasharnAt.h OM || OM shabda iti chennAtaH prabhavAtpratyakShAnumAnAbhyAm.h OM || OM ata eva cha nityatvam.h OM || OM samAnanAmarUpatvAchchAvR^ittAvapyavirodho darshananAtsmR^iteshcha OM || OM madhvAdiShvanadhikAraM jaiminiH OM || OM jyotiShi bhAvAchcha OM || OM bhAvaM tu bAdarAyaNo.asti hi OM || 

pUrvatra manuShyAdhikAratvAdityuktiH tiryagAdyapekShayaiva devAdInAM tu adhikAro.astyeva ityatrochyata iti saN^gatiH | "vishvedevA upAsate' ityupAsakatvena shrutadevAnAM upAsanAdau adhikAro.asti na veti sandehaH | nAstIti pUrvaH pakShaH | tattatpadavishiShyAnAM devAnAM utpattivinAshavatve indrAdipadaprApteH pUrvaM pashchachcha indrAdidevAnAmabhAvena taduddeshena dravyatyAgAtmakayAgAdirUpakarmavirodhasya tattaddevatAbodhakAnAdinityavedAprAmANyasya cha ApAtAt.h | pUrvaM pashchAt.h indrAntarasvIkAreNa teShAM pravAhato.anAdinityatvAN^gIkAre.api ekanAmarUpatve mAnAbhAvena nAnAnAmarUpavattvAt.h ekarUpAtharbodhakavedAprAmANyAnivAraNAchcha | anAdinityatve.avashyaM svIkArye tAdR^ishAnAM tatphale mokShe.arthitAbhAvAt.h | kiJNcha vasutvAdiphalakamadhuvidyAdiShu vasvAdInAmadhikArAyogena sarvavidyAsu anadhikArAt.h mokShaphalakasvapi "naiva daivapadaM prAptAH brahmadarshanavarjitAH' ityAdeH teShAM siddhaj~nAnatayA mokShahetuj~nAnArthaM adhikArAyogAditi | siddhAntastu | devAnAmapi vishiShyabuddhayAdimatvAt.h shUdravat.h aparyudastatvAt.h Adyantatatve mokShe.athitvasyApi sambhavAt.h teShAM utpattivinAshavatve.api "te ha nAkaM mahimAnaH sachanta yatra pUrve sAdhyAssanti devAH' "dhAtA yathA pUrvamakalpayat.h' (puruSha.sU.) "yathaiva niyamaH kAle surAdi niyamastathA' ityAdivachanaiH pramANabhUtavedasya anAdinityatvAnyathAnupapattyA cha pravAhato.anAdinityatvAt.h teShAM cha yathApUrvamiti shrutyA anAdinidhanetyAdi smR^ityA samAnanAmarUpatvena vedaprAmANyAnApatteH | madhuvidyAdeH vasutvAdiphalakatve.api vasvAdInAM j~nAne mokShe cha atishayAtharM tatra arthitvasambhavAt.h asti brahmavidyAyAM adhikAra iti | phalaM tu vishvedevA upAsata ityAdeH pUrvoktasyAprAmANyaM tatsamAdhishcha |

|| OM shugasya tadanAdarashravaNAttadAdravaNAtsUchyate hi OM || 9 ||

|| OM kShatriyatvAvagateshchottaratra chaitrarathena liN^gAt.h OM || OM saMskAraparAmarshAttadabhAvAbhilApAchcha OM || OM tadabhAvanirdhAraNe cha pravR^itteH OM || OM shravaNAdhyayanArthapratiShedhAtsmR^iteshcha OM || 

atra pUrvasiddhAntanyAyena pUrvapakShapravR^itteH ApavAdikI saN^gatiH | shUdrAdeH brahmavidyAyAmadhikAraH asti uta neti sandehaH | vishiShyabuddhayAdimatvAt.h devAdivat.h shUdrasyApi asti vedavidyAyAmadhikAraH iti pUrvaH pakShaH | nacha "upanayIta tamadhyApayIta' ityupanItasyaiva adhyayanavidhAnAt.h shUdrasya cha anupanItatayA adhyayanahInatvAt.h tadvata eva "adhyayanamAtravataH' (bra.sU.3-4-12) iti tR^itIye pautrAyaNaM prati "aha hAre tvA shUdra' (ChAM.4-2-3) varNAvare rUDha shUdrapadena raikvasya sambodhanena vidurAdeH vedArthAvadhAraNAdirUpeNa cha liN^gena, shUdre.api upanayanAdhyayanayorvA, anupanItasyaivAdhyayanamiti vA, anadhIyAnasya likhitanirIkShaNAdinaiva vA, arthaj~nAnasya kalpanAditi | siddhAntastu | "ayamashvatarIrathaH' iti vAkyasheShoktarathavattvasya "yatra vedo rathastatra na vedo yatra no rathaH' (brahmavaivarta.pu.) iti smR^ityA rathasya vedavyAptatvena shUdre tadabhAvena abhAvAt.h kShatriye tasya svAbhAvikatvAchcha | tena pautrAyaNasya kShatriyatvAvagamena bAdhakena shUdrashabdasya rUDhArthasya tyAjyatayA haMsakR^itAnAdareNa jAtashokena muniM prati AdravaNasya vAkyasheShe shravaNena shuchA dravaNarUpayogena upapattyA shUdrAdhikArAsAdhakatvAt.h nAsti shUdrasyAdhikAraH | adhyayanasya upanayanasApekShatvAt.h shUdrasya cha "nAgnirna yaj~no na vratAni cha shUdrasya' (paiN^gi.shru) iti shrutyA upanayanasaMskArAbhAvAchcha | "tadabrAhmaNAre vivaktumarhati' (ChAM.4-5-5) iti satyakAmasya ashUdratvaM nirdhAryaiva tadupanayane 
gautamasya pravR^ittatvena tadrUpAliN^gAt.h | "shravaNe trapujatubhyAM shrotraparipUraNaM adhyayane jihvAchChedaH arthAvadhAraNe hR^idayavidAraNam.h' (gautamadharmasUtra) iti shUdrasya vedashravaNAderniShiddhatayA vishiShyabuddhayAdimatve sati aniShiddhatvarUpasya adhikAraprayojakasyAbhAvAt.h | likhitanirIkShaNenApi arthAvadhAraNAyogAt.h | vidurAderjanmAntarotpannaj~nAnatvena itarashUdravailakShaNyAchcha nAsti shUdre vedavidyAdhikAra iti | phalaM tu shUdrasya devAdivat.h vishiShyabuddhayAdinyAyena adhikAre sati tanniShedhakashrutyAdivirodhaprAptyA manuShyAdhikAritvaM shAstrasya sAmAnyataH uktaM tatpramANaviruddhamiti pUrvapakShe siddhAnte sAmAnyokteH shUdretaraviShayatvAnna virodhaH | 

|| OM kammanAt.h OM || 10 ||

atra vajrashabdasya pUrvatra shUdrashabdasyeva vAkyasheShe klR^iptayogAbhAvAt.h yogavR^ittyA na viShNuvAchitvamiti shaN^kanAtpratyudAharaNasaN^gatiH | "yadidaM kiJNcha jagatsarvaM prANa ejati niHsR^itam.h | mahadbhayaM vajramudyataM ya etadviduH amR^itAste bhavanti |' (kA.2-3-2) iti kAThake shruto vajraH kiM indrAyudhaM uta viShNuriti sandehaH | indrAyudhamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | vajrashabdasya tatra rUDhatvAt.h | vAkyasheShe pUrvatreva viShNau klR^iptayogAbhAvAt.h "varjanAdvajram.h' (bra.vai.pu.) iti smR^iteshcha vajrashrutitaH durbalatvAt.h | klR^iptarUDhityAgena yaugikatayA viShNugrahaNe cha arthAntare.api yogasya suvachatvena shabdArthAvyavasthAprasaN^gAchcha udyatatvaliN^gAchcha tasya cha "udyatAyudhadordaNDAH' (mahAbhArata) ityAdi smR^itau "tenendro vajramudayachChat.h' iti shrutau cha Ayudhe prasiddhatvAt.h shrutiliN^gAbhyAM cha muktihetuvedanatvAdi brahmaliN^gAnAM bAdhAditi | siddhAntastu | "jagatsarvaM prANa ejati' prANanimittaM kampate iti shrutasarvacheShyakatvasya "ko hyevAnyAtkaH prANyAt.h (tai.2-7) ityAdi shrutismR^itibhiH viShNoranyatrAnavakAshAt.h | vajrashruteshcha shrutyupabR^iMhakasmR^ityuktena niravakAshayogena "AyudhAnAmahaM vajram.h' (bha.gI.10-18) iti prayogAchcha viShNau sAvakAshatvAt.h | yogasya smartAtvAdeva avyavasthAnApatteH | udyatatvaliN^gasya cha utpUrvasya yate rUpatayA utkR^iShyaprayatnavatvarUpatayA viShNAvapi sambhavAt.h idaM vajraM viShNureveti | phalaM tu viShNoH muktihetuvedanatvAkShepaH tatsamAdhishcha || 10 ||

|| OM jyotirdarshanAt.h OM || 11 ||

atra pUrvatreva niravakAshaliN^gAt.h jyotiHshabdasya "viShNureva jyotiH' iti shrutiprasiddhArthatyAgena pUrvapakShapravR^itteH ApavAdikI saN^gatiH | kANvashrutau ShaShThe.adhyAye "yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu hR^idyantarjyotiH' (bR^i.6-3-7) iti shrutaM jyotiH kiM jIvaH uta brahmeti sandehaH | jIva iti pUrvaH pakShaH | "sa samAnassan.h ubhau lokAvanusaJNcharati' (bR^i.6-3-7) "savA.ayaM puruSho jAyamAnaH sharIramabhisampadyamAnaH pApmabhiH saMsR^ijyate | sa utkrAmat.h mriyamANaH pApmano vijahAti' (bR^i.6-3-8) iti karmAyattalokasaJNcharaNAdi jIvaliN^gabAhulyAt.h | kiMcha "kiM jyotirayaM puruShaH' (bR^i.6-3-2) iti prashne "Adityenaiva jyotiShA.a.aste' ityAdinA AdityachandrAgnivAgAtmasu pUrvapUrvAstamaye uttarottarasya j~nAnahetutvarUpajyotiShTvamuktvA "katama AtmA' (bR^i.6-3-7) iti prashne yo.ayamityasyoktatvAt.h AdityAdijyotiShTvenoktasya cha na tatra sUryo bhAtItyAdeH viShNutvAyogena jIvatvAvashyaM bhAvAchcha | Atmashabdena paramAtmagrahaNe sati astamayAdihInAtmajyotiShTvasya jIve sArvakAlikatvena Adityernaiva jyotiShetyAdau avadhAraNAyogAditi | siddhAntastu | "viShNureva jyotiH viShNureva brahma' (chaturvedashikhA) iti shrutyA jyotiHshabdasya viShNvekavAchitvAttasya hR^idyantarjyotiriti upakrame "atrAyaM puruShaH svayaM jyotiH' (bR^i.6-3-9) iti upasaMhAre cha shrutatvena tAbhyAM viShNuparatvena nirNItavAkyamadhyapatitatvena jIvaliN^gAnAM antarNItaNyarthakatvakalpanayA harau sAvakAshatvAt.h lokadvayasaJNchArasya jIvamAdAya Ishasyaiva svAtanteNopapaveH Atmashabditeshasya jyotiShTve.api jIvasya bAhyajyotiprAdhAnyaj~nApanAya AdityenaivetyavadhAraNopapatteH viShrurevedaM jyotiriti | phalaM tu hR^idayAhitatvamukhena jyotishcharaNeti sUtrAkShepaH samAdhishcheti || 11 || N.M-3 
|| OM AkAshaH arthAntaratvAdivyapadeshAt.h OM || 12 || 

atra "bahiH kulAyAdamR^itashcharitvA' (bR^i.6-3-12) iti pUrvajyotiShi shrutAmR^itatvasya ihAkAshe "tadamR^itam.h' iti shravaNAt.h tasya 
cha anyatvAt.h pUrvoktamapi AdityAkShepAt.h AkShepikI saN^gatiH | ChAndogye "AkAsho vai nAmarUpayornirvahitA te yadantarA tadbrahma tadamR^itam.h' (ChAM.8-14-1) ityantimakhaNDe shrutAkAshaH kiM prasiddhAvyAkR^itAkAshaH kiM vA brahmeti sandehaH | pUrvapakShastu vai nAmeti nipAtadvayasya prasiddhArthatvAt.h tasya cha "akAsho vai nAma' prasiddhaH khalvAkAshaH "nAmarUpayornirvahitA' iti uddeshAnvaye AkAsho nAmarUpayornirvahitA vai nAma tasya nAmarUpanirvahitR^itvaM prasiddhamiti vidheyAnvaye vA dvedhApi svarUpeNa nAmarUpAvakAshadAnAt.h tannirvAhakatayA cha loke avakAsha eva prasiddheH Ishe aprasiddheH avakAsha eva ayamAkAsha iti | siddhAntastu | "te yadantarA' iti vAkye te nAmarUpe vinA yadastItyuktasya kArtsyena shabdagocharatvAdirUpanAmatvasya tathA nirvAhyatayA prakR^itaprAkR^itarUpaparAhityasya cha liN^gasya "yato vAcho nivartante' (tai.2-4) "arUpamasparsham.h' (kA.3.15) ityAdishrutibhiH "anAmA so.aprasiddhatvAt.h arUpo bhUtavarjanAt.h' (brAhma.pu.) ityAdismR^ityA cha viShNvekadharmatvAt.h tadbrahmetyuktabrahmabrahmashabdAt.h tadamR^itamityukatAmR^itatvaliN^gAchcha sAdhakasattvAt.h prasiddhArthakanipAtadvayasya cha "AkAsha iti hovAcha' (ChAM.1-9-1) iti shrutau svarUpeNa "eko dAdhAra bhuvanAni vishva' ityAdishrutau (R^i.saM.1-154-4) nAmarUpanirvahitR^itvena cha viShNau prasiddhatvAt.h vedaprasiddheH antaraN^gatayA vede grAhyatvenAbAdhakatvAt.h ayamAkAsho viShNureveti | phalaM tu nAmarUpanirvoDhutvatvAkhyasarvAdhAratvamukhena dyubhvAdinayAkShepaH tatsamAdhishcha | talliN^gAdityatra anavakAshaliN^gena lokarUDhityAgoktAvapIha vai nAmetyAbhyAM visheShAshaN^kayA punarArambhaH || 12 || 

|| OM suShuptyutkrAntyorbhedena OM || 13 ||

atra prAgAkAshashabdasya shrautaprasiddhayA Ishe sambhave.api iha tadabhAvAt.h sva nadraShyR^itvaM yuktamiti vA AkAshasya jaDatvena tatra IshaliN^gasya IshabhedenAyoge.api iha jIvasya Ishabhedena talliN^gaM netuM shakyate iti vA pUrvavaiShamyeNa shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | kANvashrutau aShyame.adhyAye "sa vA eSha etasmin.h samprasAde ratvA charitvA dR^iShTvaiva puNyaM cha pApaM cha punaH pratinyAyaM pratiyonyA dravati sva nAyaiva sa yattatra kiJNchitpashyati ananvAgatastena bhavatyasaN^go hyayaM puruShaH' (bR^i.6-3-15) iti shrutasva nAdidraShyA kiM jIvaH atha Isha iti sandehaH | shrutasva nAdi draShyR^itvasya loke jIva eva prasiddhatvAt.h jIva iti pUrvaH pakShaH | shrautaprasiddhayabhAve lokaprasiddherapi vede grAhyatvAt.h IshasyAsharIratvena sva nAdidraShyR^itvAyogAchcha asaN^gatvarUpabrahmaliN^gasya IshAbhedena jIvachaitanye.api yuktatvAt.h | jIvadharmasya tu sva nAdidraShyR^itvasya shuddhe brahmachaitanye ayogAt.h | jij~nAsAsUtre jIveshabhedasyoktatayA tadabhedAbhiprAye taddhamarsyeshe siddhAntinA vaktumashakyatvAchcheti | siddhAntastu | asaN^go hyayamiti shrutAsaN^gatvasya asaN^gamasparshamityAdinA IshaikadhamartvAt.h sva nAdipadArthAnAM "sandhye sR^iShyirAha hi' (bra.sU.3-1-1) iti vakShyamANanyAyena satyatvena "yassarvaj~naH' (Atha.1-9) ityAdishrutyA Ishasya sarvaj~natayA cha kArtsyena sva nAdidraShyR^itvasya Ishe mukhyataH sambhavAt.h | "prAj~nenAtmanA sampariShvaktaH' (bR^i.6-3-21) "prAj~nenAtmanA anvArUDhaH' (bR^i.6-3-35) iti suShuptyutkrAntiprakaraNayoH bhedoktyA jIveshAbhedAshravaNAyogAt.h | "svApyayasampattyoH' (bra.sU.4-4-16) ityatra suShuptiprakaraNasya muktiparasyApyuktyA bhedasya muktigatvena satyatvAchcha sva nAdidraShyA viShNureveti akSharanayokta asaN^gatvAkShepaH tatsamAdhishcha || 13 ||

|| OM patyAdishabdebhyaH OM || 14 ||

atra "asaN^go na hi saJNjate' (bR^i.6-4-22) ityuktasyAsaN^gasya IshAnyatve prAktanaH sa eveti shaN^kanAt.h AkShepikI saN^gatiH | kANvashrutau ShaShThe.adhyAye "eSha nityo mahimA brAhmaNasya' (bR^i.6-4-22) iti shrutaH brAhmaNaH kiM viriJNchaH kiM vA Isha iti sandehaH | viriJNcha evAyaM brAhmaNa iti pUrvaH pakShaH | "sa vA eSha mahAnaja AtmA' (bR^i.6-4-22) ityajashabdAt.h tasya cha akAravAchyeshajAtatvena yogena rUDhyA cha viriJNche sambhavAt.h Ishena jAyata iti yogena "tasmAdahamajaH smR^itaH' iti bhAratoktyA rUDhyA cha sambhave.api varNahIne viShNAvanavakAshena vipratvajAtau nirUDhabrAhmaNashabdasAhityena asya viriJNchaikaprApakatvAt.h mahachChabdasyApi abhimAninayanyAyena mahattatvAbhimAnini viriJNcha eva yuktatvAt.h Atmashruterapi "AtmAviriJNchaH sumanAH' ityukteH "buddherAtmA mahAn.h paraH' iti prayogAt.h viriJNche rUDhatvAt.h | sarvavashItyAdinokta brahmaliN^gAnAM tu ubhayabAdhena viriJNcheshAbhedena pUrvapUrvapakShavadupapatteH | "sthityAdaye hariviriJNchahareti saMj~nAH' (bhAga.1-2-23) ityAdeH abhedenaikavAkyatvopapattau 
vAkyabhedenobhayaparatvakalpanAyogAchcha | siddhAntastu | "sarvasya vashI sarvasyeshAnaH sarvasyAdhipatiH' ityAdinoktasarvavashitvAdiliN^gAnAM "utAmR^itatvasyeshAnaH' (puruSha.sU.) "saptArdhagarbhA' (R^i.1-164-36) ityAdishrutibhyo vaiShNavatvAt.h | brAhmaNashabdasya brahmaNA vedena aNyate gamyate iti yogena sAvakAshatvAt.h ajashruteH tathaiva sAvakAshatvAt.h ubhayabAdhena abhedAN^gIkArasya atiprasaJNjakatayA "tata ete vyajAyanta vishvo hiraNyagarbhaH' ityAdivachanabAdhitatayA cha ayogAt.h | smR^iteH tattadantargateshvararUpApekShayA upapatteH ayaM brAhmaNo viShNureveti | phalaM tu jij~nAsAdisUtreShu viShNoH vivakShitaM nityamahimatvamayuktaM ityAkShepaH tatsamAdhishcheti || 14 || 

|| iti shrIrAghavendrayatikR^itAyAM nyAyamuktAvalyAM Adye.adhyAye tR^itIyaH pAdaH samAptaH || 

|| atha chaturthaH pAdaH |

evaM tripAdyAM kAraNatvatatsaN^gatAnandamayatvAdiguNAntarabodhakavAkyasthashabdasamanvaye.abhihite atra brahmapadoktaguNapUrtisiddhaye avasaraprAptAnAM anyatraiva prasiddhanAmaliN^gAtmakashabdAnAM samanvaya uchyate | 

|| OM AnumAnikamapyekeShAmiti chenna sharIrarUpakavinyastagR^ihIterdarshayati cha OM || 1 ||

|| OM sUkShmaM tu tadarhatvAt.h OM || OM tadadhInatvAdarthavat.h OM || OM j~neyatvAvachanAchcha OM || OM vadatIti chenna prAj~no hi OM || OM prakaraNAt.h OM || OM trayANAmeva chaivamupanyAsaH prashnashcha OM || OM mahadvachcha OM || OM chamasavadavisheShAt.h OM || 

atra avyaktAdiparAvadhitvavaratvAdivAchishabdavAchyatve prAk.h hetUkR^itasarveshvaratvAdivirodha ityAshaN^kanAt.h pUrvasaN^gatiH dhyeyA | "mahataH paramavyaktaM avyaktAtpuruShaH paraH' (kA.1-3-11) "jIvA eva tu duHkhinaH' "yonimanye prapadyante' (kA.2-2-7) "kAryakAraNabaddhau tau' (mAM.2-11) itayAdau shrutAvyaktaduHkhibaddhAvarAdishabdamukhyArthaH kiM prakR^ita jIvAdiH uta IshaH iti sandehaH | pUrvapakShastu | prakR^ityAdireva na brahma avyaktAdishabdAnAM tatraiva prasiddheH viShNuvAchitve mAnAbhAvAt.h teShAM pradhAnAdyavAchakatve.api tatra vyavahAre avisheSheNa sarvashabdAnAM sarvatra vyavahArApAtena avyavasthAprasaN^gAchcha | avyakte paJNchamyuktena parAvadhitvenAkShiptAvaratvasya jIve j~nAnaduHkhitvAdeshcha "na tvatsamashchAbhyadhikashcha dR^ishyate' (bha.gI.11-43) "niraniShTho niravadyaH' ityAdipramANavirodhena prAguktasarvAdhipatitvAdivirodhena cha viShNAvayogAchcha | "mahAntaM cha samAvR^itya pradhAnaM samavasthitam.h' ityAdeH pradhAnadharmatvena nirNItamahatparatvaliN^gasya avyakte shravaNAchcheti | siddhAntastu | "nAmAni sarvANi yamAvishanti' (bhAllaveyashrutiH) ityAdishrutyA viShNoH avyaktAdisarvashabdavAchyatvAt.h "avyaktamachalaM shAntam.h' (pippa.shru.) "anena jIvenAtmanA' (ChAM.6-11-1) ityAdi shrautasmArtaprayogAt.h | sUkShmatvenAvyaktatvasya prANAdhArakatvAdeshcha avyaktAdipadapravR^ittinimittasya "yattatsUkShmaM paramaM veditavyam.h' (pippa.shru.) ityAdinA Ishe mukhyatvena teShAM tatra mukhyatvAt.h | mahachchamasashabdayoH mahattatvayaj~napAtrayoH prasiddhatve.api "mahAntaM vibhumAtmAnam.h' (kA.1-2-22) "idaM tachChiraH eSha hyarvAgbilashchamasaH' (bR^i.4-2-3) ityAdau pravR^ittinimittamukhyatvAdinA viShNushirasaH mukhyatvamiva avyaktAdishabdAnAM anyatra prasiddhatve.api Ishe mukhyatvenopapatteH | "tamevaikaM jAnatha AtmAnaM anyAvAchovimuJNchatha' iti (Atha.2-2-5) Ishasyaiva mumukShuj~neyatvavachanena anyasya tadavachanena Ishaj~nAna eva vedasya pravR^ittatvAt.h avaratvaduHkhAdeH Ishe.ayoge.api anyagatasya IshAdhInatvena svAtanteNa nimittena Ishe parAvadhitvavAchipaJNchamyantapadaduHkhyAdipadavAchyatvopapatteH | sarvasmAtpare mahatparatvasyApi sambhavAchcha avyaktAdishabdamukhyArtho harireveti | phalaM tu samanvayasUtroktasarvashabdasamanvayAkShepaH tatsamAdhishcha || 1 ||

|| OM jyotirupakramAttu tathAhyadhIyata eke OM || 2 || 

|| OM kalpanopadeshAchcha madhvAdivadavirodhaH OM || 

pUrvatra siddharUpadevatAtatkramavAchinAM indriyebhya ityAdInAM samanvaya uktaH | atra tu sAdhyarUpakamartatkramavAchinAM sa uchyata iti pUrvasaN^gatiH | "vasante vasante jyetiShA' iti vAkye shrutajyotirAdishabdAH kiM viShNuvAchinaH kiM vA tadanyakarmAdivAchina iti sandehaH | karmAdivAchina iti pUrvaH pakShaH | teShAM jyotiShyomAdikarmAdiShveva prasiddheH | prasiddhityAgena brahmavAchitve cha anyasya karmatadaN^gakramadevatA kAlAdhikAryAdiprApakasyAbhAvena niyatakarmAnuShThAnalopaH syAt.h | jyotiH padavAchyeshasambandhAt.h karmAdAvapi teShAM pUrvatreva vR^ittirityasyApi IshAdanyatra lakShaNAprasaN^genAyegAt.h | kiM cheshe teShAM rUDherabhAvena guNapUrtyAbhAvapAtena cha yogasyaiva vAchyatvena tato.api karmaNi rUDhebarlavatvAt.h | sarvashabdavAchyatvasiddhayarthaM jyotirAdipadAvayavAnAmapi brahmaparatve samudAyasya tatparatvAyogena yogasyAsambhavAchcheti | siddhAntastu | "taM yachChataM varShANyabhyArchat.h' "tasmAchChatarchinastasmAchChatarchina ityAchakShate etameva santam.h' (ai.2-2-1) ityAdinA upalakShaNatvena keShAJNchichChatarchyAdishabdAnAM mahAyogavidvadrUDhibhyAM viShNuparatvamuktvA ante "tAvA etAssarvA R^ichaH sarve vedAH sarve ghoShAH ekaiva vyAhR^itiH prANa eva' (ai.2-2-2) iti viShNau sarvashabdamukhyArthatvokteH madhvAdishabdasya kShaudrakAdau rUDhimanatihAya tadabAdhena "asau vAdityo deva madhuH' (ChAM.3-1-1) ityAdau mahAyogavR^ittyA upAsanAtharM madhvAdishabdArthasyoktivat.h jyotirAdipadAnAM anyatrarUDhivR^ittimabAdhitvaiva mahAyogAdivR^ittyA IshaparatvAN^gIkAreNa kamarAdyasiddhayabhAvAt.h | tadavayavAnAmanyavAchitvamupetyaiva samudAyasya Ishaparatvopagamena jAtamotaM jagadyasmAjjyotirityAdyuktayogasambhavAt.h jyotirAdishabdamukhyArtho harireveti phalaM tu pUrvavadeva || 2 ||

|| OM na saN^khayopasaN^grahAdapi nAnAbhAvAdatirekAchcha OM || 3 || 

|| OM prANAdayo vAkyasheShAt.h OM || OM jyotiShaikeShAmasatyanne OM || 

pUrvatra prasiddhasya jyotirAdishabdanimittasyAbhAve.api yogalabhyaM aprasiddhaM tadastItyuktam.h | iha tu paJNchajanAdishabdAnAM prasiddhameva tadIshe.astItyuchyata iti saN^gatiH | kANvashrutau ShaShThe.adhyAye "taddevA jyotiShAM jyotirAyuhopAsate.amR^itam.h | yasminpaJNchapaJNchajanAH AkAshashcha pratiShThitaH | tameva manya AtmAnaM vidvAn.h brahmAmR^ito.amR^itam.h' (bR^i.6-416,17) iti shrutapaJNchatvayuktaH janAdishabdamukhyArthaH kiM vAkyasheShe ShaShThayantena prANa chakShuHshrotramanovAchAdi shabdenoktA kiM vA dvitIyAnta tattachChabdanirdiShyaShashasvarUpANIti sandehaH viShNvanye prANAdaya eva paJNchajanAdishabdArtha iti pUrvaH pakShaH | tasya bahutvavishiShyArthavAchitvAt.h | tasya chaikamevAdvitIyamityuktivirodhena Ishe.ayogAt.h | vashIkR^itabahujane.api rAjani bahutvavAchishabdAdarshanena tadadhInatvanyAyasyApi atra anavatArAt.h | guhAmityatra guhAniviShyatvAdibAdhakena ekasyAnekatvaM netyutsargabAdhe.api iha bAdhakAbhAvena tannyAyasyApyanavakAshAt.h | tamevAtmAnamityAtmapadasAmAnAdhikaraNyAt.h | yasminnityasya brahmatvena tadAshritAnAM paJNchAnAM janAnAM AkAshasya brahmatve ekasyAdhArAdheyebhAvAnupapatteshcheti | siddhAntastu | "prANasya prANaM chakShuShashchakShuH shrotrasya shrotraM annasyAnnaM manaso manaH' iti vAkyasheShe dvitIyAntatayA shrutAnAM prANAdiniyantR^itvAdiviShNuliN^gasya shravaNena viShNurUpatvAt.h teShAM cha ShaShyayantanirdiShyaprANAdyapekShayA shabdato.arthatashcha prAdhAnyAt.h | "nAmAni sarvANi' "tAvA etAH' ityAdyuktasarvashabdavAchyatvamumukShuj~neyatvAdiprAguktahetubhyashcha ekasyApi bahurUpatvena paJNchatvasaN^khayAyAH bhedapratinidhivisheShabalena yasminniti nirdiShyasharIrasvarUpasya paJNchajanAdishabditarUpANAM cha AdhArAdheyabhAvasyApi sambhavAt.h | mAdhyandinashAkhAyAmiva kANvashrutau vAkyasheShe annAkhyarUpasyAshravaNe.api pUrvashrutajyotiShA saha paJNchatvAt.h vAkyasheShesthadvitIyAntaprANAdishabditesharUpavisheShA eva paJNchajanA iti | atra pAde sarvatra pUrvavadeva phalam.h || 3 ||

|| OM kAraNatvena cha AkAshAdiShu yathA vyapadiShyokteH OM || 4 ||

atra kAlassadAsItyAdau darshanAdekasyAdhArAdheyabhAva sambhave.api kAryakAraNabhAvasya kvApyadarshanAdayuktaH iti 
pUrvavaiShamyashaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | taittirIye brahmavalyAM "Atmana AkAshassambhUtaH AkAshAdvAyuH' (tai.2-3) ityAdi vAkye kAryatvena kAraNatvena shrutAkAshAdishabdAH kiM mukhyato viShNuvAchakA uta bhUtAdivAchakA iti sandehaH | pUrvapakShastu | "na jAyate mriyate (kA.1-1-17) ityAdeH akArye brahmaNi kAryatvavirodhena svakAryatvasya sutarAM viruddhatvAt.h vyaN^gayavyaJNjakabhAvarUpasyApi kAryakAraNabhAvasya ekasmin.h virodhAt.h | sutajaneH janakAdhInatve.api tatra jAtapadAdarshanena tadadhInanyAyasyApi annAnavatArAt.h | nAmAni sarvANIti shruterapi saN^kochAvashye bhAvAt.h AkAshAdijanmAsiddhayApAtAchcha AkAshAdishabdAH anyavAchakA eveti | siddhAntastu | viShNorevAkAshAdiniyAmakarUpANAM "ya AkAshe tiShThan.h' (bR^i.5-7-12) ityAdi shrutyA AkAshAdisthAnAM bahutvena vyaktyavyaktyapekShayA paurvAparyayogena vAyvAdyutpattau tatstharUpasya vyaktyeva, vyaN^gayavyaJNjakabhAvarUpakAryakAraNabhAvasya sambhavAt.h | bAdhakAbhAvena nAmAnItyAdi shruteH saN^kochAyogena prAguktasAdhakAnAM sattvAt.h | jyotirnayoktarItyA anyatra rUDherabhyupagatatvena AkAshAdyutpatyasiddhayabhAvAchcha AkAshAdishabdamukhyArtho harireveti || 4 ||

|| OM samAkarShAt.h OM || 5 ||

|| OM jagadvAchitvAt.h OM || OM jIvamukhyaprANaliN^gAditi chettadvayAkhyAtam.h OM || OM anyArthaM tu jaiminiH prashnavyAkhyAnAbhyAmapi chaivameke OM || OM vAkyAnvayAt.h OM || OM pratij~nAsiddherliN^gamAshmarathyaH OM || OM utkramiShyata evaM bhAvAdityauDulomiH OM || OM avasthiteritikAshakR^itsnaH OM || 

atra AkAshAdishabdAnAM anyatrApi rUDhyaN^gIkR^itau Ishe tadanyatra cha akShAdishabdavattulyA mukhyavR^ittiH syAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | sarvashabdAnAM Ishe tadanyatra cha uktA mukhyatA kiM tulyA kiM vA Ishe adhikA anyatra tu hIneti sandehaH | pUrvapakShastu | akShAdishabdAnAM anekArthavAchinAM anekatreva sarvashabdAnAmIshe tadanyatra cha mukhyatvaM tulyameva syAt.h | anyathA anyatra hInatve lakShaNetyasyaiva mukhyavR^ittiriti paribhAShA syAt.h | Ishe mukhyatvasyAdhikye tatraiva prasiddhayApAtena jagati prasiddhirna syAt.h | Ishaj~nAnAdeva puruShAtharsiddhayA karmadevatAdau shabdAnAM hInavR^ityA vyavahArasya phalAntarAnichChuM mumukShuM prati vyarthatvApAtAchcha kiJNcha shabdavR^ittihetoH IshagatatvApekShayA tatrAdhikyamiti na yuktam.h | anyatrApi sattvAt.h | nApi tadadhInatvanyAyena "asya yadekAM shAkhAM jIvo jahAtyatha sA shuShyati' (ChAM.6-11-2) iti kvachijjIvAdhInatvasya "vAyunA hi sarve lokA nenIyante' iti sarvasya vAyvadhInatvapratItyA tayorapi IshavanmukhyavAchyatvApAtAditi | siddhAntastu | brahmaNi anyato.adhikaiva shabdAnAM mukhyatA anyatra hInaiva rUDhiyogayoriva gauNalakShaNayoriva Ishe anyatra cha rUDhisattve.api vidvadavidvadrUDhibhyAM yaugikatve.api yogamahAyogAbhyAM tAratamyasambhavena mahAyogavidvadrUDhibhyAM paramamukhyavR^ittyA viShNuniShThAnAmeva teShAM anyatra tataH samAkR^iShya mukhyavR^ittyA vyavahArAt.h | bAlAnAM chitralikhitasiMhAdAviva lokAnAmanyatraiva shabdavyavahAreNa anyatraprasiddhayupapatteH | karmadevatAdhAratvAdinA Ishaj~nAnArthameva karmAdau vedavyavahArasya sambhavAt.h | jIvAdau shrutasvAtantyasya cha tadantaryAmigatatvena pAdAntyaprANanaye siddhatvAditi | phalaM tu viShNureva sarvashabdamukhyArthaH iti samanvayasUtroktAvadhAraNAkShepaH tatsamAdhishcheti || 5 ||

|| OM prakR^itishcha pratij~nAdR^iShyAntAnuparodhAt.h OM || 6 || 

|| OM abhidhyopadeshAchcha OM || OM sAkShAchchobhayA nAnAt.h OM || OM AtmakR^iteH pariNAmAt.h OM || OM yonishcha hi gIyate OM || 

atra sarvashabdAnAM viShNAvadhikA vR^ittiH anyatra hIneti prAguktamayuktaM strIliN^gashabdAnAM mukhyavR^itterevAyogAt.h kutaH Adhikyachinteti shaN^kanAt.h saN^gatiH | "eShAhyeva prakR^itiravikR^itiH' (vatsashrutiH) ityAdivAkyoktastrIliN^gaprakR^ityAdishabdAH kiM viShNuvAchino.anyavAchino veti sandehaH | anyavAchina iti pUvarH pakShaH | teShAM anyatraiva prasiddhatvAt.h strIliN^gatvAchcha | 
paramapuruShe strItvAbhAvAt.h | "nainaM vAchA striyaM bruvan.h' iti strItvaniShedhena rUpavisheSheNa strItvamityasyApyayogAt.h | brahmAdinapuMsakashabdasya kalatrAdishabdeShviva shabdasAdhutvamAtreNa yuktatve.api iha na tathA kalpakAbhAvAt.h | nAmAni sarvANItyasya saN^kochasambhavAt.h | vashIkR^itabhArye.api bhAryApadaprayogAdarshanena anyagatastrItvasyeshAdhInatvamupetya tadadhInatvanyAyena Ishe tachChabdavR^ittirityasyApyayogAditi | siddhAntastu "hantaitamevapuruShaM sarvANi nAmAnyabhivadanti' (vatsashrutiH) ityAdishrutau sAmAnyato.asheShashabdavAchyatvaM IshasyoktvA nadIsamudradR^iShyAntasyopAdAnAt.h | "mAyAM tu prakR^itiM vindyAt.h' (shve.u.4-10) "prakR^itirvAsanetyevaM tavechChAnantyakathyate' ityAdi shrutismR^itiShu ichChAyAH prakR^itipadavAchyatvAt.h tasyAshcha "so.abhidhyA sa jUtiH' ityAdishrutau IshasvarUpatvokteH | "eSha strI eSha puruShaH eSha prakR^itiH' (paiN^gishrutiH) iti sAkShAt.h prakR^itishabdavAchyatvA nAnAt.h | prakR^itiM pravishya tAM mahadAdyAtmanA pariNAmya tanniyAmakatayA Atmano bahudhAprakAreNa prakR^iShyAkR^itiH iti yogasambhavAt.h avyavadhAnena sUtihetutvarUpastrItvasya yadbhUtayonimiti shrutau yonishabdena gAnAt.h prakR^ityAdisarvastrIliN^gashabdamukhyArtho harireveti || 6 ||

|| OM etena sarve vyAkhyAtA vyAkhyAtAH OM || 7 ||

atra pUrvavaiShamyena pUrvapakShotthAnAtsaN^gatiH | "asadvA idamagra AsIdityAdau shrutAsachChUnyAdishabdAH kiM IshavAdino.anyavAdino veti sandehaH | pUrvapakShastu | yuktaM pUrvoktarUpaM strItvaM rUpAhAneH na tu niShedhyatvAdirUpaM asadAdipravR^ittinimittaM rUpahAneH | asato niHsvarUpasya niyamanAbhAvena tasya IshAdhInatvAyogena tadadhInanyAyasyApyanavatArAt.h | ato.asadAdishabdA anyavAchinaH iti | siddhAntastu | prasiddhashUnyatvAdeH IshagatatvAbhAve.api "shamUnaM kurute' ityAdismR^ityuktayogasambhavAt.h asato.apyasattvAdinA niyamanasambhavena tadadhInatvAdyuktasAdhakena cha asachChUnyAdishabdamukhyArtho harireveti | phalaM tUktameva || 7 ||

|| iti shrIrAghavendrayatikR^itAyAM nyAyamuktAvalyAM Adye.adhyAye chaturthaH pAdaH || 

|| atha dvitIyAdhyAye prathamaH pAdaH ||

pUrvoktasamanvayasya atra virodhanirAsAt.h pUrvAdhyAyenAsya hetuhetumadbhAvasaN^gatiH | yuktisamayashrutiyuktiyuktAshrutivirodhAnAM padAntyAdibhaN^gena ashvAdivatpravartamAnAnAM krameNa pAdachatuShyayena nirAsaH kriyate | chatUrUpatvAt.h Adyanaye smR^itivirodho nirasyate | 

|| OM smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^ga iti chennAnyasmR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^gAt.h OM || 1 || 

|| OM itareShAM chAnupalabdheH OM || OM etena yogaH pratyuktaH OM || 

prAk.h shrutisamanvayenoktaM viShNorvishvakartR^itvaM yuktaM naveti sandehaH | na yuktamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | shivAdikartR^itvabodhakasyaiva sAN^khayakApilAdisarvashrautasmR^itivirodhAt.h | tAsAM cha sarvaj~natvAdinA prasiddhashivAdyapraNItatvena AptirUpaguNayuktatvena prAbalyAt.h | shruteshcha apauruSheyatvena nirmUlatayA daurbalyAt.h | kaNAdAdimate shruterAptoktatvena samUlakatve.api tatsmR^itInAM vispaShyArthatvasayuktikatvAbhyAM prAbalyAttulyabalatvAbhAvena viruddhatvena cha vastuni vikalpasya durbalatve shrutyA bAdhasyAyogAt.h deshAdibhedena avirodhasya cha shrutyAdau tatratatra tasyatasya sarvakartR^itvoktyA yuktatvAt.h "virodhetvanapekSham.h' (pU.mI.) iti pUrvatantrasya virodhanaye smR^itInAM shrutimUlatvena prAmANyamiti pakSha eva shrutivirodhena tAsAM bAdhokteH iha tu smR^itInAM shivAdipratyakShamUlatvena vaiShamyAt.h | ataH tattatsmR^ityanurodhena shivAdikartR^itva eva shrutInAM neyatvAt.h bauddhArhatAdismR^itivirodhena aprAmANyAdvA iti | siddhAntastu | paJNcharAtrAdismR^itInAM sarvaj~natamaviShNvAdipraNItatvena shrutyuktasaMvAdena tatsahAyena 
vispaShyArthavAditvena cha balavattayA tadbAdhitatvAt.h shaivAdismR^ityuktasAdhanAnuShThAne.api tatphalatvenoktasya pratyakShayogyAnupalabdhyA phalavisaMvAdAt.h AptoktatvasyApyabhAvena avaidikasmR^itInAmaprAmANyAt.h shrutisamanvayenoktaM viShNorvishvakartR^itvaM yuktamiti | samanvayasUtre upakramAdibhireva vedArtho nirNeya ityuktAvapi atra te.api tadanurodhena neyA iti shaN^kanAtpunarArambhaH | shAstrayoninaye dR^iShyaphaleShu prAmANyaM apasmR^itInAmupetya tatreva vishvakAraNatve.apyastu prAmANyamiti prApte "nAvedavid.h' ityAdinA tatra na mAnatvamityuktam.h | atra tu pratyakShaphala eva visaMvAdAt.h aprAmANyamuchyata iti tenAsya agatArthatvamiti dhyeyam.h | phalaM tu atrAdhyAye sarvatra janmAdisUtroktavishvakartR^itvAkShepaH tatsamAdhishcha || 1 || 

|| OM na vilakShaNatvAdasya tathAtvaM cha shabdAt.h OM || 2 || 

|| OM dR^ishyate tu OM || 

atra phalavisaMvAdena apasmR^itInAmaprAmANye tata eva shrutishrautasmR^ityoraprAmANyaM syAditi shaN^kanAdApavAdikI saN^gatiH | shrutiH shrautasmR^itishcha kiM pramANamuta neti sandehaH | "vR^iShyikAmaH kArIryA yajeta' ityAdyuktakArIryAdyanuShThAne vR^iShyayAdyadR^iShyayA phalavisaMvAdena apasmR^itivat.h apauruSheyatve.api apramANameva shrutiH apauruSheyatvameva neti vA atra bhavati | shrautasmR^itishchaiva na mAnamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | siddhAntastu | "vAchA virUpanityayA' ityAdivachanena devAdinaye bhAShyoktayuktyA cha shruterapauruSheyatvena shrautasmR^itestadanusAritvena cha anAshaN^kitadoShatayA sAkShivatpramANatvAt.h | prAmANyasya cha "na chakShurna shrotramityAdinA vedArthasya chakShurAdyayogyatvoktyA saMvAdamanapekShyatayA svata eva j~neyatvAt.h phalavisaMvAdarUpApavAdasya adhikArivisheShANAM phaladarshanenAsiddheH | kvachitphalavisaMvAdanimittasya cha kartrAdivaiguNyanimittatvenopapatteH | apasmR^itInAM taiH saMvAdenaiva tatprAmANyaj~naptyaN^gIkAreNa tadvaiShamyAt.h pramANameva shrutishrautasmR^itaya iti || 2 ||

|| OM abhimAnivyapadeshastu visheShAnugatibhyAm.h OM || 3 || 

|| OM dR^ishyate cha OM || 

pUrvatra visaMvAdAkhyayuktimAtravirodho nirastaH | atra shruteH pratItArthaprachyutikAritvena dR^iDhayuktivirodho nirasyata iti saN^gatiH | "mR^idabravIdApo.abruvan.h tatteja evasau' ityAdi shrutiH pramANamuta neti sandehaH | AdikAlInapR^ithivyAdivaktR^itvAdyabhidhAtrI shrutirna mAnamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | mR^inna vakti jaDatvAnmR^ittvAdvA sammatavaditi yuktiviruddhArthakatvAjjaDasya karmendriyahInasya kartR^itvekShitR^itvAderayogAt.h idAnIntanamR^idAdikAraNatvena anumitasya vA parasiddhamAtrasya vA mR^idAdeH pakShIkAreNa yukteH dharmigrAhakamAnabAdhasyApyabhAvAdeva vedaikadeshasya amAnatvAt.h tatsAmAnyAditareShu tathAtvamiti jaiminIyanyAyena kR^itsnavedasyApi amAnatvamiti | siddhAntastu prAguktadishA nityatvena anAshaN^kitadoShasya vedasya aprAmANyAyogAt.h jaDasya vaktR^itvAdyayogAchcha vedaprAmANyavaktR^itvAdyabhidhAyakatvayordvayoH yAvatAvinAnupapattiH tAvatA kalpyatvAt.h tadubhayAnyathAnupapattyA "pR^ithivyAdyabhimAninyo devatAH prathitaujasaH' (bhaviShyatpurANa) ityAdivachanena mahatAM pratyakSheNa cha abhimAnichetanasya vaktR^itvAdyupayogivigrahAdimatvasya asmAdyanupalabdhibAdhanirAsAya antardhAnashaktimatvasya ityevamAdeH siddhatvAt.h mR^idAdisthamR^ittvAdipravR^ittinimittasya abhimAnyadhInatayA tadadhInatvanyAyena tachChabdAnAM tadabhimAnidevatAsveva mukhyatvAchcha mR^idAdishabditadevavaktR^itvAdyaN^gIkAre yuktivirodhAbhAvAt.h pramANameva vedaH iti || 3 ||

|| OM asaditi chenna pratiShedhamAtratvAt.h OM || 4 || 

|| OM apItau tadvatprasaN^gAdasamaJNjasam.h OM || OM na tu dR^iShyAntabhAvAt.h OM || OM svapakShadoShAchcha OM || OM tarkApratiShThAnAdapyanyathAnumeyamiti chedevamapyanirmokShaprasaN^gaH OM || OM etena shiShyA aparigrahA api vyAkhyAtAH OM || 

atra shrutyasahitayuktyavirodhAya mR^idAdishabdAnAM anyArthatAyAM shrutisahitayuktyavirodhAya "sadeva saumya' (ChAM.6-2-1) iti asadAdishabdAnAM anyArthateti kimu vAchyamiti pUrvasiddhAntanyAyena shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | viShNorvishvakartR^itvAvedakaH "yato vA' ityAdi vedaH pramANaM uta neti sandehaH | na pramANamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | layavR^ittivishvaprAgabhAvaH vishvahetuH ananyathAsiddhaniyatapUrvakShaNavR^ittitvAt.h sampratipannavaditi yuktyA "asadevedamagra AsIt.h' ityasachChabditavishvaprAgabhAva hetutvaparashrutisahitayA tasya hetutve siddhe vimatAH bhAvAH pralaye asantaH bhAvatvAt.h kAryavat.h iti laye bhAvamAtrAsiddhau kAryasya sakartR^ikatvaniyamAt.h parisheSheNa asadeva sanmanokurutetyAdi shrutisahitena IshvarAdikalpanAtaH lAghavena upAdAnasyApi prAgabhAvasyaiva kartR^itvAditi | prAgabhAvakartR^itvasAdhakayuktiviruddhatvAt.h | vR^ikSheNa sthIyata ityAdau kartrarthakatR^itIyAyAH achetane.api darshanena abhAvasya kartR^itvasvIkAre anupapatyabhAvAchcha | kiJNcha kUlapatanavat.h akartR^ikameva jagat.h kAryatvAt.h ghaTavat.h jIvakartR^ikaM vA dadhyAdivajjaDakartR^ikaM vA ityAdi yuktibhiH "akasmAddhIdamAvirAsIdityAdishrutisahitAbhirviruddhatvAchcheti | siddhAntastu | viShNoH kartR^itvasya j~nAnachikIrShAdimatvarUpatayA abhimatatvena tR^itIyAyogitvamAtratvAbhAvAt.h | tasya cha svarUpata eva niShedhAtmake ayogAt.h | kAryanAshe kAraNamAtrAvasheShaniyamena pralaye bhAvamAtrAvasheShopapatteH | tanmAvasheShasya cha vimatotpattiH bhAvAdhInA utpattimatvAt.h | vimato vinAshaH sasheShaH nAshatvAt.h sammatavat.h ityAdibhiH laye bhAvasattvAvedakayuktibhirviruddhatavAta | bhAvatvayukteruktadishA satpratipakShitatvena layakAle vyabhichAreNa cha duShyatayA pralaye bhAvAbhAvasheShasya aprAmANikatvAt.h shuShkatarkasyApratiShThatve.api IshakartR^itvAgamasahAyAsmaduktasya prAmANyasambhavAt.h | niShkAraNatvajIvakAraNatvAdeH uktayuktivirodhinaiva nirAsAchcha asadvetyAdishrutInAM cha "etena sarve vyAkhyAtAH' (bra.sU.1-4-29) ityuktanyAyena IshaparatvAt.h pramANameva viShNukartR^itvashrutij~nAnamiti || 4 || N.M-4 
|| OM bhoktrApatteravibhAgashchetsyAllokavat.h OM || 5 || 

pUrvaM brahmaNo.asatvamupetya abhAvasyaiva kartR^itvaM shaN^kitam.h | iha tu uktadishA tatsattvamupetya jIvasyApi kartR^itvamAshaN^kayate iti saN^gatiH | viShNureva kartA ityAdi shrutisamanvayenoktaM vishvakartR^itvaM yuktaM na veti sandehaH | na yuktamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | "pare.avyaye sarva ekIbhavanti' (muM.3-2-7) iti shrutyA muktairaikyAt.h anyasya anyatvAdarshanena prAgaikyasyAvashyakatvena saMsArijIvAbhinnatvAditi shrutisiddhAbhinnatvayuktiviruddhatvAt.h | nacha prAgapyaikye abhUtatadbhAvArthaka "chvi' pratyayAyogaH | prAgbhedasyApyaN^gIkArAt.h tannivR^ittyarthatvena tadupapattiH | evaM cha jIveshayoraikyasya tayoH sarvakartR^itvAlpakartR^itvaviruddhadharmatyAgena tasya jIvasAlakShaNyena vA jIvadharmatyAgena vA tasya Isha sAlakShaNyena vA sambhavena AdyayA viShNau sarvakatarR^itvasyAsambhavAt.h | antye.ativyApteriti | siddhAntastu | ekIbhAvashruteH "niraJNjanaH paramaM sAmyamupaiti divyam.h' (muM.5-3) ityuttaravAkyena "yathodakaM shuddhe shuddhamAsiktaM tAdR^igevetyAdi vAkyAntareNa cha virodhena prAgbhinnasyApi pashchAdatyantAbhedasya kvApyadarshanena cha muktyaikyaparatvena jIvaikyasya vA siddheH yuktaM viShNoH vishvakartR^itvamiti || 5 || 

|| OM tadananyatvamArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH OM || 6 || 

|| OM bhAve chopalabdheH OM || OM sattvAchchAvarasya OM || OM asadvayapadeshAnneti chenna dharmAntareNa vAkyasheShAt.h OM || OM yukteH shabdAntarAchcha OM || OM paTavachcha OM || OM yathA prANAdiH OM || 

pUrvatra Ishasya vishvakartR^itvameva neti shaN^kApAstA | atra tu shrutisiddhaM tadupetya svAdhInasattAdiyuktaM sAdhanApekShaM taditi shaN^kA apAsyata iti saN^gatiH janmAdisUtroktaM viShNossvAtanteNa kartR^itvaM yuktaM na veti sandehaH | na yuktamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | mahadAdisR^iShyiH kartranyasvatantrasAdhanasApekShA sR^iShyitvAt.h paTasR^iShyivat.h ityAdi bahuyuktiviruddhatvAt.h "adbhayaH sambhUtaH pR^ithivyai rasAchcha' (puruSha.sU.) iti shrutau abAdisvatantrasAdhanAntaroktivirodhAchcha | IshvarasR^iShyitvAttadanapekShAyAM IshAdhInasAdhanAntarApekShA na syAditi | siddhAntastu | yuktameva svatantrakartR^itvaM viShNoH "kiMsvidAsIdadhiShThAnaM ArambhaNam.h' (R^i.10-81-2) iti shrutau adhiShThAnAdeH sAdhanasyAkShepAt.h tathA "nAsadAsInno sadAsIt.h' (R^i.10-129-2) ityAdishrutau bhUtAdisAdhanAsattvakathanAt.h 
tayoshcha sAdanasattvAvedakashrutyantaravirodhena cha svarUpeNAkShepAsatavayorayoge tatsvAtantyaniShedhaparatvena tayA shrutyA vimatA sR^iShyiH na kartranyasAdhanApekShA paratantrakartranyatve sati sR^iShyitvAt.h ityAdi vyatirekAnumAnaishcha prAguktaiH viruddhatvAt.h | prANAdInAM IshAnupraviShThatvena asvAtantyavat.h "prakR^itiM puruShaM chaiva pravishya' (kUmar.pu.) iti smR^ityA IshAnupraviShThatvena sAdhanAnAM asvAtantyanishchayena bAdhitatvAt.h | kartranyasvatantrasAdhanasya shrutyAdipramANairanupalambhAt.h "adbhayaH' ityAdeH "dravyaM karma cha kAlashcha' ityAdi shrutyA avarasAdhanatvaparatvena tadvirodhyabhAvAt.h IshvarasyApi lIlayA sR^iShyau sAdhanAntaropAdAnasambhavAchcheti | 

|| OM itaravyapadeshAddhitAkaraNAdidoShaprasaktiH OM || 7 ||

|| OM adhikaM tu bhedanirdeshAt.h OM || OM ashmAdivachcha tadanupapattiH OM || OM upasaMhAradarshanAnneti chetkShIravR^iddhi OM || OM devAdivapi loke OM || OM kR^itsnaprasaktirniravayavatvashabdakopo vA OM || 

atra pUvaroktaM prANAdi jIvAnAmasvAtantyaM ayuktaM jIvAnAM svatantrakartR^itvAnubhAvAt.h ityAkShepAt.h saN^gatiH | janmAdisUtre abhimataM viShNoreva svatantrakartR^itvaM yuktaM na veti sandehaH | pUrvapakShastu | "jIvAdbhavanti bhUtAni' ityAdishrutyA ahamidaM karomItyAdi svatantrakartR^itvAnubhavena cha saMvAdinyA jIvaH kartA chetanatvAt.h siddhAntyabhimateshavat.h iti yuktyA viShNureva svatantraH kartA ityasya viruddhatvAdeva cha ghaTAdau jIvasyaiva kartR^itve siddhe lAghavena mahAdAdAvapi sa eva kartetyasya nyAyyatvAt.h Ishasya cha ayogyatvena kadApyapratyakShatApattyA shravaNAdivaiyarthyena yogyatve vAchye sadA sarvatra sataH iti ihedAnImanupalambhena yogyAnupabdhyA tadabhAvanishchayena tatkatarR^itvakalpanasya gauravaparAhatatvAchcha na yuktaM tatkartR^itvamityekaH | anyastu | mahadAdikartR^itvasya jIve anubhavavirodhAt.h astu tatreshaH kartA na tu ghaTAdAvapi tasya anubhavasiddhajIvamAtrakartR^itve kalpanAlAghavAditi | siddhAntastu | jIvasyaiva svatantrakartR^itve svahitAkaraNasya cha anubhavasiddhasyAyogAt.h | tR^iNoddharaNAdau kR^itsnasAmarthyena ekadeshena vA pravR^ittatve anubhavena "eSha nityo niravayavaH' iti shrutyA cha viruddhatvena pravR^ittyayogAchcha | bAdhakAtsadA sarvatra sthitasyApi Ishasya devAdivat.h pishAchAdivachcha antardhAnashaktyAnupalambhasambhavena "jIvAdbhavanti' ityAdishruteH apUrvatAliN^gena IshaparatvopapatteH | svatantrakartR^itAnubhavasya cha chArvAkasya jaDadehasvAtantyabuddheriva IshAdhIne jIve bhramatvAchchetanatvayukteshcha ashmAdivadasvatantratvAt.h na jIvaH svatantrakarteti satpratipakShatvena aprayojakatayA svAtantAbhAvAchcha na jIvaH | svatantraH pramiteshvaraH ghaTAdau mahadAdau cha svAtantrakartetyaN^gIkAre gauravasya prAmANikatvena adoShatvAchcha dvAvapi pUrvapakShAvayuktAviti viShNoreva kartR^itvaM yuktamiti | phalaM tu pUrvottarapakShayoH lakShaNasya yathAkramaM asambhavAtivyAptI tatsamAdhishcha siddhAnte || 7 ||

|| OM shrutestu shabdamUlatvAt.h OM || 8 ||

|| OM Atmani chaivaM vichitrAshcha hi OM || OM svapakShadoShAchcha OM || OM sarvopetA cha taddarshanAt.h OM || OM vikaraNatvAnneti chettaduktam.h OM || 

atra kR^itsnaprasaktyAdidoShaH jIvavadIshasya kartR^itve.api syAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | viShNossarvakartR^itvaM yuktaM na veti sandehaH | pUrvapakShastu | viShNostR^iNAdAnAdalpakArye.api kR^itsnaprasaktyA pravR^ittau aprekShAvatvApAtAt.h | ekadeshena pravR^ittau nehanAnetyAdi niraMshashrutivyAkopAt.h jIvAdIshevisheShAsiddhayA tatraivAyaM doSho neshe ityasya cha kalpakAbhAvAt.h "achakShaH shrautraM tadapANipAdam.h' iti shrutyA shrotrAdikAraNAbhAvAchcha ayuktaM viShNoH kartR^itvamiti | siddhAntastu | "yo.asau viruddhaH aviruddhaH manuramanuH' (paiN^gishrutiH) ityAdi loke viruddhadharmANAM Ishe.aviruddhatavokteH tasya shabdaikagamyatayA shuShkatarkAgocharatvena tadabAdhyatvAt.h "vichitrashaktiH puruShaH purANaH' ityAdishrutyA viShNoryuktiviruddhanirvAhakanityasarvaviShayakaghaTitaghaTakashaktisatvAchcha | jIve cha pUrvoktasya kasyApyabhAvena Ishasya tato visheShAt.h bhAvasya "na tasya kAryaM karaNam.h' ityAdinA prAguktashruteH prAkR^itaparatvAt.h 
j~nAnAnandAdiguNamayapANyAdyavayavayuktadehasattvAchcha yuktaM tatkartR^itvamiti | shAstrayoninaye shuShkatarkasya sAdhakatvaM netyuktam.h | atra bAdhakatvaM neti bhedaH || 8 ||

|| OM na prayojanavattvAt.h OM || 9 || 

|| OM lokavattu lIlAkaivalyam.h OM ||

pUrvaM hetumukhayuktivirodho.apAstaH atra tu phalamukhadR^iDhayuktivirodhaH nirasyata iti saN^gatiH | viShNoH tatprayojanoddeshe.apUrNatApattyA tAdR^ishasya chaitrAderiva sarvakartR^itvAyogAt.h tadanuddeshe cha chetanasya prekShAvataH pravR^itterevAyogAt.h | dayAjanyapUlAbhAvAt.h dayayA pravR^ittirityasyAyogAditi | siddhAntastu | "devasyaiSha svabhAvo.ayam.h' (mAM.u.2-9) iti shrutyA vishvasR^iShyayAdeH IshasvabhAvatvAt.h svAbhAvikasya nimeShAdeH prayojanAnuddeshe.api dasharnA phalAbhAve.api anAyAsAdhyAN^gulyagrAdichalanasyeva Ishasya vishvasR^iShyayAderanAyAsasAdhyatvena upapannatvAchcha | dayAjanyasya svaphalasyAbhAve.api paraprayojanasya sattvAchcha lIlArUpo vishvasR^iShyayAdiH yuktaH iti || 9 || 

|| OM vaiShamyanairghR^iNye na sApekShatvAttathAhi darshayati OM || 10 || 

|| OM na karmAvibhAgAditi chennAnAditvAt.h OM || OM upapadyate chApyupalabhyate cha OM || 

atra pUrvanayoktaparaprayojanarUpaphalaviShaye yuktivirodho nirasyata iti saN^gatiH | viShNossarvakartR^itvaM yuktaM naveti sandehaH | na yuktamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | viShNoH paraprayojanoddeshena pravR^ittAvupetAyAM tattadIyakarmAnapekShatayA teShAMteShAM phaladAne nirnimittaM vibhAgena sukhaduHkhAdi dadataH vaiShamyanairghR^iNyApAtAt.h karmApekShayA phaladAne karmaNAmapi tadadhInatvena nirnimittaM vibhAgena sukR^itaduShkR^ite kArayataH punaH vaiShamyAdyApAtAt.h | viShNvanadhInatve anadhInakarmApekShitatvena svAtantyachyuteti | siddhAntastu | viShNostattadIyakamarApekShayA phaladAne.api karmaNAM pravAhataH anAditvena pUrvapUrvatattadIyakarmApekShayA uttarottarasukR^itAdikarma kArayitvA phalaM dadAtItyaN^gIkAreNa vibhAgena karmAnuShThApanasya nirnimittatvAbhAvAt.h karmaNAmapi "eSha hyeva sAdhukarma kArayati' iti shrutyA svAdhInatvena asvAtantAnApatteshcha | anAdikarmaNAM svAdhInatvena anyathAkaraNashaktasyApi evameva tadapekShayA phaladAne prAptavaiShamyAdeshcha | dharmAdeH phalahetutvAvedaka vedaprAmANyAnApAdakatvena vidhiniShedhAtItasya tasya tadvato jIvasyeva pratyavAyahetutvAchcha anAditattadyogyatAnusAritvasyaivasamashabdArthatayA "samohaM sarvabhUteShu' (bha.gI.9-29) ityuktasarvasamatvarUpasadguNAvirodhitvAchcha | "sakArayetpuNyamathApi pApaM na tAvatA doShivAn.h' (chaturvedashikhA) ityAdishrutau doShatvenoktatvAchcha adoShatvAdyuktaM viShNossarvakartR^itvamiti || 10 || 

|| OM sarvadharmopapatteshcha OM || 11 ||

evaM sraShyR^itvAdyekaikaguNe ekaikadoShAbhAve cha yuktyavirodhaH pUrvanayeShUktaH atra tu upasaMhAratvAt.h sarvatreti saN^gatiH | viShNoruktanirdoShaguNapUrNatvaM yuktaM naveti sandehaH | na yuktamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | viShNuH na nirdoShatvena guNapUrNavAn.h chetanatvAt.h chaitrAdivaditi yuktivirodhAt.h anyathA doShAbhAve guNatvaM cha na syAditi | siddhAntastu | brahma sadAprAptasarvasadguNaM tatprepsutve sati tatra shaktatvAt.h sammatavat.h | brahma sadA tyaktasarvadoShaM tajjihAsutve sati tatra shaktatvAditi yuktyanugR^ihItAyAH "guNAH shrutAH suviruddhAshcha deve' (sauparNa0/jAbAlikhila) ityAdishrutyA nirdoShaguNapUrNatvasya siddheH chetanasya aprayojakatvAt.h yuktaM viShNornirdoShaguNapUrNatvam.h | nacha yuktidvaye visheShaNAsiddhiH | prekShAvattvenaiva tadanumAnAt.h visheShyasya cha "shrutestu' (bra.sU.2-1-28) iti naye siddhatvAditi | phalaM tu samanvayAdhyAyoktArthasya AkShepastatsamAdhishcha || 11 || 

|| iti shrImadrAghavendrayatikR^itAyAM nyAyamuktAvalyAM dvitIyAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH || 

|| atha dvitIyaH pAdaH ||

itareShAM chAnupalabdheriti (bra.sU.2-1-2) smR^itinaye guNasUtroktahetuvistR^itirUpatvAt.h tadanantaraM samayavirodhaH atrochyate iti vA prAguktadishA vA pUrvapAdenAsya saN^gatiH | "akShapAdakaNAdau cha' ityAdi smR^ityA samayAnAM dvaividhyAt.h hetumatvena haitukAnAM prabalatvAt.h Adau nirasyate | 

|| OM rachanAnupapatteshcha nAnumAnam.h OM || 1 ||

|| OM pravR^itteshcha OM || OM payombuvachchettatrApi OM || OM vyatirekAnavasthiteshchAnapekShatvAt.h OM || 

janmAdisUtroktaM viShNossarvakartR^itvaM yuktaM na veti sandehaH | na yuktamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | mahadAdikAryaM svatantrakAraNajanyaM sajAtIyakAraNajanyaM vA kAryatvAt.h ghaTavadityAdyanumAnaiH siddhaM vishvahetuH pradhAnaM svatantrapravR^ittirUpakartR^itvavat.h vastutvAt.h ambvAdivat.h iti svataH pariNAmavat.h dravyatvAtkShIravaditi vA.ananyApekShatayA pradhAnasya kartR^itvaM sAdhayatA nirIshvarasAN^khayanayena viruddhatvAditi | siddhAntastu | AdyAnumAnasya siddhasAdhanatAparAhatatvAt.h antyayoshcha mahadAdikaM na svatantrapravR^ittimat.h achetanatvAt.h chetanasR^iShyaM vA kAyartvAt.h ghaTavadityAdinA satpratipakShatvAt.h | "etasyaivAkSharasya prashAsane gArgi prAchyo.anyA nadyaH syandante' (bR^i.5-8-9) "etena ha vAva payomaNDaM bhavati' iti "na R^ite tvatkriyate' (R^i.10-112-9) ityAdishrutibhiH ambvAdAvapi chetanapravR^ittidR^iShyayA sAdhyavaikalyAchcha duShyatvena kevalAchetanakartR^itvasyAprAmANikatvAt.h pramANaviruddhatvAchcha | tatpratipAdakasamayasya duShyatayA tadvirodhasyAkiJNchitkaratvAt.h shrutisamanvayenoktaM viShNovirshvakartR^itvaM yuktamiti | phalaM tu atra sarvatra janmAdisUtroktakartR^itvAkShepasamAdhI || 1 || 

|| OM anyatrAbhAvAchcha na tR^iNAdivat.h OM || 2 || 

anIshvarasAN^khayamatasya vaidikavAdaM prati atyantavirodhitvAt.h Adau tannirasya atra IshaguNakapradhAnakartR^itvaparasAN^khayamataM nirasyata iti saN^gatiH | viShNoH svAtanteNa kartR^itvaM yuktaM na veti sandehaH | na yuktamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | kevalAchetanapradhAnasya pariNAmAdyayoge.api guNabhUteshAnugR^ihItasya parjanyAnugR^ihItapR^ithivyAdestR^iNAdyAtmaneva mahadAtmanA pariNAmopapatteH prAguktashrutInAM guNabhUteshaparatvena tadavirodhAchcheti evaMrUpasAN^khayamatavirodhAditi | siddhAntastu | "yachcha kiJNchijjagatsarvam.h' "mahAnA.u.) ityAdishrutau sarvavastUnAM sattAdipradAnAya sarvagatvokteH IshapreraNAM vinA kasyApi vastunaH sattvasyaivAbhAvAt.h | "sa eva bhUyo nijavIryachoditAm.h' (bhAga.1-10-23) ityAdismR^itau prakR^ityAdikAraNasattAderapi IshAyattatvokteH IshaH parjanyavannAnugrAhakamAtraM kAryakAraNAkhyasarvavastusattvAdipradatvAt.h ya evaM sa evaM yathA sammatavat.h iti tasya svAtantyasiddheshcha sAN^khayamatasya durmatatvena tadvirodhasyAkiJNchitkaraNatvAt.h yuktaM tasyaiva svAtanteNa jagatkartR^itvamiti | 

|| OM abhyupagame.apyarthAbhAvAt.h OM || 3 ||

|| OM asti tu OM || OM gauNyasambhavAt.h OM || OM shabdAchcha OM || OM syAchchaikasya brahmashabdavat.h OM || OM pratij~nAhAniravyatirekAchChabdebhyaH OM || OM yAvadvikArantu vibhAgo lokavat.h OM || 

adhibhUtAdhidaivaparamAtmajIvavichAreShu Adau sUchIkaTAhanyAyena adhibhUtAdhidaivavichAraH kriyate | atra viyatpadena bhUtAkAshatadabhimAninau chochyante | AkAshaH utpattimAnnaveti sandehaH | notpattimAniti prAptam.h | viyadanutpattyanubhavena viyat.h anutpattimat.h vibhutvAtsammatavaditi yuktyA chAnugR^ihItayA bahutvena cha prabalayA "anAdirvAyamAkAshaH' ityAdyanAditvashrutyA 
tatsiddheH | etadvirodhAyAH "AkAshassambhUtaH' iti tadutpattishruteramAnatvena anutpattishruteH bhAktatvavarNanasyApyayogAt.h | "na jAyate mriyate' ityAdau anutpattivAchishabdasya mukhyArthatvAdR^iShyayA kAraNena vinA dvairUpyAyogena ihApi mukhyArthasya nyAyyatvAditi | siddhAntastu | viyadutpattimat.h "AtmanaH AkAshassambhUtaH' (tai.2-1) ityAdyutpattishruterbAhulyAt.h | nacha shrutyantaravirodhaH | viyachChabditAnAM bhUtAkAshatadabhimAninAM parAdhInavisheShaNAvAptirUpotpattisambhavena tadutpattishrutInAM tatsarvaviShayatayA bahuviShayatvena viyadutpattimat.h alpashaktitvAt.h ghaTavadityanumAnasadhrIchInatvena prAbalyAt.h | tadanyathAnupapattyA anAditvashruteH bAhulye.api bhUte kathamapyayogena alpaviShayatayA daurbalyena bhAktatvasya nyAyyatvAt.h "prANaH shraddhA AkAshaH iti bhAgasho hyutpadyante' iti (bhAllaveya)shrutisiddhatvAchcha ekasyAnutpattichChabdasya viriJNchabrahmaNoH brahmashabdatasyeva "sa idaM sarvamasR^ijata' iti pratij~nAvirodhena cha "AtmA vA idameka eva agra AsIt.h' ityAdiprAguktotpattishrutibAhulyavirodhena kAraNena AkAshabrahmaNoH mukhyAmukhyatvasya yuktatvAt.h iti | evaM prakR^itijIvachaitanyakAlavedamahadahaMmanobuddhayAdInAmapi parAdhInavishevAptirUpA janiruktA dhyeyA | phale tu kR^itsnajagatkartR^itvAkShepasamAdhI || 1 || 

|| OM etena mAtarishvA vyAkhyAtaH OM || 2 ||

atrAkAshAdvAyurityAdi shrautakramAdvA pUrvoktanyAyAtideshAdvA saN^gatiH | vAyushabdena bhUtamukhyAmukhyAbhimAninAM grahaNe.api mukhya eva vivAdahetusattvAt.h tanmAtra evAtra vichAraH | vAyuratra prakaraNe.abhimataparAdhInavisheShAvAptirUpotpattimAnnaveti sandehaH | notpattimAniti prAptam.h | "tejo.abannAnyAkAsha iti tAnyanityAni vAyurvAva nityaShaH' iti shruteH | nachAkAshAnutpattishruterivAsyAH api gauNArthatvAt.h na punashchodyAvakAshaH | AkAshavadvAyorapi janmavatve tejo.abannAkAshAnAmanutpattipUrvakaM vAyonirtyatvokterayogAt.h | na chAkAshAdipadaiH bhUtAnAmanutpattipUrvakaM vAyornityatvokterayogAt.h | nachAkAshAdipadaiH bhUtAnAmevokteH tato mukhyavAyoH svarUpanityatvAt.h vishiShya nityatvoktiriti vAchyam.h | bhUtamAtragrahaNe hetorabhAvAt.h | "tejo.abannAnyAkAsha iti tAnyachetanAni vAyurvAva chetanaH' iti shrutau vishiShya chetanatvoktyA sarvajIvasAdhAraNasvarUpanityatvAyogAchcha | "kuvidaN^ga' (R^i.7-91-1) iti mantroktasarvadevopAsyatvAchcha | "nodayo na nimlochaH' iti shrutyA vAyorudayAstamayashUnyatvAchcha | vAyurna janimAn.h paramanityatvAt.h paramachetanatvAdIshavadityAdi yukteshcha | evaM nityatvavyApyAnekahetumato.api janimatve anubhavavirodhAditi | siddhAntastu | vAyurdehasambandhAkhyaparAdhInavisheShAvAptirUpajanimAn.h prANAdvAyurityAdyutpattishruteH | alpashaktitvayukteshcha | tAdR^ishajanyabhAvashravaNAchcha | IshavadasyApi tAdR^ishajanimatvAbhAve tayorviruddhasvAtantApAtAchcha | na choktashrutyAdivirodhaH | svarUpAtiriktaj~nAne nityatvAbhiprAyeNa tasya sarvasyopapatteriti | phale tu prAgvat.h || 2 || 

|| OM asambhavastu sato.anupapatteH OM || 

atrAsambhavajanmano nabhaHprabhR^iterjaniriva IshasyApi janirastviti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | sarvakatarR^itvenokto viShNuH kiM janimAnnaveti sandehaH | janimAneveti prAptam.h | "asataH sadajAyate' (R^i.10-72-2) iti sachChabditeshasya janmashruteH | nacha "na jAyate mriyate' (kA.1-2-18) ityAdyanAditvashrutivirodha iti | asyAH svarUpAnAditvaparatvena janishruteshcha parAdhInavisheShAvAptiparatvena vyavasthopapatteH | anyathA prAguktachitprakR^ityAdAvapi samAnatvAt.h dehAnAditvAvisheShAditi | siddhAntastu | dehAnAditvAdinA chitprakR^itisamasyApi Ishasya svatantratvAdasataH kAraNatvAnupapatteshcha sadajAyateti shruteH "brahma vA asat.h sadvAva prANaH' iti shrutyA vAyorIshajanyatvaparatvAt.h na parAdhInavisheShAvAptirUpotpattimAn.h viShNuriti | phale tu kR^itsnajagatkartR^itvAkShepasamAdhI || 3 || 

|| OM tejo.atastathAhyAha OM || 4 || 

evamIshAnIshayorajanmajanmasiddhau kAraNatvena chetyuktanyAyena tejaHprabhR^iterIshajanyatve cha siddhe anyatrAnyasmAdapi janmAsya 
netyuchyata iti saN^gatiH | tejodevatA bhUtaM chakiM IshAdiva vAyudevatAto jAyate uteshAdeveti sandehaH | vAyoragniriti shrutervAyoreveti prAptam.h | sA vAyordvAramAtrapareti vAchyam.h | tena vinApi sraShyuM shaktau Ishasya dvAravaiyarthyAt.h | ashaktau tu svAtanteNa vAyujatvasyApi prApteH | tattejo.asR^ijateti shruteH IshavAyUbhayajatve.api upapatteH IshamAtraparatve choktashrutivirodhenAprAmANyAditi | siddhAntastu | IshAdeva svAtanteNa janimattejaH tattejo.asR^ijateti shruteH | anyadanapekShya sraShyuM shaktasyApi Ishasya lIlayA vAyushabditabhUtataddevatAdvArA tejobhUtataddevatAsR^iShyayupapattyA vAyoragniriti shruteH dvaramAtraparatve bAdhakAbhAvena tadvirodhAbhAvAchcheti | kAraNatvanaye vAyushabdasyeshe mukhyatvena tejobhUtataddevatayostajjatvasiddhAvapi tadvadvAyutaddevatAto.api tayorjanmeti shaN^kA nirasyata iti bhedaH | tadananyanaye sAdhanAntarasyAsvAtantyaM yuktiprAptaM nirastam.h | iha tu shrutiprAptamiti dhyeyam.h | phale tu prAgvat.h || 4 ||

|| OM ApaH OM || 5 ||

atra tejaso.anantaraprAptAyAM janakavisheShashchintyata iti saN^gatiH | abdevatAbhUtaM cha kiM tejobhUtataddevatAto.api IshAdivatsvAtanteNotpadyate atheshAdeveti saN^gatiH | agnerApa iti shruteH tejobhUtataddevatAto.apIti prAptam.h | nacha "brahmaivedamagra AsIttadapo.asR^ijata' iti shrutivirodhaH | svedasya dharmajatavadR^iShyayA ApastejojanyAH aptvAt.h svedAdivaditi yuktyA tejasa eva "taddhayApo.ajAyanta' iti shrutyA cha sadhrIchInatvena balavatyA prAchInashrutyA bAdhitatvena asyAH amAnatvAditi | siddhAntastu | tadapo.asR^ijateti shruteH tejobhUtataddevatAnAmapIshAdeva janma | agnerApaH shrutistu "sa idaM sarvamasR^ijata' "kartA sarvasya vai viShNuH' ityAdishrutismR^itigatasarvashabdamukhyArthatvAt.h anyasya svataH shaktyabhAvAchcha prAguktadishA tatra sthitatvAttenAbAdikaM janayatIti dvAramAtrapareti || 5 || 

|| OM pR^ithivyadhikArarUpashabdAntarAdibhyaH OM || 6 || 

evamuktanyAyenApi dvAratve siddhe kutradvArateti visheSho.atra chintyata iti saN^gatiH | ApaH kiM IshasyAnnasR^iShyau dvAramuta pR^ithivI sR^iShyAviti sandehaH | "ApaH aikShanta' "tA annamasR^ijanta' (ChAM.6-2-4) "adbhayaH pR^ithivI' (tai.2-1) iti shrutidvayasya parasparaviruddhArthasya niravakAshatayA nirNayAyAgenAmAnatayA na kasyApi dvAramiti prAptam.h | annashruteH "adbhayo vA annamutpadyate' "tA annamasR^ijanta' (ChAM.6-2-4) ityAdibahuvAkyAnAM prasiddhArthaparatvarUpaguNalAbhena "yatra kva cha varShati tadeve bhUyiShThamanna bhavati (ChAM.6-2-4) iti varShajatvarUpaliN^gadvArAnurodhena prasiddhAnnaparatayA pR^ithivIparatvAyogAt.h | oShadhIbhyonnamiti shrutivirodhApattyA pR^ithupadenAnyasya grahaNAyogAchcha | uktashrutivirodhAdeva apAmubhayatra dvAratvamityasyAyogAt.h | bahukalpanApattyA cha annasyobhAbhyAM janmetyasyApyayogAt.h mukhyArthatyAgApAtena adbhayaH paramparayA annajanmetyasyApyayogAchcha amAnaM shrutidvayamiti | siddhAntastu | apauruSheyatvena nirdoShatayA shrutyoraprAmANyAyogena avashyamarthAntarasya vAchyatvAt.h | tA annamasR^ijanteti shruteH pUrvatra "tattejo.asR^ijata' iti "tadapo.asR^ijata' ityuttaratra cha "tAsAM trivR^itaM trivR^itam.h' iti shravaNena asya bhUtaprakaraNatvAt.h | "yatkR^iShNaM tadannasyeti kR^iShNarUpashravaNAt.h | tasya cha "kR^iShNaiva pR^ithivI svataH' iti (vyomasaMhitA) smR^ityA pR^ithivIliN^gAt.h | liN^gaprakaraNAbhyAM "Apashcha pR^ithivI chAnnam.h' (ai.2-3-1) iti shrautaprayogeNa cha annashabdasya pR^ithivIparatvAt.h | "yatra kva cha varShati' (ChAM.8-2-4) ityAdivAkyadvayasthAnnashabdasya pR^ithivIvAchakasyApyanyathAnupapattyA lakShaNayA "tejoshitam.h' (ChAM.8-5-3) ityAdau taijasaparatvavat.h pArthivaparatvopapattyA liN^gavirodhAbhAvAt.h | apAM pR^ithivIjanmanyeva dvAratvamiti | phale tu vastvantaradvArA sAkShAtsarvakAraNatvasyAkShepasamAdhI || 6 || 

|| OM tadabhidhyAnAdeva tu talliN^gAtsaH OM || 7 || 

evamadhibhUtAdhidaivajanmashrutyavirodhamuktvA tallayashrutyavirodhamatra vaktIti saN^gatiH | prastutaviyadAdyadhibhUtAdhidaivAni janimatvena lIyanta iti siddhau tallayakartA kiM rudro viShNurveti sandehaH | rudra eveti prAptaM saMhartR^itvenaitasyaiva suprasiddheH | "rudro mA 
vishAntakaH' (mahAnA.u) iti shrutau antakapadena tasya saMhartR^itvokteshcha | "yatprayantyabhisaMvishanti' (tai.3-1) "yamapyeti bhuvanaM sAmparAye' ityAdiviShNusaMhatarR^itvashrutistu viShNuH na mArakaH janakatvAt.h rakShakatvAt.h pitrAdivadityAdiyuktisahAyarudrasaMhartR^itvashrutivirodhAt.h aprAmANyAt.h | ata eva rudrasaMhAradvAratvamapi ayuktamiti | siddhAntastu | viShNureva sarvalayakartA "tasyAbhidhyAnAt.h' (shve.1-10) iti shrutAvanAdino viShNvadhInatvoktyA sAdivishvalayaH tadadhIna iti kaimutyasiddhatvAt.h | "yamapyeti bhuvanaM sAmparAye sa no hariH' "ya idaM sarvaM vilApayati' "sraShyApAtA cha saMhartA sa eko hariH' ityAdi shrutismR^itiShu viShNusaMhartR^itvasya spaShyaM pratIteshcha | rudrasaMhartR^itvashrutiH "nimittamAtramIshasya' (bhAga.10-79-1) ityAdismR^ityA katipayasaMhAre rudrasya dvAratvaparA | yuktistu pitrAderamArakatvasya mamatAdoShaprayuktatayA pitR^itvAdiprayuktatvAbhAvena nirdoShalokavilakShaNe harau tadanApAdikaivetyaprayojiketi | phalaM tu janmAdisUtroktasaMhartR^itvAkShepasamAdhI || 7 ||

|| OM viparyayeNa tu kramo.atra upapadyate cha OM || 8 ||

sarvasyeshe layasiddhau kena krameNetyatra chintanAtsaN^gatiH | prakR^itAdhibhUtAni kiM janmakramAnurodhena lIyante vyutkrameNa veti sandehaH | janmakramAnusAreNaiveti pUrvaH pakShaH | "kramAdutpadyate kramAdvilIyate' "kramerotpattirvilayashcha' "krameNaivAsyotpattilayau' ityAdikramalayashrutibAhulyAt.h | vyutkramAdvilayashcheti shrutistu loke prAyeNotpattikrameNa layadarshanayuktyanugR^ihItena cha prabalayA kramalayashrutyA bAdhitatvAditi | siddhAntastu | vyutkrameNaiva lIyante "vyutkramAdvilayashcha' (bhAllaveya) iti niravakAshalayashruteH | kramalayashrutInAM tu "dvividhaH krama uddiShyo vyutkramo.anukramastathA | sR^iShyAvanyo laye chAnyaH' ityAdi shrutyA vyutkramasyApi kramatvena sAvakAshatvena loke pUrvotpannAnAM pUrvanAshasya asAmarthyanimittatvAdiha cha "pUrve pUrve yato viShNorityAdi(vAmana)smR^ityA pUrvotpannAnAM sAmarthyAdhikyena pashchAdapi layopapattyA prAguktayukteraprayojakatvAt.h vyutkramashrutyabAdhAditi | phalaM tu layashrutyA virodhenAnyatarAprAmANye anyatrApyAnAshvAsApAtena viShNossaMhartR^itvAdyasiddheH tadAkShepasamAdhI || 8 || 

|| OM antarA vij~nAnamanasI krameNa talliN^gAditi chennAvisheShAt.h OM || 9 || 

|| OM charAcharavyapAshrayastu syAttadvayapadesho bhAktastadbhAvabhAvitvAt.h OM ||

pUrvoktavyutkrameNa laya ityasya kvachidapavAdashaN^kAnirAsAtsaN^gatiH | prastutAdhibhUtAni sarvANi vyutkrameNa lIyante kiM kAnichit.h krameNeti sandehaH | pUvarpakShastu | "manasashcha vij~nAnam.h' iti kramAdutpannatvena shrutamanovij~nAnatattvayoH "yachChedvAN^manasI prAj~nastadyachChet.h j~nAna Atmani' (kA.u.3-13) iti krameNaiva layashruteH manovij~nAnatattve vinA anyAni vyutkrameNa lIyante iti na cha manasashcha vij~nAnamityatra manovij~nAnashabdau na tattvaparau kintu antaHkaraNAvabodhaparAviti yuktam.h | tayoshshabdayormanovij~nAnatattvayoreva mukhyatvena nirnimivaM mukhyArthatyAgAyogAt.h | vyutkramAdvilayashcheti sarvasya vyutkramalayashrutistu loke keShAJNchitkramAt.h keShAJNchidvayutkramAt.h layadarshanena lokAnusAritvayuktyupetayA manovij~nAnayoH kramalayashrutyA bAdhiteti | siddhAntastu | manastattvAntarindriyayoH vij~nAnatattvAvabodhayoH krameNa manovij~nAnashabdayoH prayogadR^iShyayA tattvamAtravAchitvAbhAvenendriyAdAvapi mukhyatvAt.h | manasashcha vij~nAnamityatra "vij~nAnatattvaM mahataH samutpannaM chaturmukhAd.h' iti smR^itivirodhAt.h | tattvaviShayatvAyogena antarindriyatajjanyAvabodhaparatayA manovij~nAnatattvayoH yathotpattilaya ityatra visheShapramANAbhAvAt.h "sarvaM vaitatkramAdutpadyate vyutkramAdvilIyate' iti sarvavyutkramalayashruteshcha sarvANi vyutkrameNaiva lIyanta iti | phale tu shrutyorvirodhenAprAmANye tatsamanvayena prAguktasraShyR^itvasaMhartR^itvAkShepasamAdhI || 9 || 

|| OM nAtmA.ashruteH nityatvAchcha tAbhyaH OM || 10 ||

evaM brahmAnyasya sarvasya vyutkrameNa laye shrutyokte tarhi brahmaNo.api so.astviti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | sarvotpattilayakartR^itvena 
prakR^ito viShNuH dehanAshAkhyalayavAnnaveti sandehaH | "sa idaM sarvaM vilApyAntastamasi lIyate' iti so.api lIyata iti prAptam.h | nityonityAnAmiti shrutistu viShNurlayavAn.h chetanatvAt.h jIvavaditi yuktyupetapUrvashrutyA bAdhitA | nacha layashrutiH apihitatvaparA kalpakAbhAvAt.h | "asambhavastu' (bra.sU.2-2-9) ityatra Ishasya svAtanteNa hetunA anutpattyuktAvapi lIlayA dehopAdAnayogopapatteriti | siddhAntastu | viShNuH na dehanAshAkhyalayavAn.h mAnAbhAvAt.h | manasi lIyate iti shrutestu "tuchChenAbhvapihitaM yadAsId.h' (R^i.10-120-3) iti shrutau pUrvatra nAsadAsIditi sarvasya layamuktvA tama AsIditi prakR^iteH sthitimuktvA brahmaNastvapihitatvasya punaH prAdurbhAvasya choktyA "tamasi nilInaH prakR^itiM puruShaM kAlaM chAnupashyati nainaM pashyati kashchana' iti paiN^gishrutyantareNa cha apihitatvArthatvAt.h anyathA "nityo nityAnAm.h' "sa nityo nirguNaH vibhuH' ityAdibahunityatvashrutivirodhAt.h | yukteshcha shrutivirodhenAmAnatvAt.h | phale tu brahmaNo laye sR^iShyayAdyayogena tadAkShepasamAdhI || 10 ||

|| OM j~no.ata eva OM || 11 || 

|| OM yukteshcha OM || 

evaM sUchIkaTAhanyAyena alpamadhibhUtAdivichAraM kR^itvA idAnIM ApAdasamApti bahuH jIvavichAraH kriyata iti saN^gatiH | jIvaH kimutpattimAn.h uta neti sandehaH | notpattimAniti prAptam.h | nityo nityAnAmiti ShaShThayantanityapadena jIvAnAM nityatvokteH "sarva ete chidAtmano vyuchcharanti' iti tadutpattishrutestu jIvasvarUpotpattikAraNAnupalabdhyA kAraNashUnyatvAditi yuktyupetayA jIvanityatvashrutyA bAdhAt.h | nacha svarUpotpattikAraNashUnyAnAmapi viyadAdInAM parAdhInavisheShAvAptirUpajanivat.h jIvasyApi sA siddheti vAchyam.h | janmashruteH tAdR^ishotpattiparatve anutpattishruterapi brahmaNIva jIvaviyadAdAvapi tadabhAvaparatvopapatteH anekArthatvasyAnyAyyatvAt.h | evaM cha tadvirodhatAdavasthyamiti prAguktasyaivAtrAkShepAditi | siddhAntastu | "te vA ete chidAtmano.avinaShyAH paraMjyotirnivishantyavinaShyA evotpadyante' (kAShAyaNashrutiH) ityavinAshenaiva jIvasya svarUpeNAnutpattAvapi tadupAdhyutpattyA parAdhInavisheShAvAptirUpotpattiparatayA tadutpattyanutpattishrutyoH upAdhisvarUpaparatayA viShayatvenAvirodhAt.h | brahmaNi parAdhInavisheShAvAptirUpotpattishruterabhAvena tatrAnutpattishrutestadabhAvaparatve.api jIvAdau tachChatisattvena tadanutpattishrutestabhAvaparatvAyogena anekArthatvasya nyAyyatvAchcha dehasambandhAkhyatAdR^ishotpattimAn.h jIva iti | phale tu sarvasraShyR^itvAkShepasamAdhI || 11 || 

|| OM utkrAntigatyAgatInAm.h OM || 12 || 

|| OM svAtmanA chottarayoH OM || OM nANuratachChateriti chennetarAdhikArAt.h OM || OM svashabdotmAnAbhyAM cha OM || OM avirodhashchandanavat.h OM || OM avasthitivaisheShyAditi chennAbhyupagamAddhR^idi hi OM || OM guNAdvA lokavat.h OM || 

jIve dharmiNi utpatyanutpattI chintite | atra taddharme parimANe.aNutvamahatve chintyete iti saN^gatiH | prakR^ito jIvaH kiM vyApto.aNurveti sandehaH | vyApta iti prAptam.h | "vyAptyA hyAtmanashchetanA nirguNAshcha' (kAShAyaNashrutiH) iti bahuvachanAntAtmavyAptatvashruteH bahutvaM bhinnAshritamityutsarganyAyApavAdakasya "R^itaM pibantau' ityAdAvivehAbhAvena jIvaparatvAt.h | "aNurhyeSha AtmA' iti jIvANutvashrutestu aNutve sarvadehasambandhasparshAdij~nAnAyogena taddehaparimANatvena sparshAdiparij~nAnamityasya cha "naikasminnasambhavAt.h' (bra.sU.2-2-33) iti nayoktadoShaduShyatayA ayogena sarvadehasambandhasparshAdij~nAnarUpayuktyupetatvena prabalashrutaviruddhAyAH aprAmANyopapatteH | nachAMshavyAptyA sparshAdij~nAnaM yuktamiti yuktiraprayojiketi vAchyam.h | aMshAnAM chetanatvena yugapadanekeShAM aikamatyAyogena viruddhakriyasya dehasyonmathanaprasaN^gAt.h | akriyatvasya vApatteH | svarUpavyAptereva vyAptitvAditi | siddhAntastu | "so.asmAchCharIrAdutkramya amuM lokamadhigachChatyamuShmAdimaM lokamAgachChati' iti shrutotkrAntigatimatvAt.h patatrivadaNurjIvaH | tAsAM vyAptergaganAdAvadR^iShyayAM 
tAbhirvyAptatvAyogena anityatvAdyApattyA nirastamadhyamaparimANe aNutvasyaiva siddheH | "aNurhyeSha AtmA' (gaupavana) iti shruteshcha | "vyAptAhyAtmAnaH' (kAShAyaNa) iti shrutestu sa AtmedaM sR^ijatIti viShNuprakaraNena eSho hyAtmA.adhyudgato mAnashakteriti vAkyasheShe shrutAtmashrutyunmAnatvaliN^gAbhyAM guhAnayanyAyena bahuvachanasya nyAyyatvAdviShNuparA | dehaikadeshasthachandanabindoH svAMshaiH sarvadehavyAptivajjIvasyApi hR^idi hyeSha Atmeti shrutyA hR^iddeshe samyak.h sthitasya svarUpAMshaiH sarvadehavyAptyA sparshAdij~nAnasambhavena yukitaraprayojiketi | phale tu shrutisamanvayAkShepasamAdhI || 12 || 

|| OM vyatireko gandhavattathA cha darshayati OM || 13 || 

atra yadi jIve.aNuH, tarhi yogino bahurUpatvAyoga iti pUrvAkShepasaN^gatiH | jIvaH kiM ekarUpo.athavAnekarUpa iti sandehaH | ekarUpa iti prAptam.h | sa ekadhA na saptadhA iti shruteH | vibhAvAtmani yogaprabhAvAddehabAhulyena bahurUpasambhave.api aNau tadayogAditi yukteshcha | aNorapi aMshairbahurUpamityasyApi "sa nityo niravayavaH' (gaupavana) iti niravayavatvashrutivyAkopenAyogAt.h | yogino.aghaTitaghaTakashaktyA abdhipAnamiva bAhurUpyaM syAditi tu IshvarasAmyApattenAyuktam.h | sa paJNchadhA sa saptadheti bAhurUpyashrutistu sayuktikaikarUpyashrutibAdhiteti | siddhAntastu | aNobhirnnAMshahInasyApi jIvasya yogArAdhitAchintyashaktikeshvaraprasAdAyattasAmarthyAdgandhavadaMshavibhAgena bAhurUpyasyopapatteH bahurUpo jIvaH | aikarUpyashrutistu svarUpaikyaparA | niravayavatvashrutirapi bhinnAMsharAhityapareti | phale tu prAgvat.h || 13 ||

jIveshayoraikyAnna jIvashakterIshAyattatvamiti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | jIvaH kiM Ishena bhinno.abhinno veti sandehaH | abhinna iti prAptaM tattvamasItyAdau padadvayalakShaNayA jIvaparaikyashruteH | asyAshcha ekamevAdvitIyamityupakramAt.h tattvamasItyupasaMhArAt.h | tattvamasi tattvamasIti navakR^itvo.abhyAsAt.h | aikasyasya mAnAntarAprAptyA apUrvatvAt.h | tasya tAvadeva chiramiti phalavattvAt.h | yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavatItyarthavAdAt.h mR^iNmayAdidR^iShyAntenopapAdanAchcha | Sha ‡•ç.hivadhatAtparyaliN^gopetatvena bAhulyAt.h | dvAsuparNetyAdi shrutirapramANam.h | anyathaikyashruternirviShayatvApAta iti | siddhAntastu | "bhinno.achintyaH paramojIvasaN^ghAtpUrNaH paraH jIvasaN^gho hyapUNarH' (kaushika) iti bhedashrutiH kadApyaikAdhikaraNyA yogyadhamarkatvarUpaviruddhadharmAdhikaraNatvAdiyuktyupetatvena "shAstragamyapareshAnAdbhedaH svAtmana Iyate | anubhUtivirodhena kathamekatvamuchyate' ityanuvyAkhyAnoktadishA upajIvyatvena prAbalyAt.h | tadvirodhenAnubhavavirodhena cha pAdadvayalakShaNataH tatpadamAtragauNArthasya jyAyastvena cha tattvamasItyAdeH tadIyaj~nAnAnandAdisadR^ishaguNatayA tatsadR^ishastvamasItyarthakatvopapatteH aikyaparatvAyogAt.h | upakramAdeH mAnAntarAviruddha eva tAtparyagamakatvAt.h | anyatra anyathA vyAkhyAtatvAchcha bhinna eva IshAjjIva iti || 14 ||

pUrvatra pR^ithagadhikaraNAdyasUtre bandhAnmokShaM tata evAbhivAJNChediti upadesha upapAditaH | atra tu tadIyadvitIyasUtroktaM tadguNasAratvamupapAdyata iti saN^gatiH | jIvo j~nAnAnandAdirUpo na veti sandehaH | na j~nAnAnandAdirUpa iti prAptam.h | "sa duHkhAdvimukta AnandI bhavati' ityAdi shruteH | idAnIM j~nAnAnandAdirUpatAnupalabdheshcha | ahamiti jIve bhAsamAne.api tatsvarUpasyAnandAdeH pratibandhAdanupalabdhirityasyAyogena j~nAnAbhAvAdanyasya bhAvarUpaj~nAnasya pratibandhakasyAbhAvAchcha | dehAdestu sukAdyanubhavarUpabhogAyatanatvena tatpratibandhakatvAyogAchcha | AnandAdirUpatve mokShAya prayatnavaiyarthyAchcha | "vij~nAnamAtmA' (Sha.u.4-11) "sa AnandaH' ityAdishrutistvanupalabdhiyuktyupetAnandAdishrutyA bAdhitA na mAnamiti | siddhAntastu | "nityAnando nityaj~nAno nityabalaH paramAtmA' "nityAnandaj~nAnabalA devAH' ityAdi shrutismR^itibhiH jIvasya j~nAnAdirUpatokteH | bAlye.anabhivyaktapuMstvAdeH pashchAdvayaktyA AnandIbhavatItyAdi bhedavyapadeshasya shrutyAdiShu siddhatvAt.h sukhAdyAtmakasya AvaraNAnaN^gIkAre nityaM tadupalambhApAtena avashyAbhyupeyAvaraNavisheShashaktyA anupalabdheshchopapattyA samyagvyaktyarthaM prayatnasambhavAchcha j~nAnAdirUpo.ayaM jIvaH iti shrutau "evaM surAH' ityadhyAhArAdiShyasiddhiH || 16 ||

astvAnandAdInAM satAmabhivyaktiH na tu kartR^itvasya tasya kadApyabhAvAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | jIvaH kiM kartA na veti sandehaH | na karteti prAptam.h | nAnyaH karteti shruteH | sarvashisyaiva kartR^itvAN^gIkAre lAghavAchcha | itaravyapadeshAdityAdau hitAkaraNAdItyuktyA jIvakartR^itvasya niShedhAchcha | nacha shrutisUtrayoH svatantrakartR^itvaniShedhe.api paratantraM tadastviti vAchyam.h | pAratantyasya kartR^itvashakteH svAdhInatve.api takShNaH prAsAdakArayitR^ipumadhInatvavat.h vetanadAnAdinA IshAdhInarUpatve AtmAnamantaroyamayatIti shrutivirodhAt.h dAruyoShAvadIshAdhInacheShyakatve kartR^itvasyAkartR^itva eva paryavasAnAt.h tadvadeva vidhiniShedhAyogyaH syAt.h | evaM sayuktikAkartR^itvashrutivirodhAt.h "yatkarma kurute tadabhisampadyate' iti jIvakartR^itvashrutiramAnamiti jaDeshamuktAnAmapravR^ittasya vidhiniShedhAkhyashAstrasya arthavattvAnyathAnupapattirUpayuktyA mokShAdyarthasAdhanAnuShThAnadarshanAt.h pratyakSheNa "AtmAnameva lokamupAsIta' ityAdAvupAsanAdikriyAyAM jIvasya kartR^itvashravaNena cha kartR^itvasiddheH apUrNashaktitvApUrNakAmatvahetubhyAM "kartR^itvaM kAraNatvaM cha' iti shrutyA cha tasya pAratantyasiddhayA dAruyoShAvadIshAdhInacheShyakatvarUpaparatantrakartR^itvAN^gIkAreNa prAguktashrutismR^itivirodhAbhAvAt.h anvayavyatirekAbhyAM parAdhInakartR^itvashaktikatvasyaiva vidhiniShedhayogyatve tantratvakalpanena vidhiniShedhashAstravaiyarthyAt.h kartA jIva iti || 17 ||  N.M-6

|| OM chakShurAdivattu tatsahashiShyayAdibhyaH OM || 7 || 

|| OM akaraNatvAchcha na doShastathA hi darshayati OM || 

prAguktaprANasya janiriha pUrvapakShe svAtantAdAkShipyata iti saN^gatiH | atra mukhyaprANaH kiM svatantraH paratantro veti sandehaH | svatantra iti prAptam.h | "na prANaH kiJNchidAshritaH' (Agniveshya) iti shruteH | "yadAshrayAdasya cheShyAH' (mahAbhArata) ityAdismR^ityuktyA akhilajagachcheShyakamAhAtmyavattvena ananyAshrayatvayuktyupetatvena asyAH "prANaHparavashe sthitaH' (paiN^gishrutiH) iti pAratantyashrutitaH prAbalyAchcha | svAtantyashrutiyuktivirodhAdeva prAguktajanmashrutInAmaprAmANyAt.h | "sthUlatvenodeti' (gaupavana)shruteshcha lIlAvigrahagrahaNaparatvenopapattencha prAguktayukteH janirayukteti | siddhAntastu | mukhyaprANaH paratantraH "sarvaM hyevaitatparameva tiShThate prANashcha prANashcha' iti chakShurAdiprANaiH saha tadvadeva tasyeshavashatva(gaupavana)shruteH | asyAshcha "yato naiveshvaradvayam.h' iti vachanokteshvaradvayAyogarUpayuktisadhrIchInatvena prAbalyAt.h | "prANasyaitadvashe sarvaM prANaH paravashe sthitaH' (paiN^gishrutiH) iti cha svAtantrashrutiyuktyostu avAntareshvaratvena "tasyeshvaravacho bhaved.h' ityAdi tadananyeshvaratvAvAntareshvaratvaparatvAt.h | chakShurAdisAmyeshvarashabdoktAdapi suShuptau jIvaprayatnAbhAve chakShurAdInAM mukhyaprANasya vyApAradR^iShyidR^iShyibhyAM kartR^iprayojyatvAprayojyatvadR^iShyayA "tAni ha vA etAni sarvANi karaNAni' (mANDavyashruti) ityAdi shrutyA cha karaNAkaraNatvAkhyavailakShaNyAtishayena avAntareshvaratvasyopapatteshcheti "so.adhyakShaH' (bra.sU.4-2-4) ityato gatatvamasya tatraiva vakShyate | 

|| OM paJNchavR^ittirmanovadvayapadishyate OM || 8 || 

mukhyaprANaprasaN^gasannidhApitAH prANAdayo.atra chintyata iti saN^gatiH | prANAdayaH paJNcha mukhyAdAsatvena svarUpatvena vA nirNetuM shakyate na veti sandehe neti prAptam.h | "sarve vA ete mukhyadAsAH' iti dAsatvashruteH | "eSha prANaH itarAnprANAn.h pR^ithakpR^ithageva sannidhatte' (ShaT.hprashna 3-3) ityAdishrutyA "prANApAnAdayassarve' ityAdi smR^ityA choktayA tadAj~nayA kamarkAritvAditi yuktyupetatvena prAbalyAt.h | mukhyasyaiva svarUpANi prANAdyAH' (gaupavana) iti svarUpatvashruterapi svarUpatvasAdhakavyaktasadguNatvayuktyupetatvena prAbalyAt.h | shrUyate cha "pAyUpasthe.apAnaM chakShuHshrotre mukhanAsikAbhyAM prANaH svayaM pratiShThate' (Sha.pra.3-4) ityAdau vyaktasadguNatvaM teShAm.h | na hyetaddAseShu yuktaM svAmibhR^ityabhAvAyogAt.h | vastuni vikalpAyogena shrutyorviruddhArthatvenAprAmANyAditi | siddhAntastu | "atha paJNchavR^ittyaitatpravartate' ityAdishrutau manodR^iShyAntena paJNchadAsatvena paJNchasvarUpatvena mukhyaprANasyoktyA pR^ithagubhayavidhAN^gIkAreNa shrutyoryuktiyuktyoravirodhenApramANyAbhAvAt.h | "itarAn.h prANAn.h' iti dAsAnupakramyoktavyaktasadguNatvasya cha "asheShaguNapUrNAni mukhyarUpANi paJNcha cha | taddAsAH paJNcha chAnye.api prANAdyAH sadguNaiyarutAH' iti shrutyA svarUpataddAsAnAM tAratamyenopapattyA svAmibhR^ityabhAvAvirodhAt.h | itarAn.h prANAniti dAsAnupakramya pAyUpasthepAnamityAdinoktaM vyaktasadguNatvaM dAsAnAmapi kiJNchidyuktamiti prANAdayo dvedhA nirNetuM shakyanta eveti || 9 ||

|| OM aNushcha OM || 9 ||

prAguktaprANAdiprerakatvAdhikasadguNatvAya prANasya vibhutvamapyastviti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | prANo vyApto.aNurveti sandehe vyApta iti prAptam.h | "prANA evAdhastAt.h' ityAdi vyAptatvashrutyA "yatassarvaM jagadvayApya tiShThati' (vAyuprokta) ityAdi smR^ityuktasarvajagadvayApakatvayuktiyuktyA "prANovANuH' (sautrAyaNa) iti aNutvashrutitaH prabalayA vyAptatvokteH | nachaivaM vaiShNavatvena sAvakAshA | mahAn.h vai mukhyaprANaH yena vyAptaM charAcharam.h' ityAdi shrutyantare spaShyaM mukhyaprANya vyAptatvapratIteshcheti | siddhAntastu | "eSha prANo.aNurmahAnnAma' (kauNDiNya) ityAdishrutyA dehAntarbahivarrtamAnaprANavAyushabditabhedena aNutvamahatvayorvyavasthokteH | "aNurvai mukhyaprANaH yadutkrAmati naDIbhiH' iti aNutvashrutirapi nADIsaJNchAritvayuktiyuktatvena balavatvAditi || 9 || 

|| OM jyotirAdyadhiShThAnaM tu tadAmananAt.h OM || 10 || 

|| OM prANavatA shabdAt.h OM || OM tasya cha nityatvAt.h OM || 

prANAn.h mukhyaprANaM cha nirUpya iha teShAM kaM prati karaNatvamiti chintyata iti saN^gatiH | chakShurAdIndriyANi kiM jIvakaraNAni uta brahmakaraNAnIti vishaye jIvakaraNAnIti prAptam.h | "jIvasya karaNAnyAhuH prANAn.h' (sautrAyaNa) iti shrutyA jIvavashatvenAnubhUyamAnatvayuktiyuktatvena brahmaNo vA etAni karaNAnIti brahmakaraNatvashrutitaH prAbalyAt.h jIvakaraNatvokteriti | siddhAntastu | "yashchakShuShi tiShThan.h' (bR^i.5-7-18) ityAdishrutyA chakShurAdIndriyasya brahmAdhiShThAnatvoktyA tathA "yastejasi tiShThan.h' ityAdinA tejaHprabhR^itibhUtaprerakatvoktyA tadaMshabhUtachakShurAderapi brahmaprayojyatvamiti yuktibalAt.h tathA "yaH prANe tiShThan.h' ityAdishruteH sarvendriyaprerakaprANaprerakatvayuktibalAchcha brahmakAraNAnyevendriyANi mukhyasyeshaprayojyatve.api "na jIvApekShayA mukhyam.h' iti (vArAha) smR^iteH jIvaM prati karaNatvaM yuktam.h | indriyANAM jIvakaraNatvashrutistu "eShahyanenAtmanA chakShuShA darshayati' (bhAllaveya) ityAdi shrutau "karaNaiH kAraNaM brahma' (vArAha) iti smR^itau cha brahmaNaH svakAraNenaiva chakShurAdinA jIvaM prati darshanAdikArayatItyuktyA chaitrIyakuThArasya maitrakaraNatvoktiriva jIvaM prati kriyAsAdhanatvamAtrAbhiprAyA | "karaNairvAva na viyujyate' (gaupavana) iti shrutyA jIvakaraNasambandhasyAnAdinityatvAt.h chaitrIyakuThAre bahukAlasambandhini maitrIyatvoktirivopachAreNa jIvakaraNatvAbhiprAyo vA | jIvavashatvAnubhavo.api AbhimAnikatayA yukta iti || 10 ||

|| OM ta indriyANi tadvayapadeshAdanyatra shreShThAt.h OM || 11 ||

|| OM bhedashruteH OM || OM vailakShaNyAchcha OM || 

pUrvoktamukhyaprANasya jIvaM pratyakaraNatvamayuktam.h | tasyApIndriyatvena taM pratikaraNtavAt.h iti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | prAk.h prakR^itamindriyatvaM kiM sarveShAM prANAnAmutA prANAdanyeShAM dvAdashAnAmiti sandehaH | sarveShAmiti pUrvaH pakShaH | "prANA vA indriyANi' (pautrAyaNashruti) iti sAmAnyataH sarveShAmindriyatvashruteH | tasyAH sAmAnyatve.api idaMdravaNarUpayuktyupetatvena "dvAdashaivendriyANyAhuH' (kAShAyaNa) iti visheShashrutito.api balavattvAt.h | dvAdashAnAmevendriyAdhyavasAyasya duShkaratvAchcha | nahi teShAM trayodashasu anyatamasyendriyatvanivAraNaM shakyam.h | sarveShAmapIshavashatvAvisheShAditi | siddhAntastu | mukhyaprANaM R^ite dvAdashAnAmevendriyatvam.h | "dvAdashaivendriyANyAhuH prANo mukhyastvanindriyam.h' (pautrAyaNashruti) ityAdivisheShashruteH | idaMdravaNarUpayuktyupetasAmAnyashrutestu mukhyaprANetaraviShayatvasambhavAt.h | nacha prANasya chakShurAdyavisheShaH | tasya idaM dravaNayuktasarvaprANaniyantR^itvena sarvakartR^ikArayitR^itvena cha IshvarasAmyasya chakShurAdInAM tadabhAvasya "dravatAM hIndriyANAM tu' (pautrAyaNashruti) iti "sthita eva hIdaM mukhyaH prANaH karoti kArayati' (pautrAyaNashruti) ityAdishrutisiddhatvAt.h | tasyetaraprANavadIshavashatve.api itaraprANAnAmiva jIvaprayatnApekShayA IshavashatvAbhAvena vailakShaNyAchcheti || 11 ||

|| OM saMj~nAmUrtiklR^iptistu trivR^itkurvata upadeshAt.h OM || 12 ||

mukhyaprANachintanAnantaraM viriJNchaviShayachintA kriyate tasyaiva viriJNchatvAditi saN^gatiH | prAk.hchintitaprANAnAM AshrayatvAt.h (AyatanatvAt.h) prasaN^gasannidhApitaM sharIraM tadAdivastujAtaM kiM viriJNchasR^iShyaM uta paramAtmasR^iShyamiti sandehaH | "yasmAdvirechayetsarvaM viriJNchastena bhaNyate' (brAhma) iti smR^ityuktyA virechakatvAparaparyAyasraShyR^itvarUpaviriJNchatvayuktiyuktAyAH "viriJNcho vA idaM sarvaM virechayati' (gaupavana) iti shruteH "paramAddhayete nAmarUpe vyAkriyete' (Agniveshya) iti shrutito balavatvAt.h | mukhyArthasambhave viyatpAdIyanyAyena dvarasraShyR^iparatvakalpanAyogAt.h viriJNchasR^iShyamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | siddhAntastu | sharIrAdivastusR^iShyeH pR^ithivyAdibhUtatrayamishrIbhAvarUpatrivR^itkaraNasApekShatvAt.h tasya "seyaM devatemAstisro devatA' (ChAM.6-3-3) ityAdishrutyA viShNudharmatvAt.h viShNunaiva dehAdinAmaprapaJNchasR^iShyiH na viriJNchataH | prAguktayuktyupetashrutistu "brahmAdyAstadavAntarAH' (pAdma) iti smR^ityA avAntarasR^iShyipareti || 12 || 

|| OM mAMsAdibhaumaM yathAshabdamitarayoshcha OM || 13 || 

|| OM vaisheShyAttu tadvAdastadvAdaH OM || 

pUrvaM dehAdeH kartoktaH | iha tu upAdAnamuchyata iti saN^gatiH | mUrtipadena prakR^ito dehaH kiM ApyaH kiM vA pArthivaH uta taijasaH bhUtatrayAtmako veti sandehaH | mAMsAdau tR^iptijanakatvadR^iShyeH tarpakatvayuktyupetayA ApaH sharIramiti shrutyA Apa ityekaH pUrvaH pakShaH | kAThiNyagandhAdiyuktyupetayA "pR^ithivIM sharIram.h' (apyeti) iti shrutyA (bR^i.5-2-13) pArthiva ityanyaH | auShNyadarshanayuktyupetA "so.agnerdevayonyA AhutibhyaH sambhUya hiraNyasharIraH' (ai.7-4) ityAdishrutayA taijasa ityaparaH | "imAstisro devatAH puruShaM prApya' (ChAM.6-4-7) ityAdau shruto.api bhUtatrayAtmakatvapakShaH Apa eva sharIramityAdivishiShyoktyanupapatterayukta eveti | siddhAntastu | dehasyAnekabhUtaprakR^itikatve.api tattadbhUtavisheShasaMyogApekShayA vishiShyoktyupapatteH | "yatkaThiNaM sA pR^ithivI taddravaM tadApaH yaduShNaM tattejaH' (garbha.3) iti shruteranekabhUtopAdAnaka eva deha iti || 13 || 

|| iti shrIrAghavendrayatikR^itAyAM nyAyamuktAvalyAM dvitIyAdhyAyasya chaturthaH pAdaH || 

|| dvitIyAdhyAyaH samAptaH || 

|| atha tR^itIyo.adhyAyaH ||

evaM samanvayAvirodhAbhyAM jij~nAsAsUtrasthabrahmashabdArthaH siddharUpaH nirUpitaH pUvarAdhyAye | tatsthAvashiShyAtojij~nAsApadAnAmarthaH sAdhyarUpo nirUpyate anantarAdhyAyadvaye iti pUrvottarAdhyAyadvikadvayasya siddhasAdhyavichArarUpatvAt.h paurvAparyam.h | tatrApyataHpadoktaphalaM prati athajij~nAsApadAbhyAM uktavairAgyabhaktyupAsanAparokShaj~nAnAnAM hetutvena tR^itIye.atrAdhyAye sAdhanavichAra ityadhyAyasaN^gatiH | pAdAnAmapyuttarottaraM prati pUrvapUrvasya hetutvAt.h kramo dhyeyaH |
