|| OM tadantarapratipattau raMhati sampariShvaktaH prashnanirUpaNAbhyAm.h OM || 1 || 

pUrvatra chandrikAkArairuktA chintAparamparA | ato noktA mayA sA.atra tUchyate sanmude sphuTam.h | atha jij~nAsAsUtrasthAthAdipadoktavairAgyAdimokShasAdhanamananuShTheyamutAnuShTheyamiti chintA | tadarthaM jIvasya mR^itau niHsheShabhUtaviyogo.asita uta neti | tadarthaM bhUtAviyoge pramANaprayojane nasta uta sta iti | yadyAdyaH pakShaH tarhi niHsheShabhUtaviyogasyaiva mokShatayA svAbhAvikamR^ityaiva anAyAsena mokShasiddheH nAnuShTheyaM sAdhanamiti | yadyantastadA bhUtaviyogasyaiva muktitve.api mR^itau tadabhAvAt.h anuShTheyameva mokShArthaM sAdhanamiti phalaphalIbhAvaH | pUrvapakShastu | nAnuShTheyaM sAdhanam.h | tena vinApi "bhUtAnAM vinivR^ittistu maraNam.h' (bhArata) iti smR^ityA sarvabhUtavinivR^ittirUpamaraNenaiva "muktistebhyo vimochanam.h' (vArAha) iti smR^ityA bhUtavimochanarUpamokShasiddheH | nacha bhUtAnAM mR^itajIvena saha gamane pramANamasti sharIrabhogAn.h pradAya charitArthAnAM prayojanaM nAstIti | siddhAntastu | "vettha yathA paJNchamyAmAhutAvApaH puruShavachaso bhavanti' (ChAM. 5-3-9) iti prashnaprativachanayoH abupalakShitajIvasyoktibalAt.h "bhUtayuktaH paraM lokamimaM lokaM cha gachChati' ityAdipramANabalAt.h sharIrAntasampAdanArthatayA prayojanavattvAt.h bhUtAnAM jIvena saha gatyavagamena mR^itau niHsheShabhUtaviyogAbhAvAt.h "bhUtAnAM vinivR^ittiH' sati smR^iteH "mR^itikAle jahAtyenam.h' (brahmANDa) iti smR^ityA bhAgaviShayatvAttadrUpamokShArthaM anuShTheyameva sAdhanamiti | phale tu jij~nAsAsUtroktasAdhanAkShepasamAdhI || 1 || 

|| OM tyAtmakatvAttu bhUyastvAt.h OM || 2 ||

pUrvoktaprashnAdibalAt.h ekAbAkhyabhUtagatisiddhAvapi ekasya dehAnArambhakatayA.aprayojakatvAt.h mR^itireva muktiriti kiM sAdhanAnuShThAneneti AkShepAtsaN^gatiH | mR^itaM jIvaM pariShvajya kiM Apa eva gachChanti uta sarvANi bhUtAnIti chintA | tadarthaM prashnAdisthApUshabdaH kimekabhUtaparaH utAnekapara iti | tadarthamanekabhUtaparatve heturnAsti Ap.hshabdashcha na yuktaH uta viparIta iti | pUrvapakShastu | ApaH puruShavachasa iti prashnAdau ap.h shabdenApAmeva gatishravaNAt.h ap.h shabdasyAnekabhUtaparatve hetvabhAvena "bhUtAni puruShavachAMsi bhavanti' iti nirdeshApattyA cha vishiShyAp.hshabdashravaNAyogAt.h Apa eva gachChanti netarabhUtAnIti | siddhAntastu | mishrANi hi bhUtAnItyAdi shrutyA bhUtAnAM mishratvena shrutau tyAtmakAp.hshabdenaiva bhUtAni puruShavachAMsItyarthalAbhAt.h sarvabhUtAnAM mishratve.api shrutAp.hshabdasya pArthivAdisarvadeheShu sambhUyApAmeva bhUtejopekShayA bhUyastvena vaisheShyAttadvAda iti uktanyAyenopapatteH sarvANi bhUtAnyapi gachChantIti | phalaM tu sAdhanAnuShThAnAkShepasamAdhI eveti || 2 || 

|| OM prANagateshcha OM || 3 || 

pUrvatra tyAtmakApAM gatyuktyA arthAtsiddhA bhUtAnAM gatiH iha vishiShyAnumAnarUpamAnena sAdhyata iti saN^gatiH | athAdipadoktaM vairAgyAdisAdhanaM anAvashyakaM utAvashyakamiti chintA | tadarthaM prakR^itabhUtAni jIvena saha na gachChanti uta gachChantIti | tadarthaM vishiShya mAnaM nAsti utAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | pUrvoktadishA tyAtmakApAM gatyarthAt.h bhUtagatiriti nirNayasya 
visheShamAnAdhInatvAt.h tasya chehAnupalambhAt.h na gachChantIti nAvashyakaM sAdhanamiti | siddhAntastu | bhUtAni jIvena saha gachChantyeva sahagantR^ipANAvinAbhUtatvAt.h | yadyatsahagantravinAbhUtaM tattatsahagantR^i yathA rAjasahagantramAtayAvinAbhUtaM vastu rAjasahagantraM ityanumAnarUpavisheShapramANasadbhAvAt.h bhUtAni jIvena saha gatimantyeva kAraNairvAva na viyujyata iti shrutyA hetau visheShaNasya "yatra vAva bhUtAni tatra karaNAni' (bhAllaveya) iti shrutau "na chaitAni kadAchidviyujyante' ityuktyA visheShasiddheH AvashyakaM sAdhanamiti || 3 ||

|| OM agnyAdigatishruteriti chenna bhAktatvAt.h OM || 4 || 

prAguktahetorasiddhirnirasyate.atreti saN^gatiH | athAdipadoktaM sAdhanaM nAnuShTheyamutAnuShTheyamiti chintA | tadarthaM prakR^itAH prANAH kiM jIvena saha na gachChantyuta gachChantIti | tadarthaM prANAnAM agnyAdigatishrutiH kiM savarAtmanA prANagatiparA atha bhAgashaH tadgatipareti | tadarthaM bhAgaparatve kalpakaM nAsti bAdhakaM chAsti uta viparItamiti | pUrvapakShastu | "yatrAsya puruShasya mR^itasyAgniM vAgapyeti vAtaM prANashchakShurAdityam.h' ityAdinA vAgAdiprANAnAmagnyAdyadhidaivaM prati gatishravaNena jIvena sahagatyAbhAvAt.h | bhAgasho jIvena saha gachChantIti bhAgAntareNAdhidaivamityasya cha kalpakAbhAvena pratimaraNameva bhAgApagame kAlataH sarvApagamApAtena cha prANAnAmadhidaivagatau bhUtAnAmapi taissaha tatra gatau jIvena saha gatyabhAvena jIvena saha gatau tatra gatyabhAva iti sarvathA.api bhUtAnAM prANavinAbhAvAbhAvApAtena chAyogAt.h | na prANAH jIvena saha gantAraH iti nAnuShTheyaM sAdhanamiti | siddhAntastu | "puruShasya mR^itau brahman.h' (brAhma) iti smR^itau prANAnAM bhAgasha eva ubhayatra gamanasya "mR^itikAle jahAtyenam.h' (brahmANDa) iti smR^itisiddhatvena bhUtAnAM prANavinAbhAvAbhAvAt.h | prANA bhUtAni cha jIvena saha gachChantyevetyanuShTheyaM sAdhanamiti || 4 || 

|| OM prathame.ashravaNAditi chenna tA eva hyupapatteH OM || 5 || 

pUrvatrAgnyAdishruteH bhAktatvoktiprasaN^gAdatra shraddhAshruteH bhAktatvoktiriti saN^gatiH | athAdipadoktaM sAdhanaM nAnuShTheyamutAnuShTheyamiti chintA | tadarthaM bhUtAnAM jIvena saha gatirnAsti utAstIti tadarthaM tasminnetasminnagnau devAH shraddhAM juhvatIti upakrame shrutashraddhAshabdaH kiM shraddhAmAtrayuktaparaH uta shraddhayAdbhishcha yuktajIvaparaH itisa| tadarthaM kiM upakramAnurodhena "iti paJNchamyAmAhutAvApaH puruShavachasaH' (ChAM.5-9-1) ityupasaMhAro neya uta viparIta iti | tadarthaM kimupakramaH prabala uta upasaMhAra iti | Adye upakramasya yathAshrutArthatayA tadanurodhena upasaMhArasya neyatvena bhUtagatau prashnottarasyAmAnatvAt.h bhUtAnAM na sahagatiriti nAnuShTheyaM sAdhanamiti pUrvapakShe phalam.h | antye tu upasaMhArasya tyAtmakAp.hshabdAnurodhena upakramasthashraddhAshabdasya neyatvena prashnottarabalena bhUtAnAM sahagatirityanuShTheyaM sAdhanamiti siddhAnte phalam.h | pUrvapakShastu | na bhUtAnAM jIvena saha gatiH | "tasminnetasmin.h' (ChAM.5-4-3) iti shrutau upakrAntasya shraddhayeShyavataH shraddhAsahitasyaiva dvayAkhye prathamAgnau ChAndogye paJNchame homashravaNena bhUtagaterashravaNAt.h anyathA bhUtAnItyuktiprasaN^gAt.h | na chopasaMhArasthAp.hshabdavirodhena shraddhAshabdaH tatpara iti yuktam.h | asaMjAtavirodhitvena prathamopasthitatvena cha upakramasya prAbalyAt.h tadanurodhenaivopasaMhArasya neyatvAditi | siddhAntastu | upasaMhArasyAprAthamyepi upakramavyAkhyAnarUpatayA arthAnusandhAnataH prAthamyena prAbalyAttadanurodhenaivopakramasya vyAkhyeyatayA tatsthashraddhAshabdasya ajahallakShaNayA shraddhayA tyAtmakAdbhishcha yuktajIvaparatvopapatteH asti bhUtAnAM saha gatiriti | atra navInoktaprathamaprAbalyakhaNDanenopasaMhAraprAbalyavyutpAdanaprapaJNchanaM tu gurupAdakR^itopasaMhAravijayAdavaseyam.h || 5 || N.M-7
|| OM ashrutatvAditi chenneShyAdikAriNAM pratIteH OM || 6 ||

evamatItanayanirNItAp.hshrutiprANagatirUpamAnadvayAkShepeNa iha shaN^kotthAnAdantarasaN^gatiH | pUrvatraivAdyA chintA | tadarthaM prakR^itabhUtAni jIvena saha gachChantyuta na gachChantIti | tadarthaM prAguktArthikashravaNaprANagatirUpayuktI bhUtagatisAdhake na bhavataH uta bhavata iti | tadarthaM tAbhyAM kiM niyamena pratyakShAshravaNaM balavaduta viparItamiti | pUrvapakShastu | prashnanirUpaNayoH tyAtmakAp.hgatyuktyA artAdbhUtAnAM gatishravaNAdapi "agniM vAgapyeti' ityAdivata bhUtAni gachChantIti niyamena pratyakShAshravaNasyaiva balavattvAt.h 
prANagatirUpayukterapi visheShashravaNe satyeva vaidikArthasAdhakatvAt.h pratyakShagatishrutyabhAve tayorasAdhakatvAnna saha gachChanti bhUtAnIti nAnuShTheyaM sAdhanamiti | siddhAntastu | kadannabhojanasyApi bhojanatvavadArthikashravaNasyApi shravaNatvena yukteH prAguktadishA vyAptiliN^gagrAhakapramANavattayA balavattayA shravaNasAmAnyAbhAvapratibandhakatvena tayoH svayamarthasAdhakatvAt.h "atha hainaM yajamAnaM kiM na jahAti bhUtAnyeva bhUtaireva gachChati bhUtairbhu ‡•ç.hkte bhUtairutpadyate bhUtaishcharati' (kauNDiNyashrutiH) iti pratyakShashravaNAchcha | atra shrutau yajamAnapadashravaNe.api karmakR^ito.api bhUtAviyogena tadanyeShAM kaimutyasiddhatvAt.h | bhUtAni jIvena saha gachChantyevetyanuShTheyaM sAdhanamiti || 6 ||

|| OM bhAktaM vA.anAtmavittvAttathAhi darshayati OM || 7 ||

pUrvatra kaimutyena sarvajIvAnAM bhUtAviyogoktirayuktA | karmakR^ito muktishravaNena tasyaiva bhUtAviyogAbhAve kaimutyAnavatArAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atrAthAdipadenoktaM vairAgyAdimokShasAdhanaM mumukShuNA na kAryamuta kAryamiti chintA | tadarthaM "apAma somamamR^itA abhUma' (R^i.8-48-3) ityAdau karmataH shrutamamR^itatvaM kiM mukhyamuta bhAktamiti | tadarthaM mukhyatve bAdhakaM nAstyutAstIti | Adye anyato.api muktilAbhAnna vairAgyAdi kAryam.h | antye tu kAryamiti phalaphalibhAvaH | pUrvapakShastu | na vairAgyAdisAdhanaM kAryaM tena vinApyapAmetyAdi shrutyA sushakena karmaNaiva muktisiddheH | nacha shrutAvamR^itatvaM gauNaM bAdhakAbhAvAditi | siddhAntastu | "tamevaM vidvAnamR^itaH' (puruShasUkta) ityAdau Atmavida eva mukhyAmR^itatvaM anyasya netyuktyA niravakAshatachChativirodharUpabAdhakena apAmetyAdishruteH gauNArthatvAvashyaMbhAvena anyato muktyabhAvAt.h kAryameva mumukShuNA vairAgyAdi tatsAdhanamiti | shrutergauNArtatvaprakArashcha "amR^ito vAva somapo bhavati yAvadindro yAvanmanuH' ityAdi shrutyA kAmyakarmavataH kiJNchitkAlInamamR^itatvaM akAmyakarmakR^ito jij~nAso.astu j~nAnadvArA mokShAkhyAmR^itatvaM "aganmajyotiravidAma devAn.h' (R^i.8-48-3) iti vAkyasheShe jyotirbrahma vyajij~nAsiShmetyukteH "utkramiShyata evaM bhAvAt.h' (bra.sU.1-4-22) ityukteshcha "sarvApekShA cha yaj~nAdishruterashvAt.h' (bra.sU.3-4-26) iti vakShyamANatvAchcha akAmyakarmiNo j~nAninastu "agnihotradi tu tatkAryAyaiva taddarshanAd.h' (bra.sU.4-1-16) ityAdai vakShyamANadishA mokShaikadeshAnandAbhivyaktivisheSharUpamamR^itatvamityevaMrUpeNa j~neyaH | phale tu athapadAdyuktavairAgyAdisAdhanAnuShThAnAkShepasamAdhI || 7 ||

|| OM kR^itAtyaye.anushayavAn.h dR^iShyasmR^itibhyAm.h OM || 8 ||

pUrvatra karmajaphalaM amR^itatvaM bhAktamityuktam.h | iha tu karmaNaH svargAdau phalajanakatvaM bhAktaM bhAgenaiva na tu kR^itsnasyetyuchyata iti saN^gatiH | atrAthAdipadoktaM vairAgyAdikaM mumukShuNA na kAryamuta kAryamiti chintA | tadarthaM bandhakIbhUtakarmaNaH svargAdau niHsheShabhogo.arthaikadesheneti | tadarthaM karmaNo bhAgasho bhogakalpakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | "karmaNA badhyate jantuH' ityAdeH bandhakIbhUtakAmyakarmaNo jIvena sahaiva svargAdAvagatasya bhAgena bhogakalpane mAnAbhAvena niHsheShabhogasambhavAdbhogena kamar bhuktvA tachCheSheNa svargAtpunarAgamanAN^gIkAre.api evaM dvityAvartanena niHsheShakarmasamAptisambhavAchcha | bandhabIjAbhAve bandhasya svata eva nivR^itteH na kAryaM mumukShuNA vairAgyasAdhanamiti | siddhAntastu | "tataH sheSheNemaM lokamAyAti' iti shrutau "bhuktasheShAnushayavAn.h' iti smR^itau cha svargagatasya yathAyogyaM karma sahAgatamapi kiMchidbhuktavataH karmasheShayutavata evAgamanasya punaH karmakaraNasya "dashAvarANAm.h' ityanalpakarmakR^iteshchoktyA bhogena niHsheShakarmakShayAbhAt.h kAryameva vairAgyAdIti || 8 ||

|| OM yathetamanevaM cha OM || 9 ||

pUrvamanushayavAnyAtItyukte kiM yathAgataM tathaivAyAti mArgAntareNa vetyAkAN^kShAtra nivartyata iti saN^gatiH | atAdipadoktaM vairAgyaM na kAryamutakAryamiti chintA | tadarthaM gatiprakAreNaivAgamanamanyathA veti | tadarthaM mArgashravaNamAgamanopayogi utAnupayogIti | Adye buddhisthagatamArgeNaivAgamanAt.h Agatau kleshAbhAvAt.h taddhetukarmaNi vairAgyaM na | antye tu anyathApyAgamanena 
aparichitamArgakR^itakleshabhAvAt.h taddhetuvairAgyamAvashyakamiti phalaphalibhAvaH | pUrvapakShastu | parichitamArgatyAgena aparichitamArgeNAgatau hetvabhAvAt.h "yathetamAgachChati' iti shrutivirodhAchcha gatimArgeNaivAgamanamiti na kAryaM vairAgyAdIti | siddhAntastu | gamane jIvasyAsvAtanteNa tatsmaraNasyAgamanAnupayogAt.h "dhUmAdabhram.h' iti bhAShyokta(kAShAyaNa) shrutau AkAshaparyantameva gatimArgeNAgamanaM tato.arvAganyathAtvasyoktatvAdyathetamiti shruteshcha kiMchidgatiprakAreNAgateraN^gIkAreNa tadviShayatvopapatteH | gamanaprakArAdanyathApyAgamanamiti kAryaM vairAgyAdati || 9 || 

|| OM charaNAditi chenna tadupalINArtheti kArShNAjiniH OM || 10 ||

|| OM Anarthakyamiti chenna tadapekShatvAt.h OM || OM sukR^itaduShkR^ite eveti tu bAdariH OM || 

evaM gatyAgatimArgasthitau siddhAyAM tatsAdhananirNayo.atra kriyata iti saN^gatiH | athAdipadoktaM kAmyakarmaNi vairAgyaM nAvashyakamutAvashyakamiti chintA | tadarthaM kiM gatAgataM charaNaphalamuta kAmyakarmaphalamiti | tadarthaM "tadya iha ramaNIyacharaNAH ramaNIyAM yonimApadyante' (ChAM.5-10-7) iti shrutau charaNashabdaH kiM karmAN^gAchAraparaH kiMvA karmaparaH iti | pUrvapakShastu | charaNaphalameva gatAgataM na karmaphalam.h | charaNashrutau gatAgatasya charaNaphalatvokteH | na charaNameva karma | "sa yathAkArI yathAchArI' iti shrutau "AchAra iti samproktaH karmAN^gatvena shuddhidaH' iti smR^itau cha tasyAnarthakyaprasaN^gAt.h | yaj~nAdikAriNAM prakR^itatvena ye yaj~nAdikAriNo ramaNIyAM ityAdirUpeNokitasambhave vinApi charaNashabdaM karmopalakShaNasambhavAt.h | nacha "ya ime grAma iShyApUrte dattamityupAsane te dhUmamabhisambhavanti' (ChAM.5-10-3) ityAdau gatAgatasya yaj~nAdiphalatvoktivirodhaH iti vAchyam.h | tatrApyupAsata ityupashabdena samIpavR^ittivAchinA karmasamIpavR^itticharaNasya gR^ihIteriti | siddhAntastu | bhavatyeva puNyapApAkhyakarmaphalaM gatAgatam.h | "iShyApUrtaM manyamAnAvariShThaM nAnyachChreyo vedayante pramUDhAH' (muM.1-2-10) iti shrutau "traividyA mAM somapAH pUtapApAH' (bha.gI.9-20) ityAdismR^itau cha gatyAdeH karmaphalatvapratItestadbalena charaNashruteH ajahallakShaNayA yaj~nAdyarthatve.api ramaNIyAdyAchAreNaiva yaj~nakR^itAM ramaNIyatvAdikamiti sUchakatayA charaNashabdasya sArthakyasambhavAt.h | dharmaM kurutetyarthe "dharmaM charataH' iti prayogabalena charaNashruteH yaj~nAdiparatvAdeva "ya ime grAmaH' (ChAM.5-10-3) iti shruterarthAntarakalpanamapramANakam.h | "atha ye yaj~nena dAnena tapasA lokAn.h jayanti te dhUmamabhisaMvishanti' iti samAkhyAviruddhaM cheti kAmyakarmaNi kAryaM vairAgyAdIti || 10 ||

|| OM aniShyAdikAriNAmapi cha shrutam.h OM || 11 ||

|| OM saMyamenetvanubhUyetareShAmArohAvarohau tadgatidarshanAt.h OM || OM smaranti cha OM || 

astyevamuktadishA gatyAdeH puNyAkhyakarmaphalatvaM na tu pApAkhyakarmaphalatvamiti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaM vairAgyaM kiM kAmyapuNyakarmaNyeva uta pApAdAvapIti chintA | tadatharM puNyapApAkhyakarmaphalatayA prakR^itamArgagamanAdiduHkhaM kiM puNyakR^itAmeva uta apuNyakR^itAmapIti | tadarthaM gatAgataM kiM pratyavAyabhayaphalakAmanAdiprayuktamuta karmaprayuktameveti | tadarthaM bhayAdihInAnAmapi apuNyakR^itAM gatyAdau mAnaM nAstyutAstIti | Adye puNyakR^itAmeva pratyavAyabhayAdimatAM gattyAdi | antye tu puNyakR^itAmapuNyakR^itAmubhayeShAmapIti phalam.h | pUrvapakShastu | puNyakR^itAmevagamanAdiduHkhaM natvapuNyakR^itAM teShAM pratyavAyabhayavattvAt.h | bibhyatpatati pAdapAditi nyAyena bhayavata eva patanavattvAdiduHkhitvopalambhAt.h phalakAmanAvattvAchcha | kAmyapuNyakR^itAmeva gamanAdi | "kAmAnyaH kAmayate manyamAnaH sa kAmabhirjAyate tatra tatra' iti shrutau kAmina eva punarAgamanokteH | aniShyAdikR^itAM cha bhayAbhAvAtkAmanAbhAvAchcha na punarAgatyAdi duHkham.h | nacha bhayAdimattvaM patanAdiduHkhAprayojakaM kintu karmaiveti vAchyaM kalpakAbhAvAt.h | kiMcha puNyakR^itAmiva puNyamakurvatA pApaM cha kuvartAM tAtkAlikakAmoparodhAdirUpakleshAbhAvena srak.hchandanavanitAdibhogAdhikyena cha bhAvipunarAgamanAdimAtrakleshasyAkiJNchitkaratvAt.h na kAryaM tatra vairAgyAdIti | siddhAntastu | "tadya iha shubhakR^ito ye chAshubhakR^itaste shubhamanubhUyAvartanta' (bhAllaveya) iti shrutau puNyakR^itAmivAnyeShAmapyAgateruktatvAt.h | tathA 
"sarve vA ete.ashubhakR^itaH saMyamane prapatanti' (kauNTharavya) iti bhAShyoktashrutau "gachChanti pApinaH' ityAdi smR^itiShu cha puNyakR^idanyeShAM nityanarakAdimahAnarthasya chokteshcha bhagavadaj~nAninAM sarveShAmapyastyevAgamanAdiduHkhaM bhavayattvAbhAvAdihetudvayaM chAprayojakam.h | abibhyatA phalakAmanAshUnyenApi upabhuktaviShasya tanmR^itihetutAdR^iShyeH kAryaM tatrAtishayena vairAgyamiti || 11 || 

|| OM api sapta OM || 12 || 

pUrvatra haridveShiNo nityanarakoktirayuktA | "yAvadindrashchaturdasha' iti tadanityatvokterityAkShepAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaM bhagavaddveShAdAvatishayitavairAgyamanAvashyakaM utAvashyakamiti chintA | tadarthaM pUrvaM tatphalatvenokto narakaH kiM punarAvR^ittimAnuta neti | tadarthaM narakaH kimeka evotAneka iti | pUrvapakShastu | narakabhede mAnAbhAvAdekasya yAvadindrAshchaturdashetyAdAvanityatvokteH punarAvR^ittimAneva bhagavaddveShinarakaH | na cha "mahAtamasimagnAnAM na teShAmutthitiH kvachit.h' iti smR^ityA nityatvasyApyavagamena puruShabhedenaikasyaiva narakasya nityatvamanityatvaM chAstviti vAchyam.h | "chakAra narakaM shUnyam.h' ityAdevirrodhAt.h | ato na bhagavaddveShe.atishayena vairAgyamAvashyakamiti | siddhAntastu | "rauravo.atha mahAMshchaiva' (bhArata) iti bhAShyoktasmR^itau anityanarakaprapaJNchasya nityanarakadvayasya cha prAdhAnyenokteH | yAvadindrAshchaturdashetyAderanityanarakaviShayatvopapatteH | bhagavaddveShinarakaH punarAvR^ittishUnya eveti bhAvyaM tatrAtishayitavairAgyeNeti || 12 || 

|| OM tatrApi cha tadvayapArAdavirodhaH OM || 13 ||

astvaniShyAdikAriNoH dvividhAdhikAriNoH nityAnityanarakabhogaH | tAvatA na taddhetau vairAgyamAvashyakam.h | tasya duHkhasvarUpatvAbhAvAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaM pApAdau vairAgyaM na kAryamuta kAryamiti chintA | tadatharM tatphalarUpo narakaH kimaduHkharUpo.atha duHkharUpa iti | tadarthaM narakasya saduHkhatve tatprerakeshvarasya duHkhabhogaH prasajyata uta neti | tadarthaM kiM bhogo nAma duHkhasAkShAtkAramAtramuta tatkR^itanIchatvAdireveti | pUrvapakShastu | duHkhAparokShasyaiva tadbhogarUpatvAnnArakiNo duHkhitve tatprerakasya sarvaj~neshvarasya duHkhasAkShitvarUpaduHkhabhogaprasaN^gAt.h narako na duHkharUpaH | na cheshvaro na tatprerakaH sarvaM prerayatIti bhAShyoktashrutivirodhAt.h | ato na vairAgyaM kAryamiti | siddhAntastu | "nIchochchataiva duHkhAderbhoga ityabhidhIyate' iti (bhAgavatatantra) smR^ityA nIchatvAdereva bhogashabdArthatvAttasyaiva cha duHkhiprerakatve.api nirvikAre achintyashaktau harAvabhAvasya "nAsau duHkhabhuk.h' iti shrutismR^itisiddhatvena nArakiNAM duHkhitve bAdhakAbhAvAt.h saduHkho naraka iti bhAvyaM tatra vairAgyeNeti || 13 || 

|| OM vidyAkarmaNoriti tu prakR^itatvAt.h OM || 14 || 

vairAgyArthaM narakAdeH saduHkhoktirayuktA | tena vinApi tatphale gatyAdau jIvAnAM svAtanteNechChayA tatphalagatyAdityAgopAdAnasambhavAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaM kAmyakarmaNi vairAgyaM nAvashyakamutAvashyakamiti chintA | tadarthaM jIvAnAM gatyAdau svAtantyamasti uta neti | tadarthaM "athaitayoH pathornaikatareNa cha gachChanti tAnImAni kShudramishrANi' (ChAM.5-10-8) iti shrutau etayorapi kiM devayAnapitR^iyAnarUpamArgaparAmarshaH uta vidyAkarmaNoriti | pUrvapakShastu | ChAndogye paJNchame "te.achirShamabhisambhavanti' (ChAM.5-10-1) "te dhUmamabhisambhavanti' (ChAM.5-10-3) iti pUrvaprakR^itau devayAnAdimArgau etayorityuravAkye parAmR^ishya naikatareNa gachChantItyuktyA bhUtAnAM gatau bhUtasvAtantyamavagamyate | puruShaprayatnAgochare na gachChantItyuktyayogAt.h | itaravyapadeshAdityAdau jIvAsvAtantoktAvapIshAdhInasvAtantyaM sambhavatyeva | jIvAnAM svAtante savareShAmapi gatiprAptiriti tu sAdhanasvAtante.api samam.h | adR^iShyAdinA atiprasaN^gAdivANamihApi samam.h | tathAcha gatAveva svAtantAt.h "mUle labdhe naiva shAkhAgraM gantumichChati' iti nyAyena phala eva svAtantAt.h kiM kAmyakarmavairAgyeNeti | siddhAntastu | "tadya itthaM vidurye cheme.araNye shraddhAtapa upAsate te.archiShamabhisambhavanti' "atha ya ime grAma iShyApUrte 
dattamityupAsate te dhUmam.h' iti vidyAkarmaNorapi pUrvatraprakR^itatvAddevayAnAdimArgayoH tatsAdhanavidyAkarmaNoshcha prakR^itatvAvisheShe.api "vidyApathaH karmapatho dvau panthAnau prakIrtitau | tadvarjitastridhA yAti tiryagvA narakaM tamaH' iti bhAShyoktasmR^itisamAkhyayA vidyAkarmaNorevaitayorityuttaravAkye parAmarshena sAdhana eva jIvAnAM svAtanteNa phale tadabhAvAt.h sAdhane vidhisadbhAvena vidhyAdishAstrAvaiyarthyAyaiva tatreshvaraH svAtantyaM dadAtItyabhyupagamena phale.api svAtantApAdanAprasakteH Avashyakameva kAmye vairAgyAdIti || 14 ||

|| OM na tR^itIye tathopalabdheH OM || 15 || 

|| OM smaryate.api cha loke OM || OM dasharnAchcha OM || OM tR^itIye shabdAvarodhaH saMshokajasya OM || OM smaraNAchcha OM || 

atra "tiryagvA narakaM tamaH' iti pUrvoktatamaHsvarUpachintAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaM bhagavaddveShiphale tamasyatishayena vairAgyaM na kAryamuta kAryamiti chintA | tadarthaM tamaH kimitaranarakavat.h sukhaduHkhamishramuta duHkhaikasvarUpamiti | tadarthaM kiM duHkhaM sukhAvinAbhUtamuta neti | tadarthaM yatra duHkhaM sukhaM tatreti vyAptigrAhakamAnasya tamasyapavAdakaM pramANaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | yatra duHkhaM sukhaM tatreti vyApteH sArvatrikasukhaduHkhayoratIndriyatvena apratyakShatve.api "yatra duHkhaM sukhaM tatra' iti bhAShyoktasmR^ityA grahaNasambhavena duHkhayukte tamasi itaranaraka iva sukhasyApyanumAnasiddhatvAt.h apavAdakamAnasya chAdarshanAt.h anyanarakApekShayA nAtishayena tamasi vairAgyaM vidheyamiti | siddhAntastu | shrutismR^itipratyakShAnumAnArthApattibhyaH tamaso duHkhaikayuktvAvagamAt.h yatra duHkhamiti smR^iteH tamonyanarakaviShayatvAvashyaMbhAvAdbhAvyaM tatrAshayitavairAgyeNeti | tathAhi | na tamaH sukhAnuvR^ittaM "kevalaM hyevAtra duHkham.h' iti shrutiH nAdhetamasimagnAnAM sukhalesho.api kashchana' (bhaviShyatparva) iti smR^itiH | "nArAyaNaprasAdena' (pAdma) ityAdi bhAShyoktasmR^itisiddhaM chaturmukhapratyakShaM "atipriye yathA rAjA' (brAhma) ityAdi smR^itisiddhatayA prabalam.h | vipratipanna na duHkhavantaH tathAtveneshvarAniShyatvAt.h yadyatheshvarAniShyaM tattathA na bhavati yathA shasho viShANitvenetyanumAnaM cha | na chAsiddhiH | naite sukhitvena IshvareShyAH api‡•çrayatvAt.h yo yasyApriyaH sa sukhitvena tasyAniShyaH yathA rAjavirodhI rAj~naH ityanumAnena tatsiddheH | apriyatvaM cha dveShitvAdeva siddham.h | tathA "mahAtamastridhA proktam.h' ityAdi (kaumar) smR^ityA tamasaH svarUpashravaNe shrotR^INAM shravaNajaduHkhAdhikyajanyamUrChAprAptyavagamena tadanyathAnupapattirUpArthApattishcheti || 15 || 

|| OM tatsvAbhAvyApattirupapatteH OM || 16 ||

astveva duHkhahetAvaniShyAdau tatphalecha vairAgyaM na tu kAmyakarmaNi | tatphalecha sukhahetutvAt.h sukharUpatvAchcheti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaM kAmyakarmAdau vairAgyaM na yuktamuta yuktamitichintA | tadarthaM karma mahAsukhaheturuta neti | tadarthaM karmiNaH svargAdigatau "dhUmo bhUtvAbhraM bhavati' (ChAM.5-10-5) itayAdinA shruto dhUmAdibhAvaH kiM dhUmAdidevataikyatatpadaprAptyanyatararUpaH uta sAdR^ishyAdirUpa iti | tadarthaM dhUmo bhavatItyAdisAmAnAdhikaraNyaM kiM mukhyamuta sAdR^ishyAdirUpa iti | tadarthaM dhUmo bhavatItyAdisAmAnAdhikaraNyaM kiM mukhyamuta sAdR^ishyAdinA gauNamiti | tadarthaM bAdhakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | devataikyapadaprAptyoranyatara eva dhUmAdibhAvaH | sAmAnAdhikaraNyashrutermukhyArthatyAge bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | devatAbhiH snehAdivashena tAbhireva vidyAprApyasyApi svapadasya dAtumapi shakyatvena karmirastatpadaprApterasambhAvitatvAbhAvAchcha sukhahetutvAnna karmaNi vairAgyamiti | siddhAntastu | loke.anyasyAnyabhAvAdR^iShyayApi atyantabhinnasya karmiNo detaikyasyAyogAttatpadasya cha niyatAdhikAribhiH vidyayaiva gamyatayA yugapadanekakarmisamavAye.anekeShAmekapadaprAptyanupapattyA chAsambhavAt.h sAmAnAdhikaraNyashrutermukhyArthatyAgAvashyaMbhAvena dhUmAdibhAvaprAptishcha "tadgatau gatireva tu' (gAruDa) ityAdi smR^ityuktadishA devatAsAdR^ishyaparA vA tatpraveshena sthAnaikyaparA vA neyeti mahAsukhAhetutvAdyuktaM kAmyakarmaNi tatphale cha vairAgyamiti || 16 ||

|| OM nAtichireNa visheShAt.h OM || 17 ||

pUrvatrAgatau karmiNo dhUmAdibhAvashchintitaH atra tu Agatireva kiyatkAleneti chintanAdvA karmiNo devatAsvAbhAvyApattAvapi tasyAshchirakAlInatvenApi mahAsukhavattvAnna karmaNi vairAgyamiti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atrAthapadoktaM kAmyakarmaNi vairAgyaM cha yuktamuta yuktamiti chintA | tadarthaM tatkiM mahAsukhaheturuta neti | tadarthaM Agamane kAlaklR^iptirnAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | Agamane etAvati kAla evAgantavyamiti kAlaklR^iptyabhAvena "yathetamAkAsham.h' (kAShAyaNa) ityAdinAgatau bahusthAnaprAptishravaNena cha tattaddevatAsvAbhAvyena prAptAtimahAsukhatyAgena shIghramAgamane hetvabhAvAchcha | kalpAntameva madhyermAgamavasthAne prAptasukhahetau na karmaNi vairAgyaM yuktamiti | siddhAntastu | "tadya iha ramaNIya charaNA abhyAsho ha yatte ramaNIyaM yonimApadyante' (ChAM.5-10-7) ityAdishrutau "svargAllokAdavA noti vatsarAtpUrvameva tu' (nAradIya) iti smR^itau cha Agatau kamirNaH kAlaklR^iptyavagamAt.h kl.hptyakAlAdhikAvasthAne kAraNAbhAvAt.h tasyeShyatve.api jIvasyAsvAtantAt.h | anyathA sarveShAM duHkhAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h atichireNaivAgamanamiti bhAvyaM kAmye karmaNi vairAgyeNeti || 17 ||

|| OM anyAdhiShThite pUrvavadabhilApAt.h OM || 18 || 

|| OM ashuddhamiti chenna shabdAt.h OM || 

pUvartra shrutyAdinA karmiNo.achireNAgatirityuktirayuktA tatraivAnAshvAsAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaM vairAgyaM na kAryamuta kAryamiti chintA | tadarthaM nirvedamAyAdityAdivairAgyavidhAyakashrutau AshvAso na yukta uta yukta iti | tadarthaM vedaH kvachitphalavyabhichArI uta neti | tadarthaM "ta iha vrIhiyavA' (ChAM.5-10-6) iti shrutyuktakarmirAM vrIhyAdibhAvaH kiM mukhyaH uta dhUmAdibhAvavadgauNaH iti | gauNatve.api karmiNo duHkhaprApakamastyuta neti | pUrvapakShastu | na kAryaM vairAgyaM tadvidhAyakashrutAvanAshvAsAt.h | tadanAshvAsashcha svargakAmo yajetetyAdivat.h vedaikadeshe sukhasAdhanatayokte karmaNi karmaphalamArge vrIhyAdibhAvAvagatyA tachChedanakuTTanAdinA duHkhaprApterAvashyakatA phalavaiparItyenAnAshvAsAt.h | vrIhyAdibhAvasya dhUmAdhibhAvavat.h gauNatve vrIhyAdiduHkhijIvaiH sahAvasthAnena yAgAdikarmaNaH pashuhiMsArUpatayA pApatvena karmiNo duHkhaprApakasattvena cha duHkhAvashyaMbhAvAchcheti | siddhAntastu | karmiNaH shrutavrIhyAdibhAvasya jIvAntarAdhiShThitavrIhyAdidehapravesharUpatayA pUrvavadgauNatvAt.h duHkhijIvena sahAvasthAne.api karmaNo hiMsArUpatve.api "vAyavyaM shvetamAlabheta' ityAdi vedavihitatvena apApatayA duHkhAprApakatvena hetvabhAvena karmiNo duHkhAprApterna kvApi vedAnAshvAsa iti bhAvyaM vairAgyeNeti || 18 ||

|| OM retassigyogo.atha OM || 19 ||

pUrvatrAnyAdhiShThite vrIhyAdidehe iva svargAdAgatasya karmiNaH pitR^idehe praveshasAdhanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaM karmAdAvativairAgyamanapekShyamutApekShyamiti chintA | tadarthaM svargAdAgatasya karmiNaH pitR^ipravesho nAstyutAstIti | tadarthaM "yovA retassiJNchati tamevAnupratishati' iti shrutiH durbalA "svargAdavAggatashchApi mAturevodaraM vrajed.h' iti vachanaM prabalamuta viparItamiti | tadarthaM vachanaM sayuktikamuta neti | tadarthaM karmiNaH pitR^ipraveshe prayojanaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | karmiNaH pitR^ipraveshe phalAbhAvAt.h retaso dehapariNAmAyApekShitatve.api sekAnantaraM mAtR^ipraveshe.api tadupapatteH mAturevodaraM vrajediti vachanAt.h sayuktikasAdhAraNavachanabAditatayA pitR^ipraveshashruteH daurbalyena pitR^ipraveshAprApakatvAt.h nAsti pitR^ipravesha iti nApekShyamativairAgyamiti | siddhAntastu | dahekl.hptyatharmAvashyakatayA retasa uktavidhayA anyathopapattAvapi "Ishakl.hptyaiva pitaraM praviShyo yAti mAtaram.h' iti IshaklR^iptivachanena "retaHsichamevAnupravishati' (kauNTharavya) iti shrutyA cha pitR^ipraveshasiddheH mAturevetyevakArasya ayogavyavachChedakatvenopapattyA sayuktikatvAbhAvena cha pitR^ipraveshApratibandhakatvAdasti pitR^ipravesha iti bhAvyaM karmAdAvativairAgyeNeti || 19 ||

|| OM yoneshsharIram.h OM || 20 ||

pUrvasUtre athapadoktA pitR^idvArA mAtR^iprAptirevAtra sAdhyata iti saN^gatiH | athapadoktakarmAdAvativairAgyaM anAvashyakamutAvashyakamiti chintA | tadarthaM karmiNo dehaprAptau AyAso nAstyutAstIti | tadarthaM pitR^idehAdyonidvArA mAtR^IdaraM prApya svadehaM prA noti uta tathaivA notIti | tadarthamuktakramAdanyathApi janma sambhavatyuta neti | pUrvapakShastu | uktakramAdanyathApi karmiNaro janma sambhavati | tathAhi | pitussakAshAdeva tasmin.h bahireva vA mAndhAtR^idroNAderiva janmasambhavena mAturudaraprApteranAvashyakatvAttadAvashyakatve vA "dehagarbhasthitaM kvApi pravishetsvargato gataH' ityukteH | AstikAderiva saMsparshadvArA pitussakAshAnmAturudarapraveshasambhavena yoniprApteranAvashyakatvAt.h | "dehaM garbhasthitam.h' iti vachanAnmAtrupabhujyamAnAnnAdinA mAtR^IdarapraveshasambhavAt.h mAtR^idehastharetasaiva dehapariNatisambhavAchcha pitR^ipraveshasyApi vyarthatvAt.h | ato janmaprAptAvatyAyAsAbhAvAt.h nAtivairAgyeNa kR^ityamiti | siddhAntastu | pitR^ipraveshapUrvaM yonidvArA mAtR^Idarapraveshenaiva karmiNA janma nAnyathA | "divaH sthAsnuM gachChati sthAsnubhyaH pitaraM pituH mAtushsharIram.h sharIreNa jAyate' ityAdi (pauShyANaNa) shruteH | dehaM garbhasthitamityAdeH yogArAdhitabhagavatprasAdalabdhasAmarthyAtishayavatAM mahAtmanAM janmaviShayamiti karmiNo dehaprAptau AyAsasadbhAvAt.h bhAvyaM karmAdAvati vairAgyeNeti || 20 ||

|| iti shrIrAghavendrayatikR^itAyAM nyAyamuktAvalyAM tR^itIyAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH || 

|| atha dvitIyaH pAdaH ||

yaddArDhyAtharM vairAgyamuktaM pUrvapAde yA cha vakShyamANopAsanAN^gaM tAdR^ishabhaktyarthamatrapAde bhagavanmahimochyata iti pUrvottarapAdasaN^gatiH | etatpAdArthashcha bhAShyAdito vyaktaH | 

|| OM sandhye sR^iShyirAha hi OM || 1 ||

|| OM nirmAtAraM chaike putrAdayashcha OM || OM mAyAmAtraM tu kAtsnaryenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAt.h OM || OM sUchakashcha hi shruterAchakShate cha tadvidaH OM || 

pUrvatra yoneshsharIramiti jIvAnAM janmAvagatAvavasthAvarNanasya avasaraprAptatvAt.h tatrAvasthAnAM madhye "yonimanye prapadyante' ityadikAThakashrutau (2-2-7) yoniprAptyanantaraM sva noktyA tadanurodhenAtrAdau sva nArthatatpratItiniyantR^itvarUpo mahimA harernirUpyate | atra jij~nAsAsUtrasthAthashabdoktAdhikArivisheShaNIbhUtA haribhaktiH na kAryota kAryeti chintA | tadarthaM sva no.arthaH kimIshAnadhIna uta tadadhIna iti | tadarthaM kimasatya uta satya iti | tadarthaM kiM satyatve sAdhakaM nAsti bAdhakaM chAsti uta viparItamiti | pUrvapakShastu | neshAdhInaH sva nArthaH tasyAsattvAt.h | asato.api shashaviShANAderasatyatvena IshAdhInatvasya etena sarve vyAkhyAtA ityatroktAvapi ghaTAditaulyena yogakShemAdirUpatadadhInatvasya asato.anupapatteH | na chAsiddho hetuH | satyatve sAdhakAbhAvAdbAdhakabAhulyAchcha sva nArthAnAM satyatve nityatvamanityatvaM vA vAchyam.h | ubhayathApi prAgUrdhvamupalambhaprasaN^gAt.h | tadaivotpattivinAshavattvaM tu pramANAbhAvAdayuktam.h | kartrupAdAnanimittAnAmabhAvAchcha | bAhyopAdAnAdikAraNakatve kapAlAdyupalambhApAtAchcha | tadajanyatve cha shuktirUpyavadasattvasya durvAratvAchcha | asantaH eva gajAdayaH sva ne dR^iShyA iti bAdhabodhayogAchcha | evaM bAdhakAntarANi TIkoktAni j~neyAni | siddhAntastu | "yadA karmasu kAmyeShu striyam.h' (ChAM.5-2-9) ityAdi shrutismR^ititaH sva nArthAnAM shubhAdisUchakatvapramANena shAkunavatsatyatvAt.h | "na tatra rathAH' (bra.6-3-10) ityAdishrutyA prAgasatAmevArthAnAM sva na eva dR^iShyeH | sR^iShyeshchoktyA tadaivotpattinirodhayoH sambhavena prAgUrdhvamupalambhaprasaN^gAt.h | "ya eShu supteShu' iti (kA.5,7) shrutau "etasmAddhayeva putro jAyate' (gaupavana) iti shrutau cha sva nArthAnAM IshakartR^itvasyoktyA kartrabhAvachodyasya tathA bAhyArthaghaTAdivat.h sphuTamanabhivyaktatvayuktyA "manogatAMstu saMskArAn.h' iti (brahmANDa) smR^ityA cha bAhyopAdAnavilakShaNamAnasavAsanopAdAnakatvAvagamena nirupAdAnakatvachodyasya chAnavakAshAt.h | sva nAnAM 
jAgratpadArthatvasyAsattvena bAdhopapatteshcha sAdhakasadbhAvAchcha sva nArthAH satyA eveti sva nArthAH taddhiyaH tattirodhAnaM cheti sarvamIshAdhInamiti | phale tu pUrvAdhyAyoktasavarniyantR^itvarUpamahimAkShepAdidvArA bhaktyAkShepasamAdhI | sUtrakramastu | bAdhakanirAsa eva sAdhakaM sukhasthaM bhavatIti trisUtyA bAdhakAni nirasyAnte sAdhakoktiH | ata eva doShaparihArAya sUtramiti TIkA | tatrApi sR^iShyau siddhAyAM kartrAdikArakachintA | tatrApi kartuH prAdhAnyamityAdirUhyaH || 1 ||   N.M-8
|| OM parAbhidhyAnAttu tirohitaM tato hyasya bandhaviparyayau OM || 2 || 

astu sva napadArthAnAmuktadishA IshAyattatvaM na tu taddhItattirodhAnayoH | tayoH bAhyArthAj~nAnaj~nAnAbhyAmeva siddheH iti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atrAthapadoktabhaktirna kAryA uta kAryeti chintA | tadarthaM prakR^itAvirbhAvatirobhAvau kimIshAdhInau uta tadanadhInAviti | tadarthaM bAhyArthAj~nAnaj~nAne kiM sva nadhItirodhAnayoH svatantraheturuta nimittamAtramiti | pUrvapakShastu | svA nAvirbhAvatirodhAnayoH bAhyArthaj~nAnaj~nAnAdhInAnubhavena tadAvirbhAvatirodhAnayoH bAhyArthAj~nAnaj~nAnAbhyAmevopapattau IshvareNa kR^ityAbhAvAt.h | nahi bAhyAtharj~nAnAj~nAnayoH svanibandhanasvA nArthadhItannivR^ittyoranyApekShAstIti | siddhAntastu | yathA bandhamokShayoH IshAj~nAnaj~nAnanibandhanatvaprasiddhAvapi tayorjaDatvenAsvatantratayA bandhako bhavapAshena bhavapAshAchcha mochaka ityAdi vachaneneshAdhInAveva bandhamokShau tathA bAhyArthaj~nAnAj~nAnanimittakatayA pratIyamAnAvapi svA nAvirbhAvatirobhAvau IshAdhInAveva | j~nAnAj~nAnayorasvAtantAt.h | te tu nimittamAtram.h | "svA nAdibuddhikartA cha tiraskartA sa eva cha' ityAderiti | TIkAyAM tu sUtre bandhaviparyayAviti dvivachanasya sva nAdi buddhikarteti smR^ityukteshcha svArasyAnurodhena AvirbhAvasya aj~nAnAdhInatvanirAsakAdhikaraNAntarasyAbhAvena tirodhAnasya j~nAnAdhInatvanirAsakAdhikaraNAntarasyAbhAvena tirodhAnasya j~nAnAdhInatvanirAsakanyAyasamAnaviShayatvAt.h AdyasUtrAdau tirohitamityasyopalakShaNatayA siddhAnte svA nAvirbhAvatirobhAvayoH sAmyena dvandvena nirdeshAdyathAshrutaM sUtrAnurodhena tirodhAnamAtraprAdhAnyena pUrvapakShoktAvapi dvayossAmyenaiva pUrvapakSho.abhimata ityavirodhaH || 2 ||

|| OM dehayogAdvAso.api OM || 3 || 

ShaShThe kANvashrutau jyotirbrahmaNo "sa vA eSha etasmin.h (samprasAde) ratvA charitvA' (bR^i.6-3-15) ityAdinA sva noktyanantaraM jAgraduktyA sva nAvirbhAvAdichintAnantaraM atra jAgrachchintanAtsaN^gatiH | atra jAgradarthAnAM svA nArthavanna mithyAtvaM bahujanavivAdAbhAvAt.h bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | alpajanavivAdasya "nA bhAva upalabdheH (bra.sU.2-2-28) "vaidharmyAchcha na sva nAdivat.h' (bra.sU.2-2-29) ityatra nirAsAt.h | atra bhagavadadhInatAmAtraM chintyate | dehAbhimAnAdinAvasthitirUpa jAgradavasthA aharAdikAlAdhIneti prApte pUrvavadeva kAlasyAsvAtantAdIshAdhInaiveti siddhAntaH | visheShashaN^kA tu kAlAsvAtantyabuddheH bAdhakAbhAvena bhramatvAyogAt.h na nimittamAtraparatvamiti | parihArastu "sa eva jAgaritAsthApayati' ityAdishrutibalAnnimittamAtraparatvamiti | phale tu pUrvavat.h || 3 || 

|| OM tadabhAvo nADIShu tachChatarAtmani hi OM || 4 ||

pUrvatra sva najAgaraNayoH kAlAderasvAtanteNeshvarAdhInatvoktau avashiShyasupterapi pUrvanyAyeneshAdhInatvasiddhau atreshasya suptajIvaprApyatvalAbhAya suptisvarUpameva nirUpyate | atra jIvasya suptiH nADIparamAtmanoranyataratra utobhayatreti chintA | tadarthaM "satA saumya tadAsampannaH' (ChAM.6-8-1) iti cha shrutidvayamubhayatra suptivyavasthApakaM na bhavatyatha bhavatIti | tadarthamubhayatra suptiviruddhota neti | tadarthaM Adye tachcha kiM paramAtmamuta nADyAmiti tadarthaM nADyAM suptau auttarikAnusmR^itirna yuktota yukteti | tadarthaM sA kiM sauShuptikasukhAdyanubhavajanyasmR^itirUpa uta duHkhAbhAvAnumitirUpa iti | yadyAdyaH pakShaH tadA sukhAnusmR^itisiddhasauShuptikasukhaikAnubhavasya IshAdanyatrasthitau sva nAdAvivAyogAtparamAtmanIti phalam.h | yadyantyaH tadA suptau sukhAnubhavasyaivAbhAvena nADyAmeveti phalam.h | pUrvapakShastu | ubhayatra supterviruddhatvena shrutidvayasyobhayatra suptivyavasthApakatvAbhAvAt.h anyataratretyavashyaM vAchyam.h | suptikAlasyAj~nAnena pakShIkaraNAyogAt.h anumAnAnudayena "etAvantaM 
kAlaM sukhamahamasvApsamityasya smR^ititvena tatsiddhasukhaikAnubhavasya bhagavato.anyatrAvasthAne jAgradAdAvivAyogAt.h parAmAtmanyeveti | satA saumya tadA sampanno bhavatIti shruteshcha | nacha nADIShu supto bhavatIti shrutivirodhaH prAchInashrutessayuktikatvena prAbalyAditi | siddhAntastu | nityanirdoShatayA pramANabhUtayoruktashrutyoH sAkShAdasAkShAttvAbhyAM nADIsthaparamAtmanIti vyavasthayA virodhAbhAve sambhavati aprAmANyAyogAt.h sukhaikAnubhavasya chopapatteH nADIsthaparamAtmanyeveti | phale tu shrutyAdyavasthAdvArA bhaktyAdisAdhanashAstrAnAsthAtannirAsamukhena bhaktyAkShepasamAdhI | TIkAyAM tvanyataratreti pakShaM siddhavatkR^itya paramAtmani nADIShu vA ityetatsaMdihya vAdyantarapakShanirAsAya nADyAmeti pakShaM vyudasya paramAtmanyeveti pUrvapakShavyAjena sthApayitvA ubhayatretyeva siddhAntitam.h || 4 ||

|| OM ataH prabodho.asmAt.h OM || 5 ||

atra prAguktasuptaprApyatvahenaiva siddhAntakaraNAtsaN^gatiH | prakR^itasuptaprabodhaH kiM kvachit.h bherItADanAdi hetvantarAdhInaH uta sarvatreshaikAdhIna iti chintA | kvachit.h bherItADanAdi hetvantaradR^iShyeH nimittamAtrakalpakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | kvachidbherItADanAdi kAraNAntarANAmapyulambhAttatrApi Ishvarakalpane mAnAbhAvena kAraNAntarAbhAvasthale prabodhasyeshAdhInatve.api na kAraNAntarasadbhAvasthale tatra teShAmeva svAtantopapattau nimittamAtratvakalpane hetvabhAvAditi | siddhAntastu | "eSha eva suptaM prabodhayati' (kauNDiNya) iti sAvadhAraNashrutivirodhena hetvantarArAM nimittamAtratvAt.h suptaprabodhako.api Ishvara eva na tu kAraNAntarasvAtantyamiti | phale tu atha padoktabhaktyAkShepasamAdhI eveti || 5 ||

|| OM sa eva cha karmAnusmR^itishabdavidhibhyaH OM || 6 ||

pUrvatra sAmAnyataH sva nAdyavasthA IshAdhInetyuktam.h | atra tu sarvajanInAH sarvakAlInA api tadadhInA iti chintyata iti saN^gatiH | sva nAdyAvasthAprerakatvena prakR^ito viShNuH kiM keShAJNchitkAdAchitkAvasthAprerakaH uta sarvajIvAnAM sarvakAlInAvasthAprerakaH iti chintA | tadarthaM lokadR^iShyirniyAmikA bhavati uta neti | tadarthaM rAjAdilokadR^iShyayApavAdakaM mAnaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | keShAJNchitkAdAchitkAvasthAprerako na sarvajanInasarvakAlInAvasthAprerakaH loke rAjAdau khaNDeshatvadarshanAt.h | nacha dR^iShyiraprayojikA | tathAtve pratyakShasiddhA j~nAnakAlabherItADanAdi kAraNApekShApi sva nAdyavasthApreraNena syAt.h | nacha "anyabhAvavyAvR^itteshcha' (bra.sU.1-3-12) ityAdau lokadR^iShyityAgenoktANutvamahatvastrItvapuMstvAdisahabhAvavat.h "alpashruteH' (bra.sU.1-3-21) ityatroktavyomAMshavailakShaNyavat.h "shruteH' (bra.sU.2-1-28) ityAdau niraMshasyApyekadeshena pravR^ittyAdivachchAstu lokadR^iShyityAge sarvaprerakatvamiti vAchyam.h | tatrANoraNIyAn.h asthUlamanaNvityAdi eShame.antarhR^idaye jyAyAn.h yo.asau viruddho.aviruddhaH ityAdi pramANavat.h iha sarvAvasthAprerakatve mAnAbhAvAt.h yena dR^iShyityAgaH syAditi | siddhAntastu | viShNureva sarvatra sarvajIvena sarvakAlikasarvAvasthAprerakaH na tu kvachidanyo.api prerakaH | "eSha hyeva sAdhukarma kArayati' ityAdi bhAShyokta (kaushItakI 3-8) shrutibalena "Atmana evopAsyatvoktyanyathAnupapattyA cha asyaiva sarvaprerakatvAvagamAt.h | anyathA anyasyApi kvachitprerakatve shrutAvavadhAraNAt.h | nachaivaM lokadR^iShyivirodhaH | shrutyAdipramANabalena lokadR^iShyasyApi laukikadhenvAdAvadR^iShyasya kAmadhenvAdAvivopapatteriti | phale tUkta eva || 6 || 

|| OM mugdhe.ardhasampattiH parisheShAt.h OM || 7 ||

evaM pradhAnAvasthAnAM chintAnantaraM atrAvAntarAvasthAchintanAtsaN^gatiH | atra sva nAdyavasthAchintAprasaN^gasannidhApito mohaH kiM sva nAdyavasthAnyatamAntarbhUtaH uta tato.avasthAntaramiti | tadarthaM sa kiM bhagavatprAptitadanyatrasthityoranyatararUpaH uta tAbhyAmanyAdR^isha eveti | tadarthamanyAdR^ishatve mAnaM nAstyutAstIti | yadyAdyastadA avasthAntaramiti vyaktam.h | tathAnyatararUpa ityatrApi kimuktabhagavatprAptirUpaH kiM vA anyatrasthitirUpa iti chintA | tadarthaM kimayaM suptisadharma sva najAgratsadharmeti | atrApi vyaktaM phalaphalibhAvaH | atra TIkAyAmAdyasandehaH siddhAntoktadishA suj~nAna iti pradhAnAvasthAntaraM neti pradarshanAya sva 
nAditritayAnyatamatvaM siddhavatkR^itya mohe brahmaprAptireva pR^ithagavasthAtvAditi nyAyavivaraNe jAgratsva nayoH pR^ithagavasthAdityarthamupetya tadanuguNatvena saMdehapUrvapakShau darshitau | ata eva siddhAnte mohasya avasthAtrayAtiriktatve bhavedetadityAdyuktamiti j~neyam.h | pUrvapakShastu | mohaH sva nAdityavasthAntarbhUta eva na tu tato riktaH mAnAbhAvAt.h | brahmaprAptitadanyatrasthityoH suptyAdyavasthAtvena tato anyAdR^ishasthiterabhAvena atiriktatvAsambhavAchcha | bAhyAtharAj~nAnasAmyena suptyAdyantarbhAvasambhavAchcha | antarbhAvapakShe.api na bhagavadanyatrasthitirUpasva najAgradavasthAntarbhUtaH | tayoH svA nabAhyagajaturagAdyarthaj~nAnavatvarUpatvAnmohasya cha tadubhayaj~nAnashUnyasuptisamAnadharmatayA samagrabhagavatprAptirUpasuptyavasthAntarbhUta eveti | siddhAntastu | duHkhamAtrapratismR^iteriti (vArAha) smR^ityA duHkhAtmakAlAtiriktaviShayAntaraj~nAnashUnyarUpatvena sukhAdij~nAnopetasuptyAdyantarbhAvAyogAt.h mohAvasthAtrayAtiriktAvasthaiva duHkhaikAnubhavatvasyaiva bhAnatvAt.h | na chAtiriktatvAsambhavaH | paramAtmavidUratvasAmIpyapraveshAnAM tadanyatrasthititatprAptirUpANAM "hR^idayasthAt.h' (vArAha) iti smR^ityArdhapraveshasya mohatvenAvashyaM vAchyatayA parisheShapramANasiddhatvAditi | phale tu avasthAntarAvasthitajIvaprApyatvarUpamAhAtmyAbhAvatadbhAvAbhyAM bhaktyAkShepasamAdhI | atra mohaH kiM bAhyakAraNAdhIna uta IshvarAdhIna iti sandehe balavadabhighAtAdibAhyakAraNAdhInatvAnneshAdhIna iti prApte "sa eva cha' ityatrokta (bra.sU.3-2-9) siddhAntanyAyena IshAdhIna eva | bAhyakAraNadR^iShyistu "mUrChAprabodhanaM chaiva tata eva pravartate' iti vishiShyakaurmasmR^ityA nimittamAtraviShayetyarthasya pUrvanyAyenaiva siddhatvAt.h nAtra tachchintanaM kR^itamiti j~neyam.h || 7 ||

|| OM na sthAnato.api parasyobhayaliN^gaM sarvatra hi OM || 8 ||

|| OM na bhedAditi chenna pratyekamatadvachanAt.h OM || OM api chaivameke OM || 

pUrvatra sarvAvasthApravartakatvasya hareruktau iha tatpravartakavishvAdirUpeShu bhedashaN^kAnirAsAtsaN^gatiH | pratisharIraM jAgradAdisthAneShu sthito vishvAdirUpI bhagavAn.h kimanyonyaM bhedavAnutAbhinna iti chintA | tadarthaM kiM tasya bhedasAdhakaM bhinnAnekasthAnatvaM kAryakAraNabaddhatvAdibhedashravaNaTha cha kiM niravakAshamuta gauNatvAdinA sAvakAshamiti | pUrvapakShastu | anyonyaM bhedavAneva akShikaNThAdirUpabhinnasthAnakatvAt.h ghaTAdivat.h | nacha bhinnasthAnakatvaM bhedarUpasAdhyena vinA vyomavadityatroktadishA vyo na iva vA harerupapannamiti vAchyam.h | vyo nI.ashato.anekasthAnatvasambhave.api hareranekasthAnasthitavishvAdirUpANAM "saptAN^ga ekonaviMshatimukhaH' (mAM.1-3) ityAdinA pratyekaM samagrarUpashravaNena vyomavaiShamyeNa bhedasAdhyena vinA hetoranavakAshAt.h | kiMcha "kAryakAraNabaddhau tau' (mAM.2-2) ityAdinA vishvAdirUpANAM jAgratsva nasuShuptirUpakAryabaddhatvakAraNabaddhatvAbaddhatvasthUlabhuktvasUkShmabhuktvAdirUpeNa bhedavyapadeshAchchAnyonyaM bhedavAneva | nachAyaM vyapadesho bhedaM vinApi hetvantareNaiva yuktaH kalpakAbhAvAt.h hetvantaradR^iShyashcheti | siddhAntastu | anyonyaM tatra tatra sthitarUpairabhinna eva bhagavAn.h | "sarveShu bhUteShvetameva brahmetyAchakShate' (ai.u.3-2-3) sarveShu bhUteShu chakShurAdisthAneShu etamekameva pUrNaguNamAchakShate iti "eSha ta AtmAntaryAmyamR^itaH (bR^i.5-7-3) iti "ayameva saH yo.ayamAtmA' (bR^i.4-5-1) ityAdibhAShyoktashrutiShu tatra tatra sthitabhagavadrUpANAM parasparamUlarUpeNa chAbhedakathanAt.h | "amAtro.anantamAtrashcha' iti (mAM.4-7) shrutau cha bhinnAMshashUnyaH punaranantAMshashcheti vishvAdyanantarUpANAM abhedokteshcha | bhedAnumAnasya bhedapratinidhivisheSheNa vA uktAnekashrutibAdhitatayA aprAmANyenaivopapatteH | bhedavyapadeshasya cha "bhinno bhinneShu saMsthiteH' (brahmatarka) "aishvaryAdrUpamekaM cha sUryavadbahudheyate' ityAdismR^ityA goShThe gAvaH ekIbhavantItyatraikyoktivat.h vyApte harau "aN^guShThamAtraH puruShaH (kA.2-1-12) ityuktivachcha sthAnabhedenopachAreNa vA aishvaryabalena vA upapatteH | taduktamanyatra shrutibalAtsthAnAnAM bhedaH tasyAbheda eva' iti (nyA.vi) | phale tu bhedaprAptau anugrAhyAnugrAhakabhAvAdyApattyA "sa eva cha' (bra.sU.3-2-9) ityatroktaishvaryanirAsadvArA bhaktyAkShepasamAdhI || 8 ||

|| OM arUpavadeva hi tatpradhAnatvAt.h OM || 9 ||

|| OM prakAshavachchAvaiyarthyam.h OM || OM Aha cha tanmAtram.h OM || OM darshayati chAtho.api smaryate OM || 

pUrvatrobhayaliN^gamiti liN^gapadena prakR^itabhagavadrUpANAmatra aprAkR^itatvasAdhanAtsaN^gatiH | yadarthaM pUrvatra mahimoktaH sA bhaktiH viShNau na yuktAthAyukteti chintA | tadarthaM tatra mAhAtmyaM na yuktamuta yuktamiti | tadarthaM rUpavattvArUpavattvayordoShostyuta neti | tathA rUpitvArUpitvashrutyoH kimekaviShayakatvamuta bhinnaviShayakatvamiti | pUrvapakShastu | bhaktirharau na yuktA tasya rUpitve.arUpitve vA aN^gIkR^ite doShApAtena mAhAtmyAyogAt.h | rUpitve chaitravadanityatvaprasaN^gAt.h | "nAtmAshruteH' (bra.sU.2-3-10) ityatroktanityadehatvasyApi ihAkShepAt.h | "arUpamavyayam.h' (kA.3-15) ityAdishrutyaprAmANyApAtAchcha | arUpitve cha saundaryasulakShaNatvAdyayogAt.h | rugmavarNamAdityavarNamityAdishrutyaprAmANyaprasaN^gAchcha | nacha rUpyarUpitvashrutyoraprAkR^itaprAkR^itaviShayatvenAvirodhAnna ko.api doSha iti yuktaM kalpakAbhAvAditi | siddhAntastu | "aikAtmyapratyayasAram.h' (mAM.2-1) "AnandamAtramajaram.h' (chaturvedashikhA) "AnandarUpamamR^itam.h' (mu.2-2-8) ityAdibhAShyoktashrutismR^itibalena j~nAnAnandAdyAtmakadivyarUpashravaNena rUpashrutestadviShayatvasya cha "bhautikAnIharUpANi bhUtebhyo.asau paro yataH | arUpavAnataH' (mAtsya) ityAdismR^ityA prakR^ityAdyatItatvahetunA prAkR^itarUpahIne gR^ihAntashchAkShuShaprakAshe satyapi bAhyaprakAshAbhAvena prakAsho netyuktivat.h arUpashruteH aprAkR^itavigrahe.api harau prAkR^itarUpAbhAvaviShayatayopapatteH | aprAkR^itadivyavigrahasya cha anityatvAdyanApAdakatvAt.h saundaryAdisambhavAchcha mAhAtmyavattvAt.h yuktA tatra bhaktiriti | phale tu bhaktyAkShepasamAdhI || 9 ||

|| OM ata eva chopamA sUryakAdivat.h OM || 10 ||

yatpUrvanayadvaye bhagavadaMshAnAM "amAtro.anantamAtraH' itayantaM aikyakathanaM yachchArUpavaditi prAkR^itarUparAhityakathanaM tadubhayamayuktam.h | jIvasya bhagavadaMshAnAM bhedAbhedAt.h prAkR^itarUpavattvAchcheti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktabhaktirayuktota yukteti chintA | tadarthaM kiM jIvaH paramAtmanA bhinnAbhinno bhinna eveti | tadarthaM kiM paramAtmanA jIvAnAM samudAyasamudAyibhAvo.atha bimbapratibimbabhAva iti | tadarthaM pratibimbatvaM kimupAdhikR^itatvAdirUpamuta tadadhInatvAdirUpamiti | Adye tvanAdinityajIvAnAmaupAdhikapratibimbatvAyogena samudAyitvarUpatayA samudAyarUpeshvareNa bhedAbhedau aupAdhikabhede satyapi svAbhAvikasvAbhedavati svasminniva bhaktirayuktetyAdye phalam.h | ante tu tadadhInatvAdirUpapratibimbatvasya jIvAnAM yuktatvenAtyantabhinne harau bhaktiryukteti phalam.h | pUrvapakShastu | pR^ithagupadeshAdityatra jIveshabhedoktAvapi sarvachetanasamudAyasyeshatvena ekaikajIvasya paramAtmanA bhedAbhede.api bhedAvirodhAt.h | aupAdhikabhedasya cha svAbhAvikabhedakAryApratibandhakatvena svAbhinne tasminbhaktirayukteti | na cha bhedo.asiddhaH chetanatvAdaMshatvAnmatsyAdivaditi tatsiddheH | bimbapratibimbabhAvastu aupAdhiko.anAdinityayorjIveshayorna yukta iti | siddhAntastu | jIvo neshAbhinnaH tatpratibimbatvAt.h | yo yatpratibimbaH sa tenAbhinno na bhavati yathA sUryakAdiritayanumAnavirodhena chetanatvAderabhedAsAdhakatvAt.h | nachAsiddho hetuH | jIvasyApIshvarasvarUpAMshatve matsyAdisAmyApattyA j~nAnaishvaryAdyavisheShaprasaN^garUpayuktyA "rUpaMrUpaM pratirUpo babhUva' (bR^i.4-5-29) iti shrutyA "bahavassUryakA yadvatsUryasya sadR^ishA jale' iti smR^ityA cha tatsiddheH | na chAnAdinityasyaupAdhikapratibimbatvAyogaH | "pR^ithagupadeshAt.h' (bra.sU.2-3-28) "sandhye sR^iShyirAha hi' (bra.sU.3-2-1) "tadguNasAratvAt.h' (bra.sU.2-3-29) ityuktaiH bhinnatvatadadhInatvatatsadR^ishaireva dharmai pratibiMbatvopagamAditi || 10 ||

|| OM ambuvadagrahaNAttu na tathAtvam.h OM || 11 || 

pUrvatra bimbasAdR^ishyAdinA jIvasyeshapratibimbatvoktau tarhi j~nAnAnandAdirUpasAdR^ishyarUpamuktenirtyasiddhatvAnna tadarthA bhaktiH kAryeti shaN^kodayAtsaN^gatiH | atra athapadokteshvarabhaktiH na kAryota kAryeti chintA | tadarthaM Ishaj~nAnatatprasAdadvArA j~nAnAnandAdibrahmasAdR^ishyAbhivyakteH shrutaM phalatvaM na sambhavatyuta sambhavatIti | pUrvapakShastu | j~nAnAnandAdibrahmasAdR^ishyasya "puMstvAdivattvasya' (bra.sU.2-3-31) ityatroktadishA jIvasvarUpatayA nityasiddhatvAttadabhivyaktestu "anubandhAdibhyaH (bra.sU.3-3-51) iti vakShyamANadishA j~nAnahetubhaktiphalatvAyogAt.h | suptAviva kadAchit.h svayameva sambhavena cha 
IshvarAparokShaj~nAnatatprasAdadvArApi bhaktiphalatvaM tasya na yuktamiti phalAbhAvAnna kAryA bhaktiriti | siddhAntastu | sAdR^ishyasya nityasiddhatve.api IShadabhivyakteH bhaktiM vinA suptau bhAve.api samyagabhivyaktirUpamukteH "yamevaiSha' (mu.6-3) itayAdibhAShyoktashrutismR^itibalena bhaktisAdhyatvAttadarthaM bhaktiravashyaM kAyareti || 11 ||

|| OM vR^iddhihrAsabhAktvamantarbhAvAdubhayasAmaJNjasyAdevam.h OM || 12 ||

|| OM darshanAchcha OM || 

atra prAk.h phalahetutvena uktabhakteH tadupalakShitatvena sAdhanajAtasya taratamabhAvanirUpaNAtsaN^gatiH | pUrvasUtroktaM bhaktayupalakShitabhaktyAdisAdhanajAtaM kiM bhakteShvekaprakAramutAnekaprakAramiti chintA | tadarthaM tatphalatayoktAnandAdibrahmasAdR^ishyAbhivyaktiH sarvatraikaprakArA utAnekaprakArA iti | saiShAnandasyetyAdeH vairAgyaprashaMsAparatvena AnandatAratamye mAnAbhAvena phalatAratamyAsiddhayA bhaktayAditatsAdhanamapi bhakteShvekaprakArameva phalavaiShamye.api sAdhanAvaiShamye bAdhakAbhAvAchcheti pUrvapakShaH | siddhAntastu | saiShetishruteH vairAgyaprashaMsAdiparatvasya tadvAkyavaiyarthyAdinA.anyatra bR^ihadbhAShyAdisthaleShu bhAShyakAraireva nirAsAnnyAyAmR^ite.api (pR^i.643-ni) khaNDitatvAt.h saiShetyAdibhAShyoktashrutyAdisiddhAnandAdirUpaphalatAratamyAnyathAnupapattyA tattsAdhaneShu tAratamyamavashyamabhyupeyam.h | anyathA viShamaphaladAturIshvarasya vaiShamyAdidoShApAtAt.h | sa cha netyuktaM vaiShamyanaye (bra.sU.2-1-35) | sAdhanasyottamatvenetibhAShyoktasmR^itivirodhAchcheti | AnandAdishrutermuktaparatvaM cha "akSharadhiyAM tu' (bra.sU.3-3-34) ityatrAgre vyaktam.h || 12 ||

|| OM prakR^itaitAvatvaM hi pratiShedhati tato bravIti cha bhUyaH OM || 13 ||

pUrvatra shrautAnandatAratamyAnyathAnupapattyA taddhetutAratamyanirNaya ivehApi shrutAvadhikavyApAroktyanyathAnupapattyA pAlanAkhyApAranirNayAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktabhaktirayuktota yukta iti chintA | tadarthaM pAlakAkhyaguNo harerna yukta uta yukta iti | tadarthaM pAlanaM nAma kashchidvayApAro nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | sR^iShyasya vastuno yAvatsaMhAraM sthiteH svata eva siddheH saMhArAdikartuH asaMhArAdyatirikto rakShArUpo vyApAra eva neti na pAlakatvaM hareryuktamiti | siddhAntastu | yuktaiva harau bhaktiH pAlakatvAkhyaguNavattvAt.h | na chAsaMhArAtiriktaH sa neti vAchyam.h | "naitAvadenAparonyadastyukShA sa dyAvA pR^ithivI' iti (R^i.10-31-8) shrutau pUrvatra "asyedeShA sumatiH paprathAnA' (R^i.10-31-6) ityAdinoktasR^iShyisaMhArakartR^itvasya "naitAvad.h' ityanena tAvanmAtratvaM niShidhya "paro.anyadastItyAdinA pAlanAkhyavyApArAntarasyApyuktyA annAdidAnena poShaNAdirUpavyApArAntarasya pAlanasya sambhavAt.h sR^iShyiM cha pAlanaM chaiveti smR^iteshchaiveti | phale tu vyakte || 13 ||

|| OM tadavyaktamAhahi OM || 14 ||

|| OM api saMrAdhane pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAm.h OM || OM prakAshavachchAvaisheShyam.h OM || OM prakAshashcha karmaNyabhyAsAt.h OM || OM ato.anantena tathAhi liN^gam.h OM || 

pUrvatra janmAdisUtroktasR^iShyayAdyaShyake pAlakatvaM prasAdhya atra svaj~nAnadatvamiha sAdhyata iti saN^gatiH | atrAthapadoktabhagavadbhaktiH na kAryota kAryeti chintA | tadatharM kimaphalota phalavatIti | sA kiM Ishasya vyaktatve.avyaktatve chobhayathApi paramapumarthahetvIshAparokShaheturuta avyaktatve.api IshvaraprasAdadvArA taddheturiti | pUrvapakShastu | hareH stambhAdivatpratyakShayogyatve stambhAdipratyakShasyeva bhaktiM vinApi pratyakShatvasambhavAt.h avyaktaikasvabhAvatve dharmAdiriva bhaktyAdisAdhanenApi pratyakShatvAsambhavAt.h anyathA tAdR^ishasyApi pratyakShatve samArAdhanenApi yakShasAkShAtkAravadIshvarasAkShAtkArasambhavAt.h 
agnyAdibhUtAnAM sthUlasUkShmavisheSheNa pratyakShApratyakShatvavanmUlarUpeNa avyaktasyApi gR^ihItarUpeNa pratyakShatvasambhavAt.h na bhaktiH aparokShaheturiti vyarthA satI na kAryeti | siddhAntastu "arUpamakSharaM brahma sadA.avyaktaH' iti (kauNTharavya) shrutyA avyaktaikasvabhAvasyApi "AtmA vA are draShyavyaH shrotavyaH' (bR^i.4-4-5) ityAdishrutibalena bhaktipUrvakashravaNAdyAbhyAsAtprasannena achintyashaktikeshvareNaiva tadAparokShasya "nityAvyakto.api bhagavAnIkShyate nijashaktitaH' iti (nArAyaNAdhyAtma) shrutyuktena mokShasya j~nAnajaprasAdasAdhyatvaliN^gena avyaktatvapratyakShatvashrutidvayAnyathAnupapattyA cha siddhatvAt.h | "na tamarAdhayitvApi kashchidvayaktIkariShyati' (brahmavaivarta) iti smR^itisiddhamahatpratyakShAt.h avyaktatvaliN^gena sUkShmatvAnumAnAt.h bhaktihInArAdhanena "nAsau sUkShmo na sthUlaH' ityAdi (mANDavya) shrutyAdito gR^ihItarUpeNa cha IshapratyakShatvasya abhAvAvagamAt.h bhaktireva shravaNAdiyuktA bhagavadaparokShaheturiti arthavatI bhaktiravashyaM kAryeti || 14 ||

|| OM ubhayavyapadeshAttvahikuNDalavat.h OM || 15 ||

|| OM prakAshAshrayavadvA tejastvAt.h OM || OM pUrvavadvA OM || OM pratiShedhAchcha OM || 

pUrvatra hareravyaktatve pratyakShatve cha mAnAbhAvena avyaktasyApi vyaktatvoktivadihApi guNAtmatve.api guNitve chobhayatra mAnAbhAvAt.h guNAtmano.api guNitvamiti kathanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktA haribhaktirna kAyarota kAryeti chintA | tadarthaM tasya guNatvaM nAstyutAstIti | tadarthaM guNAtmano hareH guNitvaM sambhAvanApramANAbhyAM hInaM yuktiviruddhaM chAtha viparItamiti | pUrvapakShastu | tadAtmake tadvattvasya kvApyadarshanAt.h guNarUpasya hareH guNavattvamasambhAvitaM ata eva pramANashUnyaM cha | harirna guNavAn.h guNAtmakatvAt.h yathA na svaH svavAn.h yo yadvAn.h sa tadAtmako na yathA daNDavAn.h chaitraH iti vA ityAdi yuktiviruddhaM cha | nacha guNAtmakatvamasiddhaM samavAyAbhyupagamAchchetyatra (bra.sU.2-2-13) samavAyApAkaraNena "ekamevAdvitIyam.h' (ChAM.6-2-1) iti guNaguNyAdibhedaniShedhena tatsiddheH | ato guNitvAbhAvAt.h na harau bhaktiH kAryeti | siddhAntastu | kuNDalAtmakasyApyaheH visheShabalAtkuNDalitvavat.h prakAshAtmakasyApyAdityasya prakAshitvavat.h kAlasya pUrveNAbhede.api pUrvaH kAlaH iti visheShaNavisheShabhAvavachcha guNAtmano.api hareH guNitvaM pratinidhivisheShabalAnnAsambhAvitam.h | "AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn.h' (tai.2-4) "athaiSha paramaH AnandaH' iti guNatvaguNitvobhayavyapadesharUpapramANAchcha "shAstrayoni' (bra.sU.1-1-3) nayanyAyena yuktyagamyatayA "shruteH' tu ityatroktanyAyena (bra.sU.2-1-28) yuktyaviruddhaM cheti harau bhaktiH kAryeti || 15 ||

|| OM paramataH setUnmAnasambandhabhedavyapadeshebhyaH OM || 16 ||

|| OM darshanAt.h OM || OM buddhayarthaH pAdavat.h OM ||

pUrvatreshaguNAnAM tadAtmakatvaM taddharmavattvaM choktam.h | iha tu alaukikatvaM laukikashabdavAchyatvaM chochyata iti saN^gatiH | athapadoktA harAvatishayitabhaktiH na kAryota kAryeti chintA | tadarthaM tadIyaguNajAtaM laukikamutAlaukikamiti | tadarthaM tasyAlaukikatve j~nAnAnandAditattatpadavAchyatvaM ayuktamutayuktamiti | pUrvapakShastu | ghaTavilakShaNo ghaTapadavAchyatvAdR^iShyayA bhagavadAnandAdau cha "AnandaM brahmaNaH' ityAdau AnandAdipadaprayogeNa tadanyathAnupapattyA.alaukikatve mAnAbhAvena cha tadguNAjAtaM laukikameva | anyathA tatra tatpadaprayogAyoga iti | siddhAntastu | "eShaseturvidhR^itiH' (ChAM.8-4-1) "ya eSha AnandaH parasya' iti "yato vAcho nivartante' (tai.2-4) iti "etasyaivAnandasyAnyAni anyajj~nAnaM parasya cha' iti "adR^iShyamavyavahAryamavyapadeshyam.h' (kauNDiNyashruti) ityAdau brahmAnandAdiguNeShu laukikAnandAdAvasambhAvyamAnasetutvonmAnatvashabditapUrNatvabimbatvalokavilakShaNAdR^iShyatvAvyapadeshyatvAdidharmANAM uktyA alaukikatvAvashyambhAvini tattachChabdaprayogasya jIveshvarayoraMshAshitvaj~nApanArthatvena prapdhipAdavilakShaNe.api jIve pAdo.asya vishvabhUtAnItyAdau pAdashabdaprayogasya jIveshaguNAnAM arthaprakAshakatvAnukUlavedyatvAdij~nApanArthatvenopapatteH | "alaukiko.api j~nAnAdiH tachChabdenaiva bhaNyate | j~nApanArthAya lokasya' iti smR^iteshcha alaukikameveshaguNajAtamiti yuktA tatrAtishayabhaktiriti 
| vyutpattireva padAnAM tatrAyukteti tu "kAryAkhyAnAd.h' ityatra (bra.sU.3-3-19) nirasiShyate || 16 ||

|| OM sthAnavisheShAtprakAshAdivat.h OM || 17 ||

|| OM upapatteshcha OM || 

prAguktabimbatvahetukAlaukikatvasyeha AkShepeNa shaN^kodayAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktAtishayitabhaktisiddhayarthaM prAguktamIshaguNAnAM bimbatvahetukamalaukikatvaM na yuktamuta yuktamiti chintA | tadarthaM bhagavadAnandAdiguNasya vichitrabrahmAdyAnandAdibimbatvamayuktamuta yuktamiti | tadarthaM pratibimbavaichityameva kAraNamutAnyadapIti | pUrvapakShastu | "vR^iddhihrAsabhAktvam.h' ityatroktadi (bra.sU.1-2-20) brahmAdyAnandAdInAM mitho vichitratvAtteShAM cheshaguNapratibimbatve tAMshcha pratIshaguNAnAM bimbatve cha tadvadeva vaichityaM syAt.h | "adR^iShyAniyamAd.h' ityatra (bra.sU.2-3-51) adR^iShyAdivaichityeNa pratibimbavaichityoktAvapi svAbhAvikAnandAderAdimatkAraNakatvAyoga iti tasyaivehAkShepeNa bimbavaichityanibandhanatvAtpratibimbavaichityasya tathAcha bhagavadrUpeShu guNatAratamyaM cha syAt.h | tachcha netyuktam.h "na sthAnataH' (bra.sU.3-2-11) ityatra | ato bimbatvAbhAvAnneshaguNAnAmalaukikatvamiti na tatrAtishayitabhaktiH kAryeti | siddhAntastu | bimbavaichityAbhAve.api sUryakAntAdisthAnaguNena sUryAdipratibimbatve.agnijanakatvAdivaichityavat.h brahmAdyanAdibhaktyAdisthAnaguNavaichityeNa bimbabhUtabhagavadaishvaryavashena cha avichitrabhagavadAnandAdipratibimbavaichityasyopapatteH | "brahmAdiguNavaisheShyAd.h' (vArAha) iti "aishvaryAtparamAdviShNoH' iti cha (pAdma) smR^iteshcha IshaguNAnAmavaichitye.api bimbatvaM yuktamityalaukikatvAdatishayitA bhaktirAvashyakIti || 17 ||   N.M-9
|| OM tathAnyatpratiShedhAt.h OM || 18 ||

sthAnavisheShAdityasya bimbapratibimbabhAvarUpahetusAdhakatayA "paramate' (bra.sU.3-2-32) ityanenaikArthenAvyavadhAyakatvAt.h paramata ityatroktanyAyAtideshakatvAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktA bhaktiH na kAryota kAryeti chintA | tadarthaM brahma vyaktamutAvyaktamiti | tadatharM dhyAnapratItameve brahmota tadanyaditi | pUrvapakShastu | "phalamate' iti (bra.sU.3-2-39) vakShyamANadishA brahmaNa eva phalapradatvAt.h "taM yathAyathA' ityAderupAsitasyaiva phaladAtR^itvAt.h dhyAtasyAbrahmatve tasyAH phaladAtR^itvena dhyAnavaiyarthyAt.h dhyAtR^ipuruShabahutvaprayuktadhyeyabahutvasya "na sthAnataH' ityuktanyAyena bhedahIne.api harau tadrUpANAM nAnAnvenopapatteshcha dhyAnakAlapratItameva brahmeti bhaktiM vinApi puruShaprayatnena vyaktatvasambhavAnna tatra bhaktirAvashyakIti | siddhAntastu | "setUnmAnatvAdinA' IshaguNajAtasya lokato.anyatvavat.h "arUpavadeva' ityAdAvuktadishA aprAkR^itanirdoShasarvasulakShaNadivyasvarUpavigrahasya hareH nAnAdurlakShaNayuktadhyAnapratItervastutvAyogena tadanyatvAvashyaMbhAvAt.h "tadeve brahma tvaM viddhi nedaM yadidamupAsate' iti (tala.1-6) shrutau dhyAnapratItasya brahmatvaM pratiShidhya tadanyadeva brahmetyuktatvAchcha dhyAnapratItAdanyadevAvyaktaM brahmeti | nacha phalAbhAvApAtaH | "pashyanti paramaM brahma' iti (brahmatarka) smR^ityA dhyAnakAle pratItavAsanAmayapratimAsthasyaiva phalapradatvopapatteH bhaktirAvashyakIti || 18 ||

|| OM anena sarvagatamAyAmayashabdAdibhyaH OM || 19 ||

evamavyaktatve.api hareH prasannasya aparokShadAnamiva svasvAtantyamapi anyasya kvachiddadyAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktaharAvevAtishayitabhaktiH na yuktota yukteti chintA | tadarthaM kiM kvachit.h kadAchidanyo.api kartA uta sarvatra sarvadA sarvavastunaH harireva sR^iShyayAdikarteti | tadarthaM svasvAtantyaM kadAchidanyasyApi dadAtyuta neti | pUrvapakShastu | hareH kR^iShNAdyavatAreShu parapreShyatvAdyasambhAvitavividhalIlAdarshanena kvachitkadAchit.h svAtantyasyApyanyasya dAnasambhavAt.h harereva sarvasR^iShyayAdau mAnAbhAvAlloke rAjAdInAM khaNDeshatvadarshanAt.h deshAntarAdAvanyo.api sR^iShyayAdikataretyanumAnasambhavAchcha na harAvevAtishayitA bhaktiryukteti | siddhAntastu | "svAtantAtkrIDate viShNuH na hi svAtantyamanyagam.h | karoti kvApi' 
(nyAyavivaraNa) ityAderatyaktasvAtantyasyaiva krIDAvagamAdanyatra svAtantyadAnasyAsambhAvitatvAt.h harireva sarvakartetyasya "eSha sarvagataH' ityAdibhAShyoktashrutisiddhatvAdanumAnasya etachChatibalena kartrantare mAnAbhAvAchcha harireva sR^iShyayAdikarteti yuktA tatraivAtishayitA bhaktiriti || 19 ||

|| OM phalamata upapatteH OM || 20 ||

|| OM shrutatvAchcha OM || dharmaM jaiminirata eva OM || OM pUrvaM tu bAdarAyaNo hetuvyapadeshAt.h OM || 

evaM harereva sarvakartR^itve tasya vaiShamyAdidoShanirAsAya pUrvoktadishA karmasApekShatve tarhi karmaNa evAstu phalapradatvamiti vA karmaNa eva phalodayAt.h prAguktaM hareH sarvasraShyR^itvamayuktamiti vA shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | athapadoktA bhaktiH na kAyarota kAryeti chintA | tadarthaM kiM karmaiva phaladAtR^iharistatra sheShabhUta uta viparItamiti | tadarthaM "rAtirdAtuH parAyaNam.h' iti (bR^i.5-9-28) shrutaM hareH phaladAtR^itvaM gauNamuta mukhyamiti | tadarthaM karmaNaH phalAnvayavyatirekau sheShitvakalpakau uta sheShatayApi yuktAviti | tadarthaM karmaNaH sheShitvakalpakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | IshvaraH phaladAtetipakShe.api karmaNo.avaiyarthyAya vedaprAmANyAya hareH vaiShamyAdyabhAvAya kR^itakamarNaH phaladR^iShyayA cha karmApekShatave.avashyaMbhAvini phalasya karmAnvayavyatirekitvAt.h tasya cha anyathAsiddhikalpakAbhAvAt.h "rAtirdAtuH' iti shruteH "eShahyeva sAdhukarma kArayati' (kaushI.3-8) ityAdinA hareH phalapradakarmahetutayA gauNatvenApyupapatteH AptatamagautamajaiminimatatvAchcha karmaiva prAdhAnyena phalapradaM haristu karmasheSha iti na tatra bhaktiH kAryeti | siddhAntastu | chetanatvayuktyA "puNyena puNyaM lokaM nayati' (Sha.pra.3-7) ityAdivisheShashrutyA cha "rAtirdAtuH' iti shruterbalavattayA gauNArthatvAyogAt.h brahmaNaH prAdhAnyena phaladAtR^itve.api karmaNaH kAraNatvenAnvayavyatirekayoH jaiminimatasya chopapatteH brahmaiva phalapradaM na karma kintu karaNameveti yuktA tatra bhaktirita || 20 ||

|| iti shrImadrAghavendrayatikR^itAyAM nyAyamuktAvalyAM tR^itIyAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH samAptaH || 

|| atha tR^itIyaH pAdaH ||

prAguktAthapadArthavairAgyabhaktisAdhyaj~nAnahetujij~nAsAshabditopAsanAsminpAde uchyate | sA cha dvedhA sarvasachChAstrashravaNamananarUpA dhyAnarUpA cheti | tatrAdyA dhyAnAN^gatvAdAdAvuchyate |

|| OM sarvavedAntapratyayaM chodanAdyavisheShAt.h OM || 1 ||

|| OM bhedAnneti chedekasyAmapi OM || OM svAdhyAyasya tathAtvena hi samAchAre.adhikArAchcha OM || OM salilavachcha tanniyamaH OM || OM darshayati cha OM || 

atra jij~nAsAshabdokte sarvasachChAstrashravaNamanane na kArye uta kArye iti chintA | tadarthaM brahma svasvashAkhoktarItyA j~neyamuta sarvavedoktadisheti | tadarthaM harej~nareyatve sAdhakaM nAstyuta bAdhakaM chAsti atha viparItamiti | tadarthaM shAkhAbhedaH pratishAkhaM arthabhedoktish.hcha niravakAshA uta sAvakAsheta | pUrvapakShastu | brahma tathA j~neyamityatra sAdhakAbhAvAt.h pratyuta vedarAsherekaikAdhikArikatve kANvAdishAkhAbhedAyogasya vij~nAnamAnandaM brahmetyAdirUpeNa pratishAkhamarthabhedoktyayogasya ekaikasya sarvashAkhAdhyayanAbhAvena tadarthaM j~nAnAyogasya mandAnAM brahmaj~nAnavaimukhyaprasaN^garUpasya cha bAdhakasyAbhAvAt.h tattachChAkhoktameva tena tena j~neyamiti noktarUpashravaNamanane kArye iti | siddhAntastu | bhagavajj~nAnasampAdanArthaM pravR^ittAnAM "AtmetyevopAsIta' (bR^i.3-4-7) ityevamAdikANvAditattachChAkhAgatavidhInAM j~nAnArthaM pravR^ittavidhyarthamuktAnAM "atra hyete sarva ekaM bhavantIti' (bR^i.3-4-7) "na hyAsya karma kShIyate' (bR^i.3-4-15) ityAdi tatra vidhisamIpA nAtArthavAdAnAM cha tathA "svAdhyAyo.adhyetavyaH' 
(tai.A.2-15) "vedaH kR^itsno.adhigantavyaH sarahasyo dvij~nanmanA' ityevamAdeH arthAvabodhaphalakasvAdhyAyAdhyayanavidheshcha sarvAdhikArisAdhAraNyena "sarvavedoktamArgeNa karma kurvIta' iti (samAchAra) smR^ityA sarvavedoktamArgAnuShThAne sarveShAmadhikArAvagamena cha tadanyathAnupapattirUpayuktyA cha "sarvavedAnadhItya vichAyar cha j~nAtumichChenmumukShuH' iti (chaturvedashikhA) shrutyA "sarvAn.h vedAn.h setihAsAn.h' iti (brahmatarka) smR^ityA chaikaikasya sarvashAkhAdhyayanadvArA taduktArthaj~nAnAdhikArAvagamena sAdhakasadbhAvAt.h "shAkhAbhedo hyashaktijaH' iti (samAchAra) smR^ityA kANvAdishAkhAbhedasya ashaktihetukatvena pratishAkhamarthabhedokteH ekashAkhasthArthabhedoktivat.h prasaN^gabhedAdanuvAdAdirUpatayA sarvavedoktarItyA brahma j~neyamiti niyamasya sarvAsAmapAM samudra ekAyanamityuktaniyamasyeva "yathA nadInAM salilaM shakye sAgaragaM bhavet.h' iti (Agneya) smR^ityA tattachChaktyanusAritayopapattyA prAguktabAdhakAnAmabhAvAchcha sarvavedoktadishA yathAshakti sarvasachChAstrashravaNamanane sarvairapi kArye eveti | phale tu jij~nAsAshabdArthaikadeshAkShepasamAdhI || 1 || || OM upasaMhAro.arthAbhedAdvisheShavatsamAne cha OM || 2 || 

|| OM anyathAtvaM cha shabdAditi chennAvisheShAt.h OM || OM na vA prakaraNabhedAtparovarIyastvAdivat.h OM || OM saMj~nAtashchettaduktamasti tu tadapi OM || 

vaiyarthyahetunA prAguktayathAshaktisarvavedArthaparij~nAnasyAkShepeNeha shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atra pUrvoktasarvavedoktaparij~nAnaM nAvashyakamutAvashyakamiti chintA | tadarthaM sArvatrikaguNopasaMhArAnupasaMhArAbhyAM vedAthUbhUtabrahmadhyAnaM na yuktamutamayuktamiti | pUrvapakShastu nobhayathApi dhyAnaM sambhavatIti | tathAhi | na tAvaduShasaMhR^itya dhyAnaM kAryamiti pakSho yuktaH | sarvaparij~nAnasya kramabhAvitvena shakyatve.api sArvatrikasarvaguNopasaMhAreNa dhyAnasya vikShipyoktaguNAnAmekabuddhayupArUDhatvarUpasyAshakyatvAt.h | sarvAshakyatve.api kAMshchitprati tathA dhyAnaM shakyamiti kalpanasya kalpakashUnyatayA.ayogAt.h | AtmetyevopAsIteti sAvadhAraNAtmatvamAtropAsanavidhivAkyaviruddhaM cha parovarIyaHprabhR^itiprakaraNabhedAyogAt.h | nApyanupasaMhR^itya dhyAnaM kAryamiti pakShaH spaShyapramANAbhAvAt.h | Atmetyevetyatra evakArasya ayogavyavachChedakayApi sAvakAshatopapatteH | nacha parevarIyovaishvAnarAdiprakaraNabheda evAnupasaMhAre mAnamanyathA sa na syAditi yuktam.h | ekasminnapi prakaraNe sarvaguNokterapi sambhavAt.h | ata ubhayathApi dhyAnasyAyuktatvAt.h yaddhayAnAN^gatayA prAguktaM shaktAnAM sarvavedArthaparij~nAnaM sampAdyamiti tatrAnyataradapi vyarthatvAnnAvashyasampadyatAmarhatIti | siddhAntastu | ubhayathApi dhyAnaM sambhavatIti prAguktaM dvirUpamapi vedArthaparij~nAnaM yuktameveti | tathAhi | sarvavedoktaguNAnAM doShAbhAvAnAM chopasaMhAreNa dhyAnasya "upAsya ekaH' iti bhAShyokta (bhAllaveya) shrutau "sarve guNAH sarvadaiva hyupAsyAH' (nyAyavivaraNokta) iti shrutau cha vihitatvAt.h anyathA vihitakriyAlopenAnatharprasaN^gAt.h | tathA ChAndogye saptame "R^igvedaM bhagavo.adhyemi' (ChAM.7-1-2) ityAdinA nAradenAtmanaH sarvavidyAveditvamuktvA "so.ahaM bhagavo mantravidena nAtmavid.h' iti (ChAM.7-1-3) shrutyantare cha "so.ahaM nAmavideva nAtmavid.h' ityuktyA cha sarvavidyAnAM bhagavannAmatvena tadguNAbhidhAyakatvAnyathAnupapattiyuktyA cha tathA dhyAnasya siddhatvAt.h guNAbhidhAnasya "adhyAyanAya prayojanAbhAvAd.h' iti (bra.sU.3-3-15) nyAyena dhyAnArthatvAt.h "nAma vA etAH brahmaNaH sarvavidyAstasmAdekaH sarvaguNaivirchintya' iti (kauNDiNya) shrutisiddhatvAchcha | AtmetyevetyevakArasyAyogavyavachChedakatvena avirodhakatvAt.h prakaraNabhedagateshcha "puruShavidyAyAm.h' (bra.sU.3-3-25) ityatra vakShyamANatvAt.h upasaMhR^itya dhyAnaM kAryamiti pakSho yuktaH | tathAnupasaMhR^itya dhyAnaM kAryamiti pakSho.api yukta eva upasaMhR^itya dhyAnasya ashakyatvAtprakaraNabhedAt.h | "sa eSha parovarIyAnudgIthaH sa eSho.anantaH' (ChAM.1-9-2) ityAdi prakaraNeShu parovarIyastvAdikatipayaguNasyaivoktyA ekatra sarvaguNokterabhAvAt.h | tasmAdubhayathA dhyAnasya prAmANikatvena yuktatvAduktarUpavedArthaparij~nAnamarthavedeveti | phale tu pUrvAkShepasamAdhI || 2 ||

|| OM prApteshcha samaJNjasam.h OM || 3 ||

atra prAguktaguNopasaMhArAnupasaMhArapUrvakadhyAnayoradhikAribhedena yuktatvasamarthanAtsaN^gatiH | jij~nAsAshabdAbhimataM prAguktadvirUpadhyAnaM ayuktamuta yuktamiti chintA | tadarthaM adhikAribhedena vyavasthA na sambhavatyuta sambhavatIti | tadarthaM vyavasthApakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | dvirUpadhyAnasya virodhenaikasyAyogAt.h adhikAribhedena vyavasthitatvasya chAtrAsyAdhikAro.atra 
tasyeti vyavasthApakapramANAbhAvenAyogAdayuktaM dvirUpadhyAnamiti | siddhAntastu | "yasya yAvadguNAH spaShyaM pratibhAsantyupAsane yugapatsvabhujau yadvaddhayAyettAvata eva saH' iti (nyAyavivaraNokta) shrutyuktadishA "guNaissarvairupAsyosau brahmaNaH' ityAdi (bhaviShyatparva) smR^ityuktadishA cha dhyAnakAle cha yugapatspaShyasarvaguNapratItyA sarvaguNapratItirUpayogyatAvisheShayuktabrahmatadanyAdhikAribhedena vyavasthopapatteH yuktaM dvirUpadhyAnamiti || 3 ||

|| OM sarvAbhedAdanyatreme OM || 4 || 

atra pUrvatra sarvaguNadhyAnAdhyAnAyoravirodhoktau atrAnyataravaiyarthyaM nirasyata iti saN^gatiH | atra jij~nAsApadoktaM pUrvatra prakR^itaM sarvaguNadhyAnaM na kAryamuta kAryamiti chintA | tadarthaM tasya phalAtishayavattvanirNayo na sambhavatyuta sambhavatIti | tadarthaM tannirNAyakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | mokSharUpaphalasyAsarvadhyAnenApi siddheH sarvaguNadhyAnasya asarvaguNadhyAnasAdhyaphalAtishayavattvanirNayasya cha nirNAyakAbhAvenAyogAt.h vyarthaM tanna kAryamiti | siddhAntastu | sarvaguNadhyAnamasarvaguNadhyAnAdadhikaphalavat.h tato mahattvAt.h | yatsAdhanaM yato mahat.h tattato.adhikaphalavat.h yathA agniShyomAdito vAjapeyAdikamityanumAnena "sampUrNopAsanAdbrahmA sampUNarAnandabhAgbhavet.h' ityAdi(pAdma)smR^ityA cha phalAtishayavattvaniNaryopapatteH kAryameva sarvaguNadhyAnamiti || 4 ||

|| OM AnandAdayaH pradhAnasya OM || 5 ||

pUrvoktAdhikAribhedena phalabhedena cha dvirUpopAstirayuktA sarvamumukShusAdhAraNopAstimAtrAnirNaye tadvisheShAnavasarAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | jij~nAsApadoktaM bhagavadvayAkhyAnaM na yuktamuta yuktamiti chintA | tadarthaM sarvamumukShudhyeyaguNanirNayo na sambhavatyuta sambhavatIti | tadarthaM sarvadhyeyaguNAH saN^khayAnirdeshAbhyAM kl.hptAH pR^ithaksanti guNAH | yadi bhaveyuH tarhi kiyantaH | yadi chatuHpaJNchaShAH AnandAdaya ityuchyeta tarhi keShAJNchitsamuchchaye.anyeShAmapi samuchchayaprasaN^gena niyamAsambhavAt.h | AnandAdibhyo.anya evetyapi vaktuM shakyatvena eta evetinirdeshakl.hptyabhAvAchcheti sarvamumukShudhyeyaguNanirNayAbhAvAnna bhagavaddhayAnaM kAryamiti | siddhAntastu | sarveShAM bahuguNopAsane.ashakyatvAt.h sarvApekShitasya nirdoShAnandAnubhavarUpamokShasya "taM yathA yathopAsate' iti shrutyA tadanuguNopAsanasAdhyatvAchcha nirdoShatvaj~nAnAnandAnAM trayANAmAvashyakatvAt.h AtmatvashabditasvAmitvasya svasambandhAnusmaraNasya bhagavatprItihetutvena "Atmeti tUpagachChanti' (bra.sU.4-1-2) iti vakShyamANadishAvashyakatvAt.h "sachchidAnanda AtmA' (brahmatarka) ityAdismR^iteshcha sadAdayashchatvAra eveti saN^khayAnirdeshAbhyAM kl.hptisambhavena dhyeyaguNanirNayAt.h yuktameva bhagavaddhayAnamiti || 5 || 

|| OM priyashirastvAdyaprAptirupachayApachayau hi bhede OM || 6 ||

chatvAra eveti prAguktaniyamAkShepeNa shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | chatvAra eveti prAguktaniyamo yukta utAyukta iti chintA | tadarthaM "priyameva shiraH' ityAdinA shrutapriyashirastvAdayaH sarvopAsyA uta neti | tadarthaM teShAM sarvAnupAsyatve prAguktaphalaprAptirnAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | priyashirastvAdayo.api sarvApAsyAsteShAM AnandavisheShatvAt.h | AnandAdInAM cha svAbhimataphalAvAptyarthaM sarvopAsyatvokteH anyathA phalAbhAvApAtAt.h | ataH prAguktaniyamo na yukta iti | siddhAntastu | AnandavisheShamAtreNa priyashirastvAdeH sarvopAsyatve savarguNAnAmapi guNachatuShyayavisheShatvasya vaktuM shakyatayA sarveShAM sarvaguNopAstiprasaN^gAttasya cha "darshanAchcha' ityatrokta (bra.sU.3-2-21) AnandashrutisiddhaphalabhedaparilopApattyA aniShyatvena phalabhedasiddhayarthaM guNopAsaneti tAratamyasya cha vAchyatvAt.h "naiva sarvaguNAssarvairupAsyA muktibhedataH' iti (vArAha) smR^iteshcha na sarvopAsyAH priyashirastvAdayaH | nachaivaM phalAbhAvaH | "yathAyogyAn.h guNapUrNAnupAsya phalaM bhavet.h' ityAdishrutyA visheShAnupAsane.api yogyaguNopAsanenaiva muktiphalaprApteravagamAditi noktaniyamabhaN^ga iti || 6 ||

|| OM itaretvarthasAmAnyAt.h OM || 7 ||

pUrvatra yathAyogyAnitishrutyA yogyaguNopAsanenaiva phalaprAptyuktau devAnAM chaturguNAdhikaguNopAsane yogyatAnishchayAsambhavAt.h teShAM adhikaguNopAstirayukteti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | jij~nAsApadoktaM adhikaguNopAsanaM na kAryamuta kAryamiti chintA | tadarthaM tadadhikAriNAM devAnAM yogyatAniyamanirNayo.ashakya uta shakya iti | tadarthaM prApteshchetyatroktaM dhyAnakAlInaguNabhAnasya yogyatAnirNAyakatvamayuktamuta yuktamiti | pUrvapakShastu | dhyAnAtpUrvameva yogyatAniyamAj~nAne.ayogyopAsanaprasaN^gAttasya cha "achetanAsatyAyogyAnyanupAsyAnyaphalatvaviparyayAbhyAm.h' iti sAN^karShaNasUtroktadishA anarthaphalatvena dhyAkAlInaguNabhAnasya yogyatAnirNAyakatvAbhAvAnnAdhikopAsanaM kAyarmiti | siddhAntastu | tattatprApyaphalApekShayopAsanayogyatAnirNayopapatteH bhAvyutkarShaj~nasarvaguruNA tattatprApyabhaviShyatphalAnusAriguNopadeshopapatteshcha chaturbhyodhikopAsanaM kAryameveti || 7 ||

|| OM AdhyayanAya prayojanAbhAvAt.h OM || 8 ||

|| OM AtmashabdAchcha OM || 

evaM pUrvatra mandamadhyottamAdhikAribhedena anupasaMhAropasaMhArau uktvA tayoH "saMj~nAtashchet.h' iti (bra.sU.3-3-9) "prakaraNabhedAt.h' iti (bra.sU.3-3-8) cha yanmAnamuktaM tadevehAkShipya samAdhIyata iti saN^gatiH | atra jij~nAsApadAbhimatau prAguktaguNopasaMhArAnupasaMhArau na kAryAvuta kAryau iti chintA | tadarthaM tayormAnaM nAstyutAstIti | tadarthaM prAk.h "saMj~nAtaH' iti "prakaraNabhedAt.h' iti choktamubhayatra mAnaM na yuktamuta yuktamiti | pUrvapakShastu | saMj~nAtashchetyatroktadishA sarvavidyAnAM bhagavannAmatvena tatra guNAbhidhAnasya upasaMhArArthatve sarvaguNAnAM ekatraivoktiprasaN^gena vikShipya nAnAsthAneShUkteH vyarthatvAt.h mokShasyAnupasaMhAreNApi siddhayA upasaMhArasya vyarthatvAchcha | ata eva vyarthavidheH ashraddheyatvena "vidhisheShavat.h' (bra.sU.3-3-6) ityatroktavihitatvayukterapyaprayojakatvAt.h tattadvidyAprakaraNeShu etAvadevopAsanamityuktyabhAvena prakaraNabhedasyAnupasaMhAre.amAnatvena mAnAbhAvAnna kAryAvetau dvAviti | siddhAntastu | guNokterupasaMhArAnyaprayojanAbhAvAt.h nAnAsthAneShUktAnAmapi upasaMhAre muktau phalAtishayabhAvena tathokterarthavattvAt.h "AtmatvopAsanavidhAnAt.h prAgevakArasyAyogavyavachChedakatvoktAvapi iha "prApteshcha' ityatrokta (bra.sU.3-3-10) nyAyena adhikAribhedenAvyavachChedakatvAvirodhAchcha dvAvapi kAryAviti || 8 ||

|| OM AtmagR^ihItiritaravattaduttarAt.h OM || 9 ||

""AtmetyevopAsIta' iti pUrvoktashrutisthaivakArasya svAmitvAnyaj~nAnAdiguNavyavachChedakatvaprAptAvatra sa netyuchyata iti saN^gatiH | atra jij~nAsApadAbhimataM "AnandAdayaH' (bra.sU.3-3-12) ityatroktaM chaturguNopAsanaM na yuktamuta yuktamiti chintA | tadartha tatkiM prAguktashrutiviruddhaM naveti | tadarthaM Atmetyeveti prAguktAtmashabdaH kiM sushakatvAdiyuktyA svAmitvamAtravachanaH uta vAkyasheShabalAt.h j~nAnAdichaturguNavachana iti | pUrvapakShastu | AtmatvamAtropAsteH sushakatvAdAshvAparokShyahetutvAchcha sAvadhAraNashrautAtmapadasya svAmimAtravachanatvena tanmAtropAsanasyaiva kAryatvAdayuktaM chaturguNopAsanam.h | vAkyasheShastu stutitvenApyupapadyata iti | siddhAntastu atyalaukikaparamamuparthahetvAparokShye.atisushakatvasyAyuktatvAt.h guNatve.api vA sarveShAM mumukShUNAM "phalasAmyAdapekShitaH' ityAnandanayoktanyAyena (bra.sU.3-3-12) svApekShitaj~nAnAnandAdiphalaprAptyarthatvena anyopAsanasyApyAvashyakatvAt.h vAkyasheShasyArthavAdatve.api aviruddhe svArthe tAtparyAbhAvAt.h | "prANanneva prANanAmA bhavati manvAno manaH' ityAdipUrvavAkye prANapadAdinA prakR^itAnandAdiguNAnAM parAmarshena "atra hyete sarva ekaM bhavanti' (bR^i.3-4-7) ityAtmaguNe AnandAdiguNAnAmantarbhAvoktiparavAkyasheShAnurodhena "AnandAnubhavatvAchcha' ityAdi (bR^ihattantra) smR^ityanurodhena cha Atmashabdasya svAmitvAdichaturgaNavachanatvena tadavirodhAdyuktaM sarvAdhikArikachaturguNopAsanamiti | na chaivamanupasaMhAramAnatvoktivirodhaH asyAnupasaMhArarUpatvAt.h || 9 ||

|| OM anvayAdichetsyAdavadhAraNAt.h OM || 10 || 

atrAtmapadasya prAguktAnupasaMhAramAnatvamAkShipya sAdhyata iti saN^gatiH | atra prAguktamAtmapadasyAnupasaMhAramAnatvamayuktamuta yuktamiti chintA | tadarthamAtmapadoktaguNAH upasaMhartR^imAtropAsyAH utAnupasaMhartrUpAsyA aShIti | tadarthaM Atmashabdo.akhilaguNAnAmapi pratyAyakatvenAnupasaMhartR^In.h prati vibhramakaraH atha vyavasthayA tattadyogyaguNapratyAyakatayA nirNayakAra iti | pUrvapakShastu | AtmetyevopAsItetyasya "chodanAdyavisheShAt.h' (bra.sU.3-3-1) iti nyAyena akhilaguNadhyAtR^ibrahmAdIn.h pratyapi pravR^itteH tatra Atmashabdasya anupasaMhartR^imAtrayogyaguNabodhakatve AtmetyevetyavadhAraNAyogena tadanyathAnupapattyA "AptavyApterAtmashabdaH paramasya prayujyate' iti smR^ityA cha Atmashabdasya sarvaguNavAchitvenAnupasaMhartR^In.h chaturguNAdyupAsakAn.h prati tattadyogyamAtraguNApratyAyakatayA tasya vibhramakaratvAt.h taduktaguNAnupasaMhartR^ibhiranupAsyA ityayuktamanupasaMhAramAnatvam.h | nacha tasya sarvaguNapratyAyakatve.api svasvayogyaguNamAtraM sarvairupAsyamiti shaN^kayam.h | AtmetyevetyavadhAraNenAtmashabdasya yAvatpratItaM tAvatopyupAsyatvapratIteH | anyathAvadAraNavirodhAditi | siddhAntastu | Atmashabdasya sarvaguNavAchitve.api tattadguNopAsanayogyAn.h sarvaguNAn.h vaktItyasya tattadanubhavasiddhatvena tasya avibhramakaratayA taduktaguNAnAM sarvopAsyatvAdyuktamanupasaMhAramAnatvamiti || 10 ||

|| OM kAryAkhyAnAdapUrvam.h OM || 11 ||

pUrvatrAdhikAriNAM svasvayogyaguNAnyaguNAnAmAtmashabdenApratItyA tattanmAtraguNopAsanaM yuktamityuktamayuktam.h | yogyAnAmapi "paramataH' (bra.sU.3-2-32) ityuktadishA.alaukikatvena AtmashabdenApratIteriti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | Ishvare guNA dhyeyA ityuktam.h | te hi laukikA eva dhyeyA utAlaukikA iti chintA | tadatharM laukikAnAmadhyAne guNadhyAnasyaivAbhAvaH prasajyata uta neti | tadarthaM alaukikaguNAnAmanubhavo na sambhavatyuta sambhavatIti | pUrvapakShastu | alaukikaguNaviShaye pratyakShAnumAnayoraprasakteH prasaktasya cha shabdasya saN^gatigrahaNasApekShatvAt.h tasya cha sambandhij~nAnAdhInatvAt.h shabdarUpasambandhinaH pratyakShatve.api artharUpasambandhinaH shabdAdanyenApratIteH shabdAntareNa tatpratItau tatrApyevamityanavasthApattyA saN^gatigrahaNAyogena shabdenApyanubhavayogena dhyAnakAle tatpratIterabhAvAt.h tAdR^ishasya cha dhyAnAyogAt.h laukikAnAmadhyAne guNadhyAnasyaivAbhAvaprasaktyA dhyAnasAdhyAparokShaj~nAnajanmano.abhAvApAtena guNadhyAnasyAvashyakatvAt.h laukikA eva dhyeyAH | tathA chAvidyamAnadhyAnasya "na pratIke na hi saH' (bra.sU.4-1-3) iti chaturthAdyapAde nirasiShyamANatvena Ishvare dhyeyAnAM guNAnAM laukikatvasya vAstavatvAvashyaMbhAvAt.h "paramatassetUnmAna' iti sUtre bhagavadguNAnAmuktAlaukikatvamayuktamiti | siddhAntastu | alaukikAstasya guNAhyupAsyAH' iti shrutau mokShasyAlaukikatvakathanAt.h tAdR^ishamokShasya chAlaukikaguNopAsanena vinA.ayogAt.h "arthasAmAnyAt.h' (bra.sU.3-3-14) ityuktanyAyena phalAnusAridhyAnasya kartavyatayA alaukikA eva guNA dhyeyAH | nacha tAdR^ishaguNApratItirdoShaH | "shAstrovastunashchaiva vyutpattiH shAstraliN^gataH' ityabhimAninayAnuvyAkhyAnasudhayoruktarItyA "yaH sahasrAkShaH sa indraH yaH pAshahastaH sa varuNa ityAdau vAkyArthamaryAdayopasthite vastuni indrAdishabdasya vyutpattivadanukUlavedanIyo bhagavadguNo yaH saH Ananda iti sAkShAtkR^iteshuNAnAM viduShAmupadeshenopasthitau tatra tatpadashaktigrahopapattyA shabdenaitatpratItisambhAt.h prAguktaguNAnAmalaukikatvA yuktamiti || 11 ||

|| OM samAna evaM chAbhedAt.h OM || 12 ||

|| OM sambandhAdevamanyatrApi OM || 

arthasAmAnyAdityukta (bra.sU.3-3-14) nyAyena pUrvatrApUrvakAryAkhyAnAdapUvarguNajAtadhyAnaM kAryamityuktamayuktam.h | dhyAnasya svAnusAriphaladatvAniyamAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atra "arthasAmAnyAt.h' iti prAguktadhyAnasya phalAnusAritvaM nAstyutAstIti | tadarthaM tayoH samaviShamaphalavatoH upAsanamapi samaviShamarUpaM na sambhavatyuta sambhavatIti | tadarthaM 
trivikramatvAdikriyAvisheShANAM brahmabrahmANIbhyAM yathAkramamupAsyAnupAsyatve na yukte uta yukta iti | pUrvapakShastu | trivikramatvAdikriyAvisheShANAmanityatvena dhyAnakAle.abhAvAdavidyamAnasya cha ninditatvena brahmANIbrahmaNorapi kriyAvisheShAnupAsanasya vAchyatvena guNaviShaye sAmyasya kriyAvisheShaviShaye vaiShamyasya durvachanatvena prakArAntareNa brahmANIbrahmabhyAM kriyamANopAsanayoH samatvasya viShamatvasya chAbhAvena samaviShamatvAyogAt.h tadubhayaprApyaphalasya sthAnaikyaguNatAratamyarUpatayA samaviShamatvena tAbhyAM kriyamANopAsanasya svasadR^ishaphalAnusAritvAbhAvAdarthasAmAnyAdityuktamayuktamiti | siddhAntastu | "guNakriyAdayo viShNoH svarUpaM nAnyadiShyate' iti tattvanirNayodAhR^ita(tR^itIyaparichChede) shrutyA guNakriyAdInAM viShNunA tAdAtmyarUpasambandhena nityatayA dhyAnakAle asattvAbhAvena tadupAsane brahmaNo.asadupAsanAprasakteH | kriyAdivisheShaNAmalaukikatve.api "guNAstraivikramAdyAshcha saMhartavyA na saMshayaH | viriJNchasyaiva nAnyeShAm.h' iti (bR^ihattantra) smR^ityA viriJNchasyaiva yogatvena teShAM brahmopAsyatvavat.h brahmANyA nityavikrAntyAdikriyAntarbhAvenaivopAsyatayA pR^ithagupAsyatvAbhAvena kriyAviShaye viShamatvasya guNAdiviShaye samatvasya cha sambhavena brahmANIbrahmabhyAM kriyamANopAsanasyApi phalasyaiva samaviShamatvena kvApyupAsane phalAnusAritvasya vyabhichArAbhAvAt.h arthasAmAnyAdityuktaM yuktamiti || 12 ||
