|| OM navA visheShAt.h OM || 13 ||

|| OM darshayati cha OM || 

"AtmetyevopAsIta' ityAtmapadoktaguNopAsanasyAvashyakatvAdAtmapadena cha brahmANyabhimataguNebhyo nyUnaguNokterapi sambhavena sarvaguNAnAM kriyAsamanvayasya cha uktaniyamAbhAvAt.h brahmANyAH prAguktasarvaguNopasaMhAraM kriyAsAmAnyopasaMhArashchAyukta iti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atrAtmashabdasya "AtmashabdAchcha' ityatroktaM (bra.sU.3-3-16) anupasaMhAramAnatvaM na yuktamuta yuktamiti chintA | tadarthaM AtmashabdoktAH guNAH na sarvopAsyA iti | tadarthaM tasya guNAbhidhAyakatve.api adhikAriNaM prati tattadyogyaguNAbhidhAyakatvamapi prAguktaM na yuktamuta yuktamiti | tadarthaM tattadupAsanAyogyaguNamAtrAbhidhAyakatvaniyamo na sambhavatyuta sambhavatIti | pUvarpakShastu | Atmashabdo brahmANaM prati sarvAnIshvaradharmAn.h brahmANIM prati asheShaguNAn.h kriyAsAmAnyAni anyAMshcha prati tadupAsanAyogyaguNAneva tannyUnAdhikAn.h vaktIti pratisvikaniyamAbhAvena prAguktatattadadhikAriyogyaguNAbhidhAyakatvasya "anvayAt.h' ityatroktasyAyogAt.h (bra.sU.3-3-17) na sarvopAsyA AtmashabdoktA guNA ityanupasaMhAramAnatvamAtmashabdAchchetyatroktamayuktamiti | siddhAntastu | Atmashabdasya sarvaguNoktishaktasyApi tattadyogyaguNapratyAyakatvAnnyUnAdhikasambhave.api tattadadhikArisAmarthyavashena Atmashabdena yasya yAvanto guNAH pratIyante tatra tAvanto dhyeyA iti vyavasthAsambhavAt.h "sarvAn.h guNAn.h' itibhAShyokta(bhAllaveya) shrutibalAchchAtmashabdoktaguNAH sarvopAsyA eveti yuktamanupasaMhAramAnatvamiti || 13 ||

|| OM sambhR^itidyuvyAptyapi chAtaH OM || 14 ||

atra "ukShA sa dyAvA pR^ithivI' (R^i.10-31-7) "eShahi sarveShu lokeShu bhAti' iti (ChAM.4-15-4) shrutasambhR^ityAdiguNasya sarvopAsyatvashaN^kAyAM prAguktAdhikArivisheSheNa siddhAntakaraNAtsaN^gatiH | atra "AnandAdayaH' (bra.sU.3-3-12) ityatroktaM chaturguNopAsanaM na yuktamuta yuktamiti chintA tadarthaM sambhR^itidyuvyAptI sarvopAsye uta neti | tadarthaM guNopAstau tajjanyaphalApekShaiva heturuta yogyatAvisheSho.apIti | pUrvapakShastu | sarveShAM mumukShUNAM mokShe j~nAnAnandAderiva svAvarasambharaNasya prakAshavyApterapekShitatvAt.h phalApekShayA eva cha tatsAdhanAnuShThAne niyAmakatvAt.h yogyatAvisheShasya hetutve vA savareShAmapi yogyatAvisheShasya sattve.api virodhAbhAvAt.h tadabhAve vA sAdhanAnuShThonana tadanuguNaphalaprAptivirodhAchcha apekShitasambharaNAdiphalasya "yAdR^isho bhAvitaH shrIshastAdR^isho jIva Abhavet.h' iti (bhAga.tR^itIyaskandhatAtparya) smR^ityA arthasAmAnyAdityuktanyAyena sambhR^ityAdiguNavishiShyatayA bhagavadupAsanenaiva prApyatvAchcha sarvopAsye eva sambhR^itidyuvyAptI | nachaivaM "sarvaguNA api' iti shaN^kayaM sarveShAM sarvaguNApekShAbhAvAt.h | ato na yuktaM sarveShAM chatvAra eva guNA upAsyA iti | siddhAntastu | phalApekShAyA eva 
tatsAdhanAnuShThAne niyAmakatve traivarNiketareShAmapi svargahetuyAgAdyanuShThAnAtphalaprAptiprasaN^gena "anyathA anarthakR^idbhavet.h' itibhAShyokta(brahmatarka)smR^itAvayogyAnuShThAnasyAnarthaphalalatvoktyA cha yogyatAvisheShasyaiva niyAmakatvAttasya cha "devAdInAmupAsyAstu bhR^itivyAptyAdayo guNAH' iti (brahmatarka) smR^ityA devAdInAmeva bhAvena sarveShAmabhAvAt.h na sarvopAsye sambhR^itidyuvyAptI kintu dovopAsye iti yuktaM prAguktaM chaturguNopAsanam.h | apekShitaM prakAshAdimAtraM tu bhagavadrUpapratItyavinAbhUtaprakAshAdinaiva labhyamiti || 14 ||  N.M-10


|| OM puruShavidyAyAmapi chetareShAmanA nAnAt.h OM || 15 ||

evaM iyatA granthena suranaraviriJNchirUpamadhyamAdhamottamAdhikAriNAM bahvalpasarvaguNadhyAnAya trividhairapi svasvayogyaguNA itastataH upasaMhAryA iti yatsiddhaM tadayuktam.h | ekaikatraiva vidyAyAM tattadyogyaguNoktisambhavAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atra "sarvavedAnta' naye (bra.sU.3-3-1) trividhAdhikAriNAM yathAshaktiyatsarvaparij~nAnamuktaM tadayuktamuta yuktamiti chintA | tadatharM teShAM svasvayogyaguNAnAmupAsanasya itastato nopasaMhAryA utopasaMhAryA iti | tadarthaM svasvayogyaguNA ekaikatra vidyAyAmA nAyante atha neti | tadarthamekaikatra tattadyogyaguNAnAmanuktij~nApakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | ekaikatra tattadyogyaguNA nochyante ityatra j~nApakAbhAvena ekaikatraiva tattadapekShitaguNoktisambhavena tanmAtraparij~nAnenApi svasvayogyadhyAnaviShayaguNAnAM buddhayArUDhasambhavena kR^ityAbhAvAt.h na itastato dhyeyapuMguNA upasaMhAryA iti trayANAM yathAshaktisarvaparij~nAnaM yuktamiti | siddhAntastu | "sarvataH pauruShe sUkte' iti bhAShyokta (brahmatarka) smR^ityA sarvavidyottamapuruShasUktavidyAyAmapi kaimutyasiddhatvena uttamAdhikAriNAM sarvato guNopasaMhArasyAvashyakatvAt.h madhyamAdhikAriNAmapi mahadalpaguNAbhidhAyakavidyAsu saN^khayAsAmyasambhave.api svasvAbhimataguNAnAmekaikatraivoktiniyamAbhAvAt.h itastataH kAyar evopasaMhAraH iti yuktaM sarveShAM yathAshaktisarvaparij~nAnamiti || 15 ||

|| OM vedhAdyarthabhedAt.h OM || 16 ||

pUrvatra itastato.apekShitaguNopasaMhArasya sarvaiH kartavyatvaprasaktau satyAM vedhAdiguNopasaMhAro.apyapekShitaphalahetutvAt.h savaraiH kAryeti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atra "AnandAdayaH' ityatroktaH pUrvanaye prasaktaH sarveShAM chaturguNopAstiniyamo na yukta uta yukta iti chintA | tadarthaM "taM pratyaMchamarchiShA.a.avidhya marman.h' (R^i.10-87) ityAdishrutyukto vedhAdiguNaH kiM sarvopAsyo.atha neti | tadarthaM tatphale.apekShAyogyatve staH uta neti | pUrvapakShastu | vedhAdibhagavadguNopAsanAphalasya duShyajananigrahasya sarvasajjanAnAmapekShitatvAt.h "prANastvA vaMsho hAsyatItyenaM brUyAt.h' (ai.3-1-4) | "AtatAyinamAyAntaM hanyAdevAvichArayan.h' iti shrutismR^ityoH vihitatvena yogyatAvattvasyApyavagamAchcha vedhAdeH sarvopAsyatvAtprAguktaniyamo na yukta iti | siddhAntastu | "bhindhi viddhi shruNIhi' iti (bR^ihattantra) smR^itau vedhAdiguNopAstiphalasya yatiprApyaphalAdvilakShaNaphalatvoktipUrvaM yatInAM tatrAyogyatvasyoktatvAt.h | tata eva tatrApekShAyA apyayogAt.h | na sha noShIti mAmAttha hAsyatastvAmato hi tau | j~nAnasAmarthyAvAnitthaM brUyAddevAdiruttamaH' (ai.bhAShya. 3-1-4) iti smR^ityA devaviShayatvena smR^iteshcha kShatriyaparatvena cha sarveShAM yogyatvAnirNAyakatvAt.h yogyatApekShayorabhAve tannibandhanavedhAdiguNopAsteH abhAvasiddheryuktaH prAguktaniyama iti || 16 ||

|| OM hAnautUpAyanashabdasheShatvAtkushAchChaMdastutyupagAnavattaduktam.h OM || 17 ||

|| OM sAmparAye tartavyAbhAvAttathAhyanye OM || 

evamatItairnayaiH trividhAdhikAriNAmupAsanopayuktatattadyogyaguNopasaMhAro nirNItaH | itaH paraM upAsanAyAH phalanaiyatyayogyatAtAratamyAdhikAreyattAgurupradAnAdItikartavyatAdikaM nirUpayituM atropAsanAyAH nirupAdhikatvarUpasvabhAva 
uchyate iti saN^gatiH | yadarthaM pUrvaM guNopasaMhAro nirNItaH yasmAchcha atharsAmAnyAdityuktasvasadR^ishaphalatvaM "samAna evaM cha' ityatra (bra.sU.3-3-20) samarthitaM sopAsanA muktena na kriyata uta kriyata iti chintA | tadarthaM muktena kriyata ityatra pramANaM nAstyutAstIti | tadarthaM "etatsAmagAyannAste' iti (tai.3-10) shrutiH gauNamuktiparA uta paramamuktipareti | tathA kriyate ityatrApi kiM vidhyAdyupAdhInA kriyate atha kushAchchandastutyupagAnavadIshvarakriyAvat.h svechChayA lIlarUpatayeti chintA | tadatharM upAsanAvidhInAM mukte.api pravR^ittirastyuta neti | tadatharM muktau prAptavyaphalamastyuta neti | muktasya niShkriyatvena sAmagAyanAdikriyAyogena "etatsAmagAyannityAdeH gauNamuktiparatvena muktAvupAsanAstitve mAnAbhAvAt.h | na chAphalasya karaNAyogena saphalatvopagame.apUrNatAprasaN^gena cha muktena upAsanA na kriyate iti prApte "sa ya evaM vidasmAllokAtpretya' iti pUrvavAkye brahmaj~nAninashvaramadehatyAgamuktvA pashchAdAnandamayanyAyena AnandamayAdibhagavadrUpapaJNchakaprAptiM "etamannamayamAtmAnamupasaN^kramya' ityAdinoktvA A nAtasya "etatsAma' iti vAkyasya gauNamuktiparatvAyogena paramamuktiparatvena pramANasadbhAvAt.h "kR^iShNo muktai rijyate' iti (bhArata) muktasya yajanAdikriyAsattvena kaimutyanyAyAchcha muktenopAsanaM kriyata eveti siddhAnta ityAdyaH pakShaH | dvitIyastu vidhInAM iShyasAdhanatvam.h | tadbodhakAshcha "upAsIta' ityAdi vidhipratyayArthAH | te "brahmavidA noti param.h' iti (tai.2-1) brahmaj~nAnena mokSho bhavatItyukte tatkathamityapekShAyAM tAdarthe pravR^ittA api yathA baddhAn.h prati upAsanaM mokSharUpeShyasAdhanamiti pratyAyayanti evaM muktaM pratyapi AnandAtishayasya prAchInakarmaphalatvasya "agnihotrAdi tu tatkAryAyaiva' iti (bra.sU.4-1-16) vakShyamANatvena tatsAdhanatvabodhanAsambhave.api muktau tadA tadA prAptAniShyaparihArarUpaphalasyeShyasya sambhavena tatsAdhanatAbodhakatvasambhavena mukte.api pravR^ittirasti | anyathA tatkR^iterevAyogAt.h | ato vidhiphalakAmanAdyupAdhinaiva upAsanA kriyata iti prApte "tIrNo hi tadA sarvAn.h shokAn.h hR^idayasya bhavati' (bR^i.6-3-22) ityAdeH muktau sarvAriShyaparihArasya siddhatvena prAptavyAniShyaparihArasyApyabhAvenaiva tatsAdhanatvamAdAyApi iShyasAdhanatvamupAsanasya muktaM prati bodhayitumashakyatvena baddhena muktasya samAnadharmatApattyA cha mukte upAsanAvidhInAmapravR^itteH | vidhiphalakAmanayorabhAve.api niyatabrahmayaj~nAnantaraM kushaiH svechChayA dvijAnAM mantrasAmAdhyayanavat.h IshvarakriyAvachcha svechChayA lIlArUpatayaivopapatteH kriyate muktenopAsaneti | tathA cha smR^itiH "tIrNatartavyabhAgAshcha svechChayopAsate param.h' (vAyuprokta) iti siddhAnta iti | atra prayojanaM pUrvapAdoktabhaktyAkShepasamAdhI | atrAdyamadhikaraNasharIraM bhAShye "etatsAmagAyannAste' iti shrutyuktyA bhavediyaM chintA yadi muktasya upAsanameva syAttadeva kutaH iti TIkayA muktau upAsanabhAve phalAdikamapi syAditi nyAyavivaraNena cha sUchitam.h | dvitIyaM tu muktasyopAsanA kartavyA navetyAdi bhAShyAdineti j~neyam.h | TIkAyAM tu bhAShyavivaraNayorekavAkyatAsampAdanAya vyAmishreNa nirUpaNaM kR^itamityavirodhaH | yadvA muktenopAstiH na kriyate kriyate veti chintA | tadarthaM muktAvupAstibhAve sAdhakaM nAstyatha viparItamiti | tadarthaM muktasya vidhiviShayatvAdikaM bAdhakaM bhavatyuta neti | pUrvapakShastu | muktasyopAsanAvattve mAnAbhAvena vidhibaddhatvena vA tadabaddhatvena vA ubhayathApyupAsanAbhAve phalaprAptyA apUrNatAprasaN^gena Adye saMsArisamAnadharmApattyA antye avihitakaraNasyaivAyogena bAdhakena muktenopAsanA na kriyata iti | siddhAntastu | etatsAmagAyannityAdi sAdhakabhAvena upAsanAvidhInAM mokShavAkyasheShatayA muktyarthatvena muktasya tadaviShayatve.api kushAchChandastutyupagAnavatsvechChayaivAnandavR^iddheH prAchInanivR^ittakarmaphalatvena sarvAniShyanivR^itteH prAptatvena prApyaphalAbhAve.api IshvarakriyAvanmuktasya lIlAtvenopAsanAkriyAyAH svabhAvopapatteH bAdhakAbhAvena cha muktenopAsanA kriyata ityekarUpeNaiva pUrvottarapakShau dhyeyau || 17 ||

|| OM Chandata ubhayavirodhAt.h OM || 18 ||

|| OM gaterarthavattvamubhayathA.anyathA hi virodhaH OM || OM upapannastallakShaNArthopalabdherlokavat.h OM || 

upAsanAprasaN^gasannidhApitaM karmApyupAsanAvanmuktau niyatameveti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | pUrvatra prakR^itA muktAH kimupAsanavanniyamena karma kurvantyuta neti chintA | tadarthaM niyamena tadanuShThApakamastyuta neti | tadarthaM shaktatvAdyevAnuShThApakamuta vidhyAdivattvamaShIti | pUrvapakShastu | sAdhanAnuShThAne hi tajjanyaphalArthitve sati shaktatvaM prayojakam.h | muktAnAM cha prAptaphalatvenArthitvAbhAve.api siddhavaiduShyANAM svechChayopAsanAnuShThAnavat.h karma karaNe.api shaktisadbhAvAtkarmaNo bhagavatpUjArUpatvAchcha anuShThApakasadbhAvAtkarmApi 
niyamena kuvarntyeva | anyeShAM tasyAnanuShThApakatve upAsanamapi niyamena na kuryuH avisheShAditi | siddhAntastu | karmaNo bhagavatpUjAtmakatve.api muktAnAM tadanuShThAnashaktatve.api na tAvanmAtraM niyamenAnuShThAne hetuH | kiM tu vihitatvaM akaraNe pratyavAyavatvaM aprAptaphalatvaM cha | na chaitatsarvaM muktAnAmapi mokShasyApumarthatvaprasaN^gena vidhyAderabhAvAtprAptaphalatvAchcha teShAm.h | ato niyamena na karma kurvanti kintu bhagavatpUjAtvAt.h pUrvAnuShThAnavAsanAbalAchcha kadAchideva kurvanti | upAsanaM tu pUrvaniyamenAnAratamanuShThAnena tadvAsanAbalAnnityaj~nAnasvarUpAchcha niyamenAnutiShThanti | "kadAchitkarma kuvarnti kadAchinnaiva kurvate | nityaj~nAnasvarUpatvAnnityaM dhyAyanti keshavam.h' (brahmANDa) iti smR^iteriti || 18 ||

|| OM aniyamaH sarveShAmavirodhAchChabdAnumAnAbhyAm.h OM || 19 ||

pUvarM j~nAnadvArA karmaphalasya mokShasya prAptatvAnna karmAnuShThAnanaiyatyamityuktau tarhi j~nAninAM sarveShAM phalaprAptiruta keShAJNchideveti chintanAtsaN^gatiH | yadvA upAsanAvidhInAM j~nAnadvArA mokShavAkyasheShatvamupAyanashabdasheShatvAdityatra uktamayuktam.h | satyapi j~nAne keShAJNchinmokShAbhAvAdityAshayenAtrashaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | pUrvanayasya tu prAsaN^gikatvAt.h na vyavadhAyakatvam.h | tallakShaNArthopalabdheH' (bra.sU.3-3-13) ityAdau pUrvatrArthapadena prakR^ito mokShaH kiM keShAJNchideva j~nAninAM j~nAninAM prApya uta sarveShAM j~nAninamiti chintA | tadarthaM j~nAniShvapi upAsane yogyAyogyavibhAgo.astyuta neti | tadarthaM j~nAniShvapi yogyAyogyavibhAgabhAve j~nApakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | keShAJNchideva j~nAninAM mokSho na sarveShAm.h | j~nAniShvapi keShuchidayogyatvasambhavAt.h | "kAmaM bhavema vR^ijinairnirayeShu naShyAshcheto.alivadyarhi te padayo rameta' iti (bhAga.3-16-49) tR^itIyaskandhe kR^imArokteH | ayogyAnAM cha mokShasyopAsakeShvayogyAnAM sarvaguNopasaMhArasyevAprApyatvAt.h | na chopAsakeShu sarvaguNopasaMhArayogyajanavat.h j~nAniShu muktayogyajano nAstyeva | prAguktakumoroktistu bhagavatpAdaratistutipareti vAchyam.h | sarvaguNopasaMhArayogyAyogyavibhAgo.asti j~nAniShu nAstItyatra j~nApakAbhAvAditi | siddhAntastu | sarveShAmeva j~nAninAM mokSho na keShAJNchideveti niyamaH "sarvairguNairbrahmaNaiva hyupAsyo nAnyaiH' iti niShedhabalenopasaMhAre yogyAyogyavibhAgasattve.apIha j~nAniShu keShAJNchinmuktiniShedhAbhAvena pratyuta "na kashchidbrahmavitsR^itimanubhavati mukto hyeSha bhavati' iti (kauNDiNyashrutiH) sarvaj~nAninAM muktinaiyatyavachanena vimatA j~nAnino niyatamokShAH j~nAnitvAtsammataj~nAnivaditi nirbAdhashrutimUlAnumAnena cha j~nAniShvayogyAbhAvanishchayAtsarvaj~nAniprApyo mokSha iti tatsAdhanopAsanaM niHshaN^kaM kAryameva | yuktaM chopAyanasheShatvaM taddhidhInAmiti || 19 ||

|| OM yAvadadhikAramavasthitirAdhikArikANAm.h OM || 20 ||

|| OM akSharadhiyAM tvavirodhaH sAmAnyataddhAvAbhyAmaupasadavattaduktam.h OM ||

yadyevamaniyamena j~nAnino mokShaH tarhi akiJNchitkaro.asau yogyatAvisheShaH tatprayojakaphalatAratamyasyAnyenaivopapatteriti pUrvoktatarkapratihatashaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH| yeShAmupAsakAnAM j~nAnaprAptau satyAM mokShanaiyatyaM prAguktaM tadupAsakAH kiM yogyatAtAratamyavanto uta na tadvanta iti chintA | tadatharM tatra pramANaM nAstyutAstIti | tadarthaM muktAvAnandAditAratamyaM sAdhakaM nAsti bAdhakaM chAsti atha viparItamiti | pUvarpakShastu | "vR^iddhihrAsabhAktvam.h' iti naye (bra.sU.3-2-20) dasharnAchchetiguNasUtropAttayA "athAta Anandasya mImAMsA bhavati' ityAdishruteH saMsAriparatvena muktAvAnandatAratamye mAnAbhAvAt.h dveSherShyAdiprasaN^garUpabAdhakAchcha muktau tAratamyamevAyuktam.h | yuktaM chedapi kR^iShyAdiprayatnatAratamyena dhAnyAdiphalatAratamyavadupAsanAdiprayatnatAratamyenaivopapAdyate iti tasya yogyatAtAratamyAprayojakatvena pamANAbhAvAnnopAsakAH yogyatAtAratamyavantaH iti | siddhAntastu | "nAnAvidhA devasaN^ghA vimuktau' ityAdi visheSha(tura) shrutyA "narAdibrahmaparyantaM vimuktAnAM shatochChrayaH | apyAnande mithopyuktastvadhvaryUNAM shrutau pR^ithak.h' iti smR^ityA cha AnandashruteramuktaviShayatvAyogena muktau tAratamye pramANAbhAvAt.h viShayalampaTatvamatsarAdidoShitvAnupakAritvAnAmeva leke dveSherShyAdiprayojakatvasya dR^iShyatvena dveSherShyAdinimittaviShayalampaTatvAdeH brahmaj~nAnitayA mukteShvabhAvAt.h uttamebhyo.adhamAnAM j~nAnAdilakShaNopakArabhAvena anupakAritvAbhAvAt.h bAdhakAbhAvAchcha yuktameva muktau tAratamyam.h | tattu prAchInayogyatAtAratamyena vinA.anupapadyamAnaM 
yogyatAtAratamyaM gamayet.h | nachopAsanAdiprayatnatAratamyenAnyathopapattiH | "svAdhikArAdhiko yatnaH prAyasho nopapadyate | kathaMchidadhike yatne doShaH kashchitsamApatet.h' iti vachanena prayatnatAratamyasyApi yogyatAtAratamyanibandhanAt.h | ato yogyatAtAratamyavanta evopAsakA iti | phalaM tu prApteshchetyatroktayogyatAbhedasamarthanam.h || 20 ||

|| OM j~nayadAmananAt.h OM || 21 || 

|| OM antarA bhUtagrAmavaditi chettaduktam.h OM || OM anyathA bhedAnupapattiriti chennopadeshavat.h OM || 

prAguktayogyatAniyamasya niravadhikatvamAshaN^kaya sAvadhikatvarUpavisheShachintanAtsaN^gatiH | ChAndogye saptame nAmAvAN^.hmanassaMkalpachittadhyAnavij~nAnabalAnnAptejaAkAshasmarAshAprANashabditAH uShAsvAhA parjanyamitrAgnivaruNavidyutpravAhAniruddhAhaMkArikaprANendromArudravANImArutAMtadevatAH uttarottaramAdhikyenoktAH | pUrvatrAdhikAripadena prakR^itAste upAsanAdhikAravantaH kiM mukhyaprANAvadhikA na bhavanti uta tadavadhikA eveti chintA | tadarthaM prANAdadhikAdhikArisAdhakamanumAnaM "prANo vA sarvebhyo bhUyAnna prANAdbhUyAniti shrutibAdhitaM na bhavatyuta bhavatIti | tadarthaM shrutau sarvashabdaH kiM paramAtmAnyapara iva adhikAryantarAnyaparatayApi saMkuchadvR^ittiH sambhavatyuta neti | pUrvapakShastu | "prANo vAva sarvebhyaH' ityatra sarvashabdasyAsaMkuchadvR^ittitve mukhyaprANya nirupacharitasarvottamatvaprAptyAsarvottamavastudvayAyogena shrutyAdisiddhasarvottamatAkaviShNvabhede vAchye "chakShurAdivat.h' ityAdau (bra.sU.3-4-11) bhAShyoktAnekamAnasiddhaprANaparamAtmabhedAbhAvaprasaN^gabAdhakena tadanyaparatvena saN^kuchadvR^ittitve.avashyaM vAchye adhikArivisheShavyatiriktaparatvenApi saMkoche bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | tathA cha tasyAH shruteH prANaH svottamAdhikAriyuktaH adhikAritvAt.h nAmAdivadityanumAnabAdhakatvena tadabAdhitAdasmAdanumAnAt.h prANAdapyuttamAdhikArisiddheH upAsanAdhikAriNo na mukhyaprANAvadhikA iti | siddhAntastu | sarvashabdasyAnekamAnabalena bhagavadanyatra saMkuchadvR^ittitve.api chakShurAdivattvityAdau tatratatra bhAShyoktavachanaiH "uttamatvaM hi devAnAm.h' ityAdi (uttarAdhikaraNe) vakShyamANabhAShyavachanaishcha prANAddharerevottamatvapratipAdanaparaiH tadanusAriNyAH bhagavanmAtravyatiriktaparatvena saMkuchadvR^ittikasarvashabdopetaprAguktashrutyA cha bAdhitatvena anumAnasyApramANatvAt.h prANAvadhikA evopAsakA iti | phalaM tu sarvaguNopasaMhArasya brahmAdhikArikatvoktisamarthanam.h || 21 ||

|| OM vyatihAro vishiMShati hItaravat.h OM || 22 ||

pUrvatra prANasyaiva hiraNyagarbhatvAt.h tasya prAguktassarvaguNopasaMhAro yukta ityaktamayuktam.h | tasyaiva savarottamatvenAnyasya tadupAsyasyAbhAvAditi shaN^kAnAdvA upAsanAdhikAriNo nirUpyopAsyamiha nirUpyata iti vA saN^gatiH | pUrvatra prANAduttamatvena prakR^ito viShNuH kiM prANAnnottamaH athottama iti chintA | tadarthaM ChAndogye "prANo vA AshAyA bhUyAn.h' ityA nAnAt.h (ChAM.7-15-1) prANAdupari "satyaM tveva vijij~nAsitavyam.h' (ChAM.7-16-1) ityA nAtaH sarvottamaH satyanAmakaH kiM prANAdananya utAnyo viShNuriti chintA | tadarthaM prANaprakaraNAt.h satyaprakaraNasya bhedakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | nAmAdiprANaparyantAnAM paJNchadashaprakaraNAnAM bhedakasya prashnaprativachanabhAvasyeveha "asti prANAdbhUyaH iti prashnasya "satyaM vAva prANAdbhUyaH' iti prativachanasya prANasatyaprakaraNabhedakasyAbhAvena prANasatyayoranyatvAnna satyashabdArthabhUtaH san.h viShNuH prANAduttamaH | na cha prakaraNabhedakayoH prashnaprativachanayoradhyAhAraH j~nApakAbhAvAditi | siddhAntastu | "sa vA eSha evaM pashyannevaM manvAna evaM vijAnannativAdI bhavati' iti (ChAM.7-15-4) prANavAdino.atishayitavastuvAditvenAtivAditvamuktvA pashchAt.h "eSha tu vA ativadati yaH satyenAtivadati' (ChAM.7-16-1) iti satyasya vastu vadatopyativAditvoktyA prANAtivAdito.api satyativAdinaH tushabdena vyAvartanAt.h j~nApakAt.h prashnaprativachanayoradhyAhAreNa prakaraNavichChedAt.h "uttamatvaM hi devAnAm.h' iti (bR^ihattantra) smR^iteshcha satyanAmA viShNuH prANAduttama iti tushabdo nAdhyAhArakalpakaH "vij~nAnaM tveva' (ChAM.7-17-1) "matistveva' (ChAM.1-18-1) ityAdau vakShyamANadishA bhedahIne.api vastuni shravaNena vyabhichArAditi chodyantu "bhUmaH' naye (bra.sU.1-3-8) nirastam.h | nirAsakaprakArashcha chandrikAyAM vyaktaH | phalaM tvAnandAdaya ityatrokta AtmatvopAsanasamarthanam.h || 
22 ||

|| OM saiva hi satyAdaya OM || 23 ||

atra prAgukte viShNoH prANAduttamatve visheShachintanAtsaN^gatiH | prakR^itAtprANAt.h satyapadokto viShNurevottamaH atha bahavo.apyuttamAH santIti chintA | tadarthaM satyasyopari paThitAnAM vij~nAnamatishraddhAniShThakR^itisukhabhUmAhaMkArAtmanAM navAnAM kiM satyAt.h parasparaM cha bheda utAbheda iti | tadarthaM abhede j~nApakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | satyAdInAmAtmAntAnAM abhede j~nApakAbhAvAt.h shabdAntaranyAyena bhedasyaiva nyAyyatvAt.h prANAtsatyAdayo bahava uttamA iti | siddhAntastu | vij~nAnAdeH satyAditonyatve "satyaM bhagavo vijij~nAsya' (ChAM.7-16-1) ityAdi prashne vij~nAnAderukterasAMgatyApatteH tadanyathAnupapattibalena "satyaM bhagavo vijij~nAsya' ityasya satyaguNajij~nAsAparatve sati satyAvinAbhUtavij~nAnoktiH | evaM "vij~nAnaM bhagavo vijij~nAsya' (ChAM.7-17-1) ityatrApi vij~nAnaguNajij~nAsAyAM tadavinAbhUtaguNoktiparatvena sarveShAmabhedasya nyAyaprAptatvAt.h "satyAdyA ahamantA yadguNAH' ityAdi (adhyAtma)smR^iteshcha teShAmabhedAt.h viShNureva prANAduttama iti || 23 ||

|| OM kAmAditaratra tatra chAyatanAdibhyaH OM || 24 ||

|| OM AdarAdalopaH OM || OM upasthitestadvachanAt.h OM || 

evaM satyAdeH sarvasya viShNutvoktau shriyopyadhikAritvAt.h prANAdUrdhvaM shriyo.apyadhyAhAraH syAt.h | tathAcha prANAvadhitvamadhikArivargasyoktamayuktamiti shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atra prANaviShNusannidhApitA shrIH kimupAsanAyAmadhikArirI atha neti chintA | tadarthaM sA baddhA uta neti | tadarthaM sItAdirUpeNa bhUmau bhavanAdikaM jIvavaddehayogAdirUpajanmAdyeva uta prAdurbhAvAdirUpamiti | tadarthaM shriyo bhagavadarchanaM janmAdihetukarmAdibandhamochananimittaM uta muktavannirupAdhikabhaktyatishayanimittamiti | tadarthaM bhaktinimittatvakalpakaM nAstyutAstIti | pUrvapakShastu | "yadarchitaM brahmabhavAdibhissuraiH shriyA cha devyA munibhishcha sAtvataiH' (bhAgavata.10-33-7) ityAdau shriyo.api bhagavadupAsanA shrUyate | sA chetareShAmiva bhagavatprItidvArA bandhamochanArthA | tasyAH kR^itakR^ityatve tadayogAt.h | bhaktyatishayanimittatve kalpakAbhAvAt.h | anyathA sAttvataprabhR^itInAmapi sA tadarthA na syAt.h | evaM cha tadbalAtsItArukmiNyAdirUpeNa bhavanatirodhAnAdeH karmAdhInadehopAdAnatyAgarUpatvena itarajIvavat.h baddhatvAvagamAt.h baddhatve sati sAdhutvAchcha adhikAriNI evopAsanAyAM shrIriti | siddhAntastu | sarvAyatanetyAdibhAShyoktashrutyAdibalena nityaM bhagavatsambandhitvena atishayitatatprasAdAt.h nityamuktatvAvagamAt.h tadbalena bhUmau bhavanAdeH IshechChAdhInasvechChAmAtrahetukatayA prAdurbhAvarUpatvena kamarAdhInadehayogAdirUpatvAbhAvAvagamena "yathAshrIrnityamuktApi' iti smR^ityA chArchanasya bhaktyatishayanimittatvakalpanAnnAdhikAriNI shrIriti | phalaM tu upAsakAnAM prANAvadhitvasamarthanam.h || 24 ||

|| OM tannirdhAraNArthaniyamastaddR^iShyeH pR^ithagghyapratibandhaH phalam.h OM || 25 ||

pUrvatra shriyaH kR^itArthatA phalAbhAve.api AdarAdupAsanA.alopoktau tarhyakR^itArthAnAM phalAbhAvAt.h shravaNAdisamastopAsanasya lopa eva syAditi shaN^kanAtsaN^gatiH | atra shravaNamananadhyAnarUpatrividhamupAsanaM vyastaM kAryamuta samastamiti chintA | tadarthaM trividhasyApi phalaM nAstyutAstIti | tadarthaM tritayasyApi tatsAdhanatve manopayogau na sta uta sta iti | pUrvapakShastu | upAsanaM hi bhagavaddarshanArthaM "draShyavyaH' shruteH | tasya cha shravaNamananAbhyAM vA dhyAnenaiva vopapattau na tritayasAdhyatve pramANamasti | "draShyavyaH shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH' iti shrutistu vaikalpikasAdhanavidhAnenApyupapannA | kiM cha na tritayasyopayogo.asti | na chAj~nAtaj~nApanena shravaNasya, tanniyamajananena manasya, dR^ishijananena dhyAnasyopayoga iti yuktam.h | tathAcha tritayasyApi pR^ithaktvaphalatvena darshanoddeshena tritayavidhAnAnupapatteH | evaM cha pramANopayegayorabhAve darshanasya 
tritayasAdhyatvAbhAvena phalAbhAvAnna samastopAsanaM kAryamiti | siddhAntastu | "draShyavya' iti shrutau darshanoddeshena tritayasyApi vidhAnAdvikalpadyotakashabdAbhAvena samuchchayasAdhanatAvagamAt.h samuchchitAnAmeva dR^ishirUpaphalahetutritayaM kAryameva | nachopayogAbhAvaH shaN^kayaH | darshanaM prati dhyAnasyaiva hetutve.api dhyAnasya dR^ishijanane.apekShitAyAH pratibandhakAj~nAnasaMshayaviparyayanivR^itteH sampAdanena shravaNamananayorupayogitvAditi | phalaM tu jij~nAsAsUtroktatritayasamarthanam.h || 25 ||

|| OM pradAnavadeva hi taduktam.h OM || 26 ||

pradhAnakartavyatvasiddhau tadaN^gamihanirUpyata iti vA pUrvaM shravaNAditrayasyApi phalamuktaM ihAMgamuchyata iti vA dR^ishi hetordhyAnasya shravaNamananAkhyamaN^gamuktaM iha tritayasyApyaMgamuchyata iti vA saN^gatiH | atra prakR^itashravaNAditrayaM yathAkathaMchidanuShThitaM j~nAnaheturuta prItipUrvakagurUpadeshayuktamiti chintA | tadarthaM tasya tAdR^ishagurUpadeshayuktatvena phalahetutve sAdhakaM nAsti shrutivirodhAdibAdhakaM chAstyuta viparItamiti | pUrvapakShastu | gurUpadeshayuktameva shravaNAdikaM dR^ishiheturityatra pramANAbhAvAt.h pratyuta draShyavya iti shrutau dR^ishyuddeshena shravaNAditrayasyaiva vidhAnena tadvirodharUpasya j~nAnasya guruprasAdAdhInatve j~nAnino.api mokShasya tadadhInatvaprasaMgena kadAchidgurukopena mokShAbhAvasyApyApattyA "aniyamassarveShAm.h' ityukta (bra.sU.3-3-31) bhaMgarUpasya bAdhakasya cha sattvAchcha na gurupradAnayuktaM j~nAnahetuH kiMtu kevalameva shravaNAdikam.h | nacha gurukopo na mokShapratibandhakaH | tathAtve gurupradAnamapi j~nAne.akiMchitkaramiti | siddhAntastu | prItipUrvakagurUpadesharUpAMgayuktameva shravaNAdikaM j~nAnaheturna kevalam.h | "AchAryavAn.h puruSho veda' iti (6-14-2) shrutau j~nAnasya guruprasAdAdhInatvAvagamena tena vinA shravaNAdimAtreNa j~nAnAsiddheH | "samyaglakShaNasampanno yaddadyAtsuprasannadhIH | shiShyAya satyaM bhavati tatsarvaM nAtra saMshayaH' iti "nAtiprasannahR^idayo yaddadyAdgururapyasau | na tatsatyaM bhavettasmAdarchanIyo gurussadA' iti smR^iteshcha | nacha draShyavya iti shrutivirodho bAdhakaH | shravaNAdeH pradhAnasAdhanatvAdgurudAnasya tadaN^gatvAt.h somarasAdhyAyagasya dR^iDhamuShyinipIDanAdhInatve.api tasya tadaN^gatvavat.h j~nAnasya gurupradAnAdhInatve.api tasya j~nAnahetushravaNAdyaN^gatvopapatteH | aN^gasya cha pradhAnasAdhanena saha tulyakakShyatayA vidhAnAbhAve.api dR^iDhamuShyinipIDanAderiva atharAdvachanAntarAdvA prAptatvena pradAnasya draShyavyashrutyanumatatvAt.h | nacha kadAchitkopena j~nAnasya vA j~nAnino mokShasya vA.abhAvApAto bAdhaka iti vAchyam.h | j~nAnamokShayorIshvaraklaptatvena tadabhAvAyogAt.h | gurushApAdeshcha "j~nAnino gurushApepi' ityAdi (nyAyavivaraNodAhR^ita) smR^ityA j~nAnAdihrAsahetutvena sAphalyopapatteriti | phalaM tu itaretvarthasAmAnyAt.h' ityatrokta(bra.sU.3-3-14) gurusApekShatvasya samarthanam.h || 26 ||

|| OM liN^gabhUyastvAttaddhi balIyastadapi OM || 27 || 

pUrvaprakR^itAN^gAN^ginomardhye.atrAN^gasya balavatvasAdhanAtsaN^gatiH | atra shravaNAdisAdhanaM tadaMgagurupradAnaM cheti dvayaM samabalaM utAnyataradbalavaditi chintA | tadarthaM puruShatvasAmyaM gurushiShyaprayatnayoH sAmyApAdakaM bhavatyuta neti | tathAnyataradbalavadityatra shiShyaprayatno balavAnatha gurudAnaM balavaditi chintA | tadarthaM pradAnasya balavattve sAdhakaM nAsti bAdhakaM chAstyathaviparItamiti | pUrvapakShastu | pradAnasya balavattve kvApItikartavyatAyAH sAdhanAdapi prAbalyAdasharnena itikartavyatvabhaN^gaprasaN^gAt.h shravaNAdivaiyarthyaprasaN^gAchcha bAdhakAbhAvAt.h sAdhakAbhAvAchcha na pradAnaM balavat.h kintu shravaNAdyeva pradhAnasAdhanatvAt.h | mAstu vA balavat.h gurushiShyayoH puruShatvAvisheShAt.h gurupradAnaM shiShyaprayatnashcha dvayaM samameva syAt.h | nahi kashchinnyUnAdhikabhAve.api visheSho.astIti | siddhAntastu | na tAvatsAmyaM yuktaM puruShatve gurutvashiShyatvavat.h tatprayatnayorapi nyUnAdhikabhAvasambhavena puruShatvamAtrasyAprayojakatvAt.h nyUnAdhikabhAve pradAnasyaivAdhikyamuktam.h liN^gabAhulyarUpasAdhakabhAvAt.h | hiMsAyAH pApajananashaktAyA api yAgIyahiMsAyAH prokShaNAMjanaparyagnikaraNAdItikartavyatAbalena puNyajanakatvadarshanena tatretikartavyatAyAH prAbalyavat.h atra pradAnasya prAbalye aN^gatvabhaN^gaprasaN^gAbhAvAt.h | shrotavya ityAdi shrutyA "guruprasAdo balavAn.h' ityAdi (vArAha) smR^ityA cha shravaNAderapyAvashyakatvena tadvaiyarthyAbhAvAchcha bAdhakAbhAvAchcheti | liN^gabAhulyaM cha TIkAdau vyaktam.h | phalaM tu setikartavyatvasyaiva shravaNAderj~nAnahetutvarUpaprAguktaprameyasamarthanam.h | anyathA kvachidguroranapekShitatvaprasaN^gena prAguktamayuktaM syAditi || 27 ||

|| OM pUrvavikalpaH prakaraNAtsyAtkriyAmAnasavat.h OM || 28 ||

|| OM atideshAchcha OM || 

yatprasAdo balavAnityuktaM sa gururatra chintyata iti saN^gatiH | atra prakR^ito guruH kiM pUrvaprApta eveti niyamo.athAnyo.api gR^ihItuM shakya iti chintA | tadarthaM pUrvatyAge kAraNaM nAsti bAdhakaM chAsti uta viparItamiti | tathA anyo.api grAhya iti pakShe sa kiM yaH kashchiduta pUrvasmAdanapakR^iShyaH samagrAnugrahakartaiveti | pUrvapakShastu | shubhalAbhArthaM hi gurusvIkAro bhavati | sa cha pUrvaprAptaguruNaiva bhaviShyatIti tattyAge kAraNAbhAvAt.h | "(gurutyAge bhavenmR^ityuH mantratyAge daridratA) gurumantraparityAgI rauravaM narakaM vrajet.h' iti doShashravaNarUpabAdhakAchcha pUvarprApta eva guruH natvanyo.api grAhya iti | anyo.api grAhya iti pakShe cha niyAmakAbhAvAdyaH kashchideveti | siddhAntastu | guruparigraho hi na kevalaM kiMchichChubhalAbhArthaM kintu yAvadapekShitasvayogyashubhalAbhArtham.h | tasya yadi pUrvagR^ihIto na samarthaH tarhi svApekShitAlAbhaprasaN^gena samagrAnugrahArthatvarUpakANasattvAdanyo.api guruH svIkAryaH | so.api na yAdR^ishatAdR^ishaH kintu svasmAdanapakR^iShyaH samagrAnugrahakartaiva | sa cha samashchet.h pUrvAnuj~nayA svIkAryo na veti vikalpaH samaphalayordhyAnayoriva na tu svIkArya eveti niyamaH | uttamashchetpUrvAnuj~nAM vinaiva svIkAryaH syAt.h | sarvasyoktArthasya "pUrvasmAduttamo labdhaH' iti (bR^ihattantra) smR^ityA "samagrAnugrahaM kashchit.h' iti (mahAsaMhitA) smR^ityA cha siddhatvAt.h "brahmopAsva' iti (pauShyAyaNa) shrutau pUrvaguruNaiva svasamottamasvIkArAyAtidishyamAnatvAchcha | nacha doShavachanavirodhaH | tasyAdhamasvIkAraviShayakatvena vyarthasvIkAraviShayakatvena pUrvAnuj~nAbhAvaviShayakatvena sAvakAshatvAditi | phalaM tu itaretvityatroktArthasya sarvaj~nagurUktaprakAreNa guNAdidhyAnaM kAryamityasya samarthanam.h || 28 || N.M-11
